     1                                  ; ============================================================================
     2                                  ; Simple OS Shell — minimal command interpreter
     3                                  ; ============================================================================
     4                                  ; Assembled as flat binary, loaded at 0800:0100 by boot sector
     5                                  ; Commands: DIR, ECHO, CLS, VER, and .COM file execution
     6                                  ;
     7                                  ; Disk layout (360K FAT12):
     8                                  ;   Sector 0:     Boot sector
     9                                  ;   Sectors 1-2:  FAT1
    10                                  ;   Sectors 3-4:  FAT2
    11                                  ;   Sectors 5-11: Root directory (112 entries)
    12                                  ;   Sectors 12+:  Data area (cluster 2 = sector 12)
    13                                  
    14                                  	cpu	8086
    15                                  	org	0x0100		; .COM file format
    16                                  
    17                                  SHELL_SEG	equ	0x0800	; Segment where shell is loaded
    18                                  PROG_SEG	equ	0x2000	; Segment where programs are loaded
    19                                  ROOT_DIR_SEC	equ	5	; First sector of root directory
    20                                  ROOT_DIR_SECS	equ	7	; Number of root directory sectors
    21                                  DATA_START_SEC	equ	12	; First data sector (cluster 2)
    22                                  SECS_PER_CLUST	equ	2	; Sectors per cluster
    23                                  FAT_SEC		equ	1	; First FAT sector
    24                                  TOTAL_SECS	equ	720	; Total sectors (360K)
    25                                  MAX_CMD_LEN	equ	80
    26                                  MAX_DIR_ENTRIES	equ	112	; Root dir entries (subdir = 32 per cluster)
    27                                  DIR_BUF_SIZE	equ	ROOT_DIR_SECS * 512	; 3584 bytes
    28                                  
    29                                  ; ============================================================================
    30                                  ; Entry point
    31                                  ; ============================================================================
    32                                  start:
    33                                  	; Set up our own stack
    34 00000000 FA                      	cli
    35 00000001 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
    36 00000004 8ED0                    	mov	ss, ax
    37 00000006 BCFEFF                  	mov	sp, 0xFFFE
    38 00000009 FB                      	sti
    39                                  
    40                                  	; Set DS = CS = SHELL_SEG
    41 0000000A 0E                      	push	cs
    42 0000000B 1F                      	pop	ds
    43                                  
    44                                  	; Install interrupt vectors
    45 0000000C 31C0                    	xor	ax, ax
    46 0000000E 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
    47                                  	; INT 20h — program terminate
    48 00000010 26C7068000[5338]        	mov	word [es:0x80], int20_handler
    49 00000017 26C70682000008          	mov	word [es:0x82], SHELL_SEG
    50                                  	; INT 21h — DOS services
    51 0000001E 26C7068400[261D]        	mov	word [es:0x84], int21_handler
    52 00000025 26C70686000008          	mov	word [es:0x86], SHELL_SEG
    53                                  	; INT 22h — Terminate address (goes through cleanup handler)
    54 0000002C 26C7068800[5338]        	mov	word [es:0x88], int20_handler
    55 00000033 26C7068A000008          	mov	word [es:0x8A], SHELL_SEG
    56                                  	; INT 23h — Ctrl-C handler
    57 0000003A 26C7068C00[AE38]        	mov	word [es:0x8C], int23_handler
    58 00000041 26C7068E000008          	mov	word [es:0x8E], SHELL_SEG
    59                                  	; INT 24h — Critical error handler
    60 00000048 26C7069000[BF38]        	mov	word [es:0x90], int24_handler
    61 0000004F 26C70692000008          	mov	word [es:0x92], SHELL_SEG
    62                                  
    63                                  	; Initialize memory management — create MCB chain
    64                                  	; First MCB at PROG_SEG (0x2000), one large free block
    65                                  	; Size = (0xA000 - 0x2000 - 1) paragraphs = 0x7FFF paragraphs
    66 00000056 B80020                  	mov	ax, PROG_SEG
    67 00000059 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
    68 0000005B 26C60600005A            	mov	byte [es:0x00], 'Z'	; Last block
    69 00000061 26C70601000000          	mov	word [es:0x01], 0	; Free (no owner)
    70 00000068 26C7060300FF7F          	mov	word [es:0x03], 0xA000 - PROG_SEG - 1 ; Size in paragraphs
    71 0000006F C706[143E]0020          	mov	word [mcb_first], PROG_SEG
    72                                  
    73                                  	; Restore ES
    74 00000075 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
    75 00000078 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
    76                                  
    77                                  	; Allocate environment block (16 paragraphs = 256 bytes)
    78 0000007A BB1000                  	mov	bx, 16
    79 0000007D B448                    	mov	ah, 0x48
    80 0000007F CD21                    	int	0x21
    81 00000081 7235                    	jc	.env_failed
    82 00000083 A3[2D3E]                	mov	[env_seg], ax
    83                                  	; Fill environment block
    84 00000086 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
    85 00000088 31FF                    	xor	di, di
    86                                  	; COMSPEC=A:\SHELL.COM
    87 0000008A BE[333E]                	mov	si, env_comspec
    88 0000008D E81E00                  	call	.env_copy_str
    89                                  	; PATH=A:	mov	si, env_path
    91 00000090 E81B00                  	call	.env_copy_str
    92                                  	; PROMPT=$P$G
    93 00000093 BE[513E]                	mov	si, env_prompt
    94 00000096 E81500                  	call	.env_copy_str
    95                                  	; Double null terminates the environment
    96 00000099 26C60500                	mov	byte [es:di], 0
    97 0000009D 47                      	inc	di
    98                                  	; Word count (usually 1) + program name
    99 0000009E 26C7050100              	mov	word [es:di], 1
   100 000000A3 83C702                  	add	di, 2
   101                                  	; Program name ASCIIZ
   102 000000A6 BE[5D3E]                	mov	si, env_progname
   103 000000A9 E80200                  	call	.env_copy_str
   104 000000AC EB10                    	jmp	.env_done
   105                                  .env_copy_str:
   106 000000AE AC                      	lodsb
   107 000000AF 268805                  	mov	[es:di], al
   108 000000B2 47                      	inc	di
   109 000000B3 08C0                    	or	al, al
   110 000000B5 75F7                    	jnz	.env_copy_str
   111 000000B7 C3                      	ret
   112                                  .env_failed:
   113 000000B8 C706[2D3E]0000          	mov	word [env_seg], 0
   114                                  .env_done:
   115                                  	; Restore ES/DS
   116 000000BE B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
   117 000000C1 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
   118 000000C3 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
   119                                  
   120                                  	; Run AUTOEXEC.BAT if it exists
   121 000000C5 BE[EF3B]                	mov	si, autoexec_name
   122 000000C8 E80815                  	call	run_batch
   123                                  
   124                                  ; ============================================================================
   125                                  ; Main command loop
   126                                  ; ============================================================================
   127                                  cmd_loop:
   128                                  	; Reset segments
   129 000000CB B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
   130 000000CE 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
   131 000000D0 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
   132 000000D2 FA                      	cli
   133 000000D3 8ED0                    	mov	ss, ax
   134 000000D5 BCFEFF                  	mov	sp, 0xFFFE
   135 000000D8 FB                      	sti
   136                                  
   137                                  	; Check if we're in batch mode
   138 000000D9 803E[0E3E]00            	cmp	byte [batch_active], 0
   139 000000DE 7403                    	je	.cmd_interactive
   140                                  	; Get next line from batch buffer
   141 000000E0 E97A15                  	jmp	batch_next_line
   142                                  
   143                                  .cmd_interactive:
   144                                  	; Print prompt with current path
   145 000000E3 B00D                    	mov	al, 0x0D
   146 000000E5 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
   147 000000E7 CD10                    	int	0x10
   148 000000E9 B00A                    	mov	al, 0x0A
   149 000000EB B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
   150 000000ED CD10                    	int	0x10
   151 000000EF A0[083E]                	mov	al, [cur_drive]
   152 000000F2 0441                    	add	al, 'A'		; 0='A', 1='B'
   153 000000F4 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
   154 000000F6 CD10                    	int	0x10
   155 000000F8 B03A                    	mov	al, ':'
   156 000000FA B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
   157 000000FC CD10                    	int	0x10
   158                                  	; Print backslash (always shown)
   159 000000FE B05C                    	mov	al, '\'
   160 00000100 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
   161 00000102 CD10                    	int	0x10
   162                                  	; Print current path (if any)
   163 00000104 803E[073E]00            	cmp	byte [cur_dir_pathlen], 0
   164 00000109 7406                    	je	.prompt_done
   165 0000010B BE[C63D]                	mov	si, cur_dir_path
   166 0000010E E8B137                  	call	print_string
   167                                  .prompt_done:
   168 00000111 B03E                    	mov	al, '>'
   169 00000113 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
   170 00000115 CD10                    	int	0x10
   171                                  
   172                                  	; Read command line
   173 00000117 BF[9F3C]                	mov	di, cmd_buffer
   174 0000011A E8B837                  	call	read_line
   175                                  
   176                                  	; Skip leading spaces
   177 0000011D BE[9F3C]                	mov	si, cmd_buffer
   178 00000120 E80138                  	call	skip_spaces
   179                                  
   180                                  	; Empty line?
   181 00000123 803C00                  	cmp	byte [si], 0
   182 00000126 74A3                    	je	cmd_loop
   183                                  
   184                                  cmd_dispatch:
   185                                  	; Check for built-in commands
   186 00000128 BF[6D3C]                	mov	di, cmd_dir
   187 0000012B E8FF37                  	call	str_compare_cmd
   188 0000012E 7503E90A01              	je	do_dir
   189                                  
   190 00000133 BF[713C]                	mov	di, cmd_echo
   191 00000136 E8F437                  	call	str_compare_cmd
   192 00000139 7503E94D06              	je	do_echo
   193                                  
   194 0000013E BF[763C]                	mov	di, cmd_cls
   195 00000141 E8E937                  	call	str_compare_cmd
   196 00000144 7503E95706              	je	do_cls
   197                                  
   198 00000149 BF[7A3C]                	mov	di, cmd_ver
   199 0000014C E8DE37                  	call	str_compare_cmd
   200 0000014F 7503E96606              	je	do_ver
   201                                  
   202 00000154 BF[7E3C]                	mov	di, cmd_type
   203 00000157 E8D337                  	call	str_compare_cmd
   204 0000015A 7503E96406              	je	do_type
   205                                  
   206 0000015F BF[833C]                	mov	di, cmd_del
   207 00000162 E8C837                  	call	str_compare_cmd
   208 00000165 7503E93C07              	je	do_del
   209                                  
   210 0000016A BF[873C]                	mov	di, cmd_ren
   211 0000016D E8BD37                  	call	str_compare_cmd
   212 00000170 7503E92409              	je	do_ren
   213                                  
   214 00000175 BF[8B3C]                	mov	di, cmd_copy
   215 00000178 E8B237                  	call	str_compare_cmd
   216 0000017B 7503E9DA09              	je	do_copy
   217                                  
   218 00000180 BF[903C]                	mov	di, cmd_cd
   219 00000183 E8A737                  	call	str_compare_cmd
   220 00000186 7503E9D30C              	je	do_cd
   221                                  
   222 0000018B BF[933C]                	mov	di, cmd_mkdir
   223 0000018E E89C37                  	call	str_compare_cmd
   224 00000191 7503E9DC0E              	je	do_mkdir
   225                                  
   226 00000196 BF[993C]                	mov	di, cmd_rmdir
   227 00000199 E89137                  	call	str_compare_cmd
   228 0000019C 7503E94010              	je	do_rmdir
   229                                  
   230                                  	; Check for drive switch (A: or B:)
   231 000001A1 BE[9F3C]                	mov	si, cmd_buffer
   232 000001A4 E87D37                  	call	skip_spaces
   233 000001A7 807C013A                	cmp	byte [si+1], ':'
   234 000001AB 7544                    	jne	.not_drive_switch
   235 000001AD 807C0200                	cmp	byte [si+2], 0
   236 000001B1 7408                    	je	.maybe_drive
   237 000001B3 807C0220                	cmp	byte [si+2], ' '
   238 000001B7 7402                    	je	.maybe_drive
   239 000001B9 EB36                    	jmp	.not_drive_switch
   240                                  .maybe_drive:
   241 000001BB 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
   242 000001BD 3C61                    	cmp	al, 'a'
   243 000001BF 7206                    	jb	.check_upper_drv
   244 000001C1 3C7A                    	cmp	al, 'z'
   245 000001C3 772C                    	ja	.not_drive_switch
   246 000001C5 2C20                    	sub	al, 0x20
   247                                  .check_upper_drv:
   248 000001C7 3C41                    	cmp	al, 'A'
   249 000001C9 7406                    	je	.switch_a
   250 000001CB 3C42                    	cmp	al, 'B'
   251 000001CD 7412                    	je	.switch_b
   252 000001CF EB20                    	jmp	.not_drive_switch
   253                                  .switch_a:
   254 000001D1 E82611                  	call	save_drive_state	; Save current drive's state
   255 000001D4 C606[083E]00            	mov	byte [cur_drive], 0
   256 000001D9 B000                    	mov	al, 0
   257 000001DB E86611                  	call	load_drive_state	; Load drive A's state
   258 000001DE E9EAFE                  	jmp	cmd_loop
   259                                  .switch_b:
   260 000001E1 E81611                  	call	save_drive_state	; Save current drive's state
   261 000001E4 C606[083E]01            	mov	byte [cur_drive], 1
   262 000001E9 B001                    	mov	al, 1
   263 000001EB E85611                  	call	load_drive_state	; Load drive B's state
   264 000001EE E9DAFE                  	jmp	cmd_loop
   265                                  .not_drive_switch:
   266                                  
   267                                  	; Not a built-in — check for .BAT file first, then try .COM
   268                                  	; Check if the command has .BAT extension
   269 000001F1 BE[9F3C]                	mov	si, cmd_buffer
   270 000001F4 E82D37                  	call	skip_spaces
   271 000001F7 56                      	push	si
   272                                  	; Scan for ".BAT" or ".bat"
   273 000001F8 89F7                    	mov	di, si
   274                                  .check_bat_ext:
   275 000001FA 8A05                    	mov	al, [di]
   276 000001FC 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
   277 000001FE 7439                    	je	.not_bat
   278 00000200 3C20                    	cmp	al, ' '
   279 00000202 7435                    	je	.not_bat
   280 00000204 3C2E                    	cmp	al, '.'
   281 00000206 7403                    	je	.found_dot
   282 00000208 47                      	inc	di
   283 00000209 EBEF                    	jmp	.check_bat_ext
   284                                  .found_dot:
   285                                  	; Check if extension is BAT
   286 0000020B 47                      	inc	di
   287 0000020C 8A05                    	mov	al, [di]
   288 0000020E 3C42                    	cmp	al, 'B'
   289 00000210 7406                    	je	.dot_b
   290 00000212 3C62                    	cmp	al, 'b'
   291 00000214 7402                    	je	.dot_b
   292 00000216 EB21                    	jmp	.not_bat
   293                                  .dot_b:
   294 00000218 47                      	inc	di
   295 00000219 8A05                    	mov	al, [di]
   296 0000021B 3C41                    	cmp	al, 'A'
   297 0000021D 7406                    	je	.dot_ba
   298 0000021F 3C61                    	cmp	al, 'a'
   299 00000221 7402                    	je	.dot_ba
   300 00000223 EB14                    	jmp	.not_bat
   301                                  .dot_ba:
   302 00000225 47                      	inc	di
   303 00000226 8A05                    	mov	al, [di]
   304 00000228 3C54                    	cmp	al, 'T'
   305 0000022A 7406                    	je	.is_bat
   306 0000022C 3C74                    	cmp	al, 't'
   307 0000022E 7402                    	je	.is_bat
   308 00000230 EB07                    	jmp	.not_bat
   309                                  .is_bat:
   310 00000232 5E                      	pop	si
   311 00000233 E89D13                  	call	run_batch
   312 00000236 E992FE                  	jmp	cmd_loop
   313                                  .not_bat:
   314 00000239 5E                      	pop	si
   315 0000023A E9A217                  	jmp	do_exec
   316                                  
   317                                  ; ============================================================================
   318                                  ; DIR — list root directory
   319                                  ; ============================================================================
   320                                  do_dir:
   321                                  	; Check for /W switch
   322 0000023D C606[F23E]00            	mov	byte [dir_wide], 0
   323 00000242 E8DF36                  	call	skip_spaces
   324 00000245 803C2F                  	cmp	byte [si], '/'
   325 00000248 7519                    	jne	.dir_no_switch
   326 0000024A 807C0157                	cmp	byte [si+1], 'W'
   327 0000024E 7408                    	je	.dir_set_wide
   328 00000250 807C0177                	cmp	byte [si+1], 'w'
   329 00000254 7402                    	je	.dir_set_wide
   330 00000256 EB0B                    	jmp	.dir_no_switch
   331                                  .dir_set_wide:
   332 00000258 C606[F23E]01            	mov	byte [dir_wide], 1
   333 0000025D 83C602                  	add	si, 2
   334 00000260 E8C136                  	call	skip_spaces
   335                                  .dir_no_switch:
   336 00000263 C606[073D]00            	mov	byte [wild_active], 0
   337                                  
   338                                  	; Check for optional path argument
   339 00000268 803C00                  	cmp	byte [si], 0
   340 0000026B 7503E98902              	je	.dir_cur		; No argument — use current directory
   341                                  
   342                                  	; Build header path by resolving the argument against cur_dir_path
   343                                  	; Start with a copy of cur_dir_path, then apply each component
   344 00000270 56                      	push	si
   345                                  
   346                                  	; Copy cur_dir_path to dir_hdr_path as starting point
   347 00000271 56                      	push	si
   348 00000272 BE[C63D]                	mov	si, cur_dir_path
   349 00000275 BF[F43E]                	mov	di, dir_hdr_path
   350                                  .dir_hdr_init:
   351 00000278 AC                      	lodsb
   352 00000279 AA                      	stosb
   353 0000027A 08C0                    	or	al, al
   354 0000027C 75FA                    	jnz	.dir_hdr_init
   355 0000027E 5E                      	pop	si
   356                                  
   357                                  	; Skip drive letter if present
   358 0000027F 807C013A                	cmp	byte [si+1], ':'
   359 00000283 7503                    	jne	.dir_hdr_no_drv
   360 00000285 83C602                  	add	si, 2
   361                                  .dir_hdr_no_drv:
   362                                  	; Check for absolute path
   363 00000288 803C5C                  	cmp	byte [si], '\'
   364 0000028B 7506                    	jne	.dir_hdr_components
   365 0000028D 46                      	inc	si
   366                                  	; Absolute — clear header path
   367 0000028E C606[F43E]00            	mov	byte [dir_hdr_path], 0
   368                                  
   369                                  .dir_hdr_components:
   370                                  	; Process each component
   371 00000293 803C00                  	cmp	byte [si], 0
   372 00000296 7503E9AD00              	je	.dir_hdr_final
   373 0000029B 803C20                  	cmp	byte [si], ' '
   374 0000029E 7503E9A500              	je	.dir_hdr_final
   375                                  
   376                                  	; Check for ".."
   377 000002A3 803C2E                  	cmp	byte [si], '.'
   378 000002A6 7563                    	jne	.dir_hdr_name
   379 000002A8 807C012E                	cmp	byte [si+1], '.'
   380 000002AC 7514                    	jne	.dir_hdr_check_dot
   381                                  	; Verify ".." ends with \, null, or space
   382 000002AE 807C025C                	cmp	byte [si+2], '\'
   383 000002B2 7427                    	je	.dir_hdr_dotdot
   384 000002B4 807C0200                	cmp	byte [si+2], 0
   385 000002B8 7421                    	je	.dir_hdr_dotdot
   386 000002BA 807C0220                	cmp	byte [si+2], ' '
   387 000002BE 741B                    	je	.dir_hdr_dotdot
   388 000002C0 EB49                    	jmp	.dir_hdr_name
   389                                  .dir_hdr_check_dot:
   390                                  	; Single "."
   391 000002C2 807C015C                	cmp	byte [si+1], '\'
   392 000002C6 740E                    	je	.dir_hdr_skipdot
   393 000002C8 807C0100                	cmp	byte [si+1], 0
   394 000002CC 747A                    	je	.dir_hdr_final
   395 000002CE 807C0120                	cmp	byte [si+1], ' '
   396 000002D2 7474                    	je	.dir_hdr_final
   397 000002D4 EB35                    	jmp	.dir_hdr_name
   398                                  .dir_hdr_skipdot:
   399 000002D6 83C602                  	add	si, 2			; skip ".\"
   400 000002D9 EBB8                    	jmp	.dir_hdr_components
   401                                  
   402                                  .dir_hdr_dotdot:
   403                                  	; Remove last component from dir_hdr_path
   404 000002DB 56                      	push	si
   405 000002DC BF[F43E]                	mov	di, dir_hdr_path
   406                                  	; Find end
   407 000002DF 89FE                    	mov	si, di
   408                                  .dir_hdr_dd_end:
   409 000002E1 803C00                  	cmp	byte [si], 0
   410 000002E4 7403                    	je	.dir_hdr_dd_scan
   411 000002E6 46                      	inc	si
   412 000002E7 EBF8                    	jmp	.dir_hdr_dd_end
   413                                  .dir_hdr_dd_scan:
   414 000002E9 4E                      	dec	si
   415 000002EA 39FE                    	cmp	si, di
   416 000002EC 720C                    	jb	.dir_hdr_dd_root
   417 000002EE 803C5C                  	cmp	byte [si], '\'
   418 000002F1 7402                    	je	.dir_hdr_dd_trunc
   419 000002F3 EBF4                    	jmp	.dir_hdr_dd_scan
   420                                  .dir_hdr_dd_trunc:
   421 000002F5 C60400                  	mov	byte [si], 0
   422 000002F8 EB05                    	jmp	.dir_hdr_dd_done
   423                                  .dir_hdr_dd_root:
   424 000002FA C606[F43E]00            	mov	byte [dir_hdr_path], 0
   425                                  .dir_hdr_dd_done:
   426 000002FF 5E                      	pop	si
   427 00000300 83C602                  	add	si, 2			; skip ".."
   428 00000303 803C5C                  	cmp	byte [si], '\'
   429 00000306 758B                    	jne	.dir_hdr_components
   430 00000308 46                      	inc	si			; skip trailing '\'
   431 00000309 EB88                    	jmp	.dir_hdr_components
   432                                  
   433                                  .dir_hdr_name:
   434                                  	; Append this component to dir_hdr_path
   435 0000030B BF[F43E]                	mov	di, dir_hdr_path
   436                                  .dir_hdr_find_end:
   437 0000030E 803D00                  	cmp	byte [di], 0
   438 00000311 7403                    	je	.dir_hdr_at_end
   439 00000313 47                      	inc	di
   440 00000314 EBF8                    	jmp	.dir_hdr_find_end
   441                                  .dir_hdr_at_end:
   442                                  	; Add separator if path not empty
   443 00000316 81FF[F43E]              	cmp	di, dir_hdr_path
   444 0000031A 7404                    	je	.dir_hdr_append
   445 0000031C C6055C                  	mov	byte [di], '\'
   446 0000031F 47                      	inc	di
   447                                  .dir_hdr_append:
   448 00000320 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
   449 00000322 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
   450 00000324 741F                    	je	.dir_hdr_comp_done
   451 00000326 3C20                    	cmp	al, ' '
   452 00000328 741B                    	je	.dir_hdr_comp_done
   453 0000032A 3C5C                    	cmp	al, '\'
   454 0000032C 7410                    	je	.dir_hdr_comp_sep
   455 0000032E 3C61                    	cmp	al, 'a'
   456 00000330 7206                    	jb	.dir_hdr_app_store
   457 00000332 3C7A                    	cmp	al, 'z'
   458 00000334 7702                    	ja	.dir_hdr_app_store
   459 00000336 2C20                    	sub	al, 0x20
   460                                  .dir_hdr_app_store:

   937                                  	; === Wide mode ===

   963 000006B6 B90400                  	mov	cx, 4

   971                                  	; Column tracking

  1024                                  	; Calculate free space: count free clusters in FAT

  1047 00000752 EBEC                    	jmp	.dir_count_free
  1048                                  .dir_free_done:

  1058 00000768 CD10                    	int	0x10
  1059 0000076A B00A                    	mov	al, 0x0A
  1060 0000076C B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  1061 0000076E CD10                    	int	0x10
  1062 00000770 E958F9                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  1063                                  .dir_no_free:

  1107 000007B5 CD10                    	int	0x10
  1108 000007B7 E911F9                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  1109                                  
  1110                                  ; ============================================================================

  1117                                  
  1118                                  ; ============================================================================
  1119                                  ; TYPE — display file contents
  1120                                  ; ============================================================================
  1121                                  do_type:
  1122                                  	; SI points past "TYPE" — skip spaces to get filename
  1123 000007C3 E85E31                  	call	skip_spaces
  1124 000007C6 803C00                  	cmp	byte [si], 0
  1125 000007C9 7509                    	jne	.type_has_name
  1126 000007CB BE[973A]                	mov	si, msg_need_fname
  1127 000007CE E8F130                  	call	print_string
  1128 000007D1 E9F7F8                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  1129                                  
  1130                                  .type_has_name:
  1131                                  	; Resolve path (handles DIR\FILE.TXT, \DIR\FILE, FILE.TXT)
  1132 000007D4 E86D0C                  	call	resolve_path
  1133 000007D7 722D                    	jc	.type_not_found
  1134                                  
  1135                                  	; Read resolved directory
  1136 000007D9 E8850D                  	call	read_resolved_dir
  1137 000007DC 7303E9BC00              	jc	.type_disk_err
  1138                                  
  1139                                  	; Search for file
  1140 000007E1 BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  1141 000007E4 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  1142                                  .type_search:
  1143 000007E8 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  1144 000007EA 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0x00
  1145 000007EC 7418                    	je	.type_not_found

  1147 000007F0 740E                    	je	.type_search_next
  1148 000007F2 51                      	push	cx

  1150 000007F4 BF[F03C]                	mov	di, exec_fname
  1151 000007F7 B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  1152 000007FA F3A6                    	repe	cmpsb
  1153 000007FC 5E                      	pop	si
  1154 000007FD 59                      	pop	cx
  1155 000007FE 740F                    	je	.type_found
  1156                                  .type_search_next:

  1159 00000804 75E2                    	jnz	.type_search
  1160                                  
  1161                                  .type_not_found:

  1163 00000809 E8B630                  	call	print_string
  1164 0000080C E9BCF8                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  1165                                  
  1166                                  .type_found:
  1167                                  	; Get starting cluster and file size
  1168 0000080F 8B441A                  	mov	ax, [si+26]
  1169 00000812 A3[163E]                	mov	[exec_cluster], ax
  1170 00000815 8B441C                  	mov	ax, [si+28]
  1171 00000818 A3[183E]                	mov	[exec_size], ax
  1172 0000081B 8B441E                  	mov	ax, [si+30]
  1173 0000081E A3[1A3E]                	mov	[exec_size+2], ax
  1174                                  
  1175                                  	; Load FAT
  1176 00000821 E8D90B                  	call	read_fat
  1177 00000824 7277                    	jc	.type_disk_err
  1178                                  
  1179                                  	; Read and print file cluster by cluster
  1180 00000826 A1[163E]                	mov	ax, [exec_cluster]
  1181                                  
  1182                                  .type_read_cluster:
  1183                                  	; Convert cluster to sector
  1184 00000829 50                      	push	ax
  1185 0000082A 83E802                  	sub	ax, 2
  1186 0000082D B90200                  	mov	cx, SECS_PER_CLUST
  1187 00000830 F7E1                    	mul	cx
  1188 00000832 83C00C                  	add	ax, DATA_START_SEC
  1189                                  
  1190                                  	; Convert linear sector to CHS
  1191                                  	; Save sector number, compute CHS
  1192 00000835 31D2                    	xor	dx, dx
  1193 00000837 B91200                  	mov	cx, 18			; SPT * heads
  1194 0000083A F7F1                    	div	cx			; AX = cylinder, DX = remainder
  1195 0000083C 50                      	push	ax			; Save cylinder
  1196 0000083D 89D0                    	mov	ax, dx
  1197 0000083F 31D2                    	xor	dx, dx
  1198 00000841 B90900                  	mov	cx, 9			; SPT
  1199 00000844 F7F1                    	div	cx			; AX = head, DX = sector (0-based)
  1200 00000846 88C6                    	mov	dh, al			; DH = head
  1201 00000848 88D1                    	mov	cl, dl
  1202 0000084A FEC1                    	inc	cl			; CL = sector (1-based)
  1203 0000084C 58                      	pop	ax
  1204 0000084D 88C5                    	mov	ch, al			; CH = cylinder
  1205                                  
  1206                                  	; Read cluster into dir_buffer (reuse as temp)
  1207 0000084F B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  1208 00000852 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  1209 00000854 BB0040                  	mov	bx, dir_buffer
  1210 00000857 B402                    	mov	ah, 0x02
  1211 00000859 B002                    	mov	al, SECS_PER_CLUST
  1212 0000085B 8A16[0D3E]              	mov	dl, [resolved_drive]
  1213 0000085F CD13                    	int	0x13
  1214 00000861 7239                    	jc	.type_disk_err_pop
  1215                                  
  1216                                  	; Print bytes from buffer, up to file size remaining
  1217 00000863 BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  1218 00000866 B90004                  	mov	cx, SECS_PER_CLUST * 512	; bytes in cluster
  1219                                  
  1220                                  .type_print_byte:
  1221                                  	; Check if file size remaining is zero
  1222 00000869 833E[183E]00            	cmp	word [exec_size], 0
  1223 0000086E 7507                    	jne	.type_not_eof
  1224 00000870 833E[1A3E]00            	cmp	word [exec_size+2], 0
  1225 00000875 7421                    	je	.type_eof_pop
  1226                                  .type_not_eof:
  1227 00000877 AC                      	lodsb
  1228 00000878 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  1229 0000087A BB0700                  	mov	bx, 0x0007
  1230 0000087D CD10                    	int	0x10
  1231                                  	; Decrement file size
  1232 0000087F 832E[183E]01            	sub	word [exec_size], 1
  1233 00000884 831E[1A3E]00            	sbb	word [exec_size+2], 0
  1234 00000889 49                      	dec	cx
  1235 0000088A 75DD                    	jnz	.type_print_byte
  1236                                  
  1237                                  	; Get next cluster
  1238 0000088C 58                      	pop	ax
  1239 0000088D E86B14                  	call	fat12_next_cluster
  1240 00000890 3DF80F                  	cmp	ax, 0xFF8
  1241 00000893 7294                    	jb	.type_read_cluster
  1242                                  
  1243                                  	; Done
  1244 00000895 E933F8                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  1245                                  
  1246                                  .type_eof_pop:

  1248 00000899 E92FF8                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  1249                                  
  1250                                  .type_disk_err_pop:
  1251 0000089C 58                      	pop	ax		; Discard saved cluster
  1252                                  .type_disk_err:
  1253 0000089D BE[853A]                	mov	si, msg_disk_err
  1254 000008A0 E81F30                  	call	print_string
  1255 000008A3 E925F8                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  1256                                  
  1257                                  ; ============================================================================
  1258                                  ; DEL — delete a file
  1259                                  ; ============================================================================
  1260                                  do_del:
  1261                                  	; SI points past "DEL" — skip spaces to get filename
  1262 000008A6 E87B30                  	call	skip_spaces
  1263 000008A9 803C00                  	cmp	byte [si], 0
  1264 000008AC 7509                    	jne	.del_has_name
  1265 000008AE BE[973A]                	mov	si, msg_need_fname

  1267 000008B4 E914F8                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  1268                                  
  1269                                  .del_has_name:
  1270                                  	; Check for wildcards in the argument
  1271 000008B7 56                      	push	si
  1272 000008B8 C606[073D]00            	mov	byte [wild_active], 0
  1273                                  .del_scan_wild:

  1278 000008C8 7503E92801              	je	.del_scan_done

  1289

  1291 000008E3 7503E92D01              	je	.del_no_wild
  1292                                  
  1293                                  	; --- Wildcard DEL ---
  1294                                  	; Find last separator to split dir from pattern
  1295 000008E8 56                      	push	si

  1297                                  .del_w_find_sep:

  1300 000008EF 7415                    	je	.del_w_sep_done

  1313                                  .del_w_sep_done:
  1314 00000906 5E                      	pop	si
  1315                                  
  1316                                  	; Parse wildcard pattern from the filename portion
  1317 00000907 83FB00                  	cmp	bx, 0
  1318 0000090A 7527                    	jne	.del_w_has_dir
  1319                                  	; No directory part — pattern is the whole argument, use current dir
  1320 0000090C BF[FC3C]                	mov	di, wild_pattern
  1321 0000090F E8E20F                  	call	parse_wildcard
  1322 00000912 A0[083E]                	mov	al, [cur_drive]
  1323 00000915 A2[0D3E]                	mov	[resolved_drive], al
  1324 00000918 A1[C23D]                	mov	ax, [cur_dir_cluster]
  1325 0000091B A3[093E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_cluster], ax

  1331 00000930 E98300                  	jmp	.del_wild_ready
  1332                                  
  1333                                  .del_w_has_dir:

  1337 00000936 BF[FC3C]                	mov	di, wild_pattern
  1338 00000939 E8B80F                  	call	parse_wildcard

  1347 0000094C 7303E9F100              	jc	.del_not_found

  1470                                  
  1471                                  ; Free the FAT cluster chain starting at AX

  1817                                  	; Walk source FAT chain, for each source cluster:
  1818                                  	;   1. Find a free cluster in FAT
  1819                                  	;   2. Read source cluster data

  1826

  1829

  1886 00000D34 BB0040                  	mov	bx, dir_buffer

  1960                                  ; ============================================================================
  1961                                  ; cluster_to_chs — Convert cluster number to CHS in CH/CL/DH
  1962                                  ; ============================================================================
  1963                                  ; Input:  AX = cluster number
  1964                                  ; Output: CH = cylinder, CL = sector (1-based), DH = head
  1965                                  ;
  1966                                  cluster_to_chs:
  1967 00000DD2 83E802                  	sub	ax, 2
  1968 00000DD5 B90200                  	mov	cx, SECS_PER_CLUST
  1969 00000DD8 F7E1                    	mul	cx
  1970 00000DDA 83C00C                  	add	ax, DATA_START_SEC
  1971 00000DDD 31D2                    	xor	dx, dx
  1972 00000DDF B91200                  	mov	cx, 18
  1973 00000DE2 F7F1                    	div	cx
  1974 00000DE4 50                      	push	ax			; Save cylinder
  1975 00000DE5 89D0                    	mov	ax, dx
  1976 00000DE7 31D2                    	xor	dx, dx
  1977 00000DE9 B90900                  	mov	cx, 9
  1978 00000DEC F7F1                    	div	cx
  1979 00000DEE 88C6                    	mov	dh, al			; Head
  1980 00000DF0 88D1                    	mov	cl, dl
  1981 00000DF2 FEC1                    	inc	cl			; Sector (1-based)
  1982 00000DF4 58                      	pop	ax
  1983 00000DF5 88C5                    	mov	ch, al			; Cylinder
  1984 00000DF7 C3                      	ret
  1985                                  
  1986                                  ; ============================================================================
  1987                                  ; fat12_read_cluster — Read FAT12 entry for a cluster
  1988                                  ; ============================================================================
  1989                                  ; Input:  AX = cluster number
  1990                                  ; Output: AX = FAT entry value
  1991                                  ;
  1992                                  fat12_read_cluster:
  1993 00000DF8 53                      	push	bx
  1994 00000DF9 51                      	push	cx
  1995 00000DFA 52                      	push	dx
  1996 00000DFB 89C2                    	mov	dx, ax			; Save cluster number for odd/even test
  1997 00000DFD 89C3                    	mov	bx, ax
  1998 00000DFF 89C1                    	mov	cx, ax
  1999 00000E01 D1E9                    	shr	cx, 1
  2000 00000E03 01CB                    	add	bx, cx			; BX = byte offset in FAT
  2001 00000E05 1E                      	push	ds
  2002 00000E06 B90008                  	mov	cx, SHELL_SEG
  2003 00000E09 8ED9                    	mov	ds, cx
  2004 00000E0B 8B87004E                	mov	ax, [fat_buffer + bx]
  2005 00000E0F 1F                      	pop	ds
  2006 00000E10 F7C20100                	test	dx, 1			; Test original cluster number
  2007 00000E14 7406                    	jz	.frc_even
  2008 00000E16 B104                    	mov	cl, 4
  2009 00000E18 D3E8                    	shr	ax, cl
  2010 00000E1A EB03                    	jmp	.frc_done
  2011                                  .frc_even:
  2012 00000E1C 25FF0F                  	and	ax, 0x0FFF
  2013                                  .frc_done:
  2014 00000E1F 5A                      	pop	dx
  2015 00000E20 59                      	pop	cx
  2016 00000E21 5B                      	pop	bx
  2017 00000E22 C3                      	ret
  2018                                  
  2019                                  ; ============================================================================
  2020                                  ; fat12_write_cluster — Write FAT12 entry for a cluster
  2021                                  ; ============================================================================
  2022                                  ; Input:  AX = cluster number, BX = value to write
  2023                                  ;
  2024                                  fat12_write_cluster:
  2025 00000E23 51                      	push	cx
  2026 00000E24 52                      	push	dx
  2027 00000E25 57                      	push	di
  2028 00000E26 89C7                    	mov	di, ax
  2029 00000E28 89C1                    	mov	cx, ax
  2030 00000E2A D1E9                    	shr	cx, 1
  2031 00000E2C 01CF                    	add	di, cx			; DI = byte offset in FAT
  2032 00000E2E 1E                      	push	ds
  2033 00000E2F B90008                  	mov	cx, SHELL_SEG
  2034 00000E32 8ED9                    	mov	ds, cx
  2035 00000E34 A90100                  	test	ax, 1
  2036 00000E37 7413                    	jz	.fwc_even
  2037                                  	; Odd: write to high 12 bits
  2038 00000E39 B104                    	mov	cl, 4
  2039 00000E3B D3E3                    	shl	bx, cl
  2040 00000E3D 8B85004E                	mov	ax, [fat_buffer + di]
  2041 00000E41 83E00F                  	and	ax, 0x000F
  2042 00000E44 09D8                    	or	ax, bx
  2043 00000E46 8985004E                	mov	[fat_buffer + di], ax
  2044 00000E4A EB0D                    	jmp	.fwc_done
  2045                                  .fwc_even:
  2046                                  	; Even: write to low 12 bits
  2047 00000E4C 8B85004E                	mov	ax, [fat_buffer + di]
  2048 00000E50 2500F0                  	and	ax, 0xF000
  2049 00000E53 09D8                    	or	ax, bx
  2050 00000E55 8985004E                	mov	[fat_buffer + di], ax
  2051                                  .fwc_done:
  2052 00000E59 1F                      	pop	ds
  2053 00000E5A 5F                      	pop	di
  2054 00000E5B 5A                      	pop	dx
  2055 00000E5C 59                      	pop	cx
  2056 00000E5D C3                      	ret
  2057                                  
  2058                                  ; ============================================================================
  2059                                  ; CD — change current directory
  2060                                  ; ============================================================================
  2061                                  do_cd:
  2062 00000E5E E8C32A                  	call	skip_spaces
  2063 00000E61 803C00                  	cmp	byte [si], 0
  2064 00000E64 7533                    	jne	.cd_has_arg

  2066 00000E66 A0[083E]                	mov	al, [cur_drive]

  2068 00000E6B B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E

  2087 00000E92 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  2088 00000E94 CD10                    	int	0x10
  2089 00000E96 E932F2                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2090                                  
  2091                                  .cd_has_arg:
  2092                                  	; Use resolve_path to parse the argument
  2093                                  	; But we need to handle the case where the entire arg is a directory
  2094                                  	; resolve_path returns the PARENT dir + final component name
  2095 00000E99 E8A805                  	call	resolve_path
  2096 00000E9C 7303E9BF01              	jc	.cd_not_found
  2097                                  
  2098                                  	; If exec_fname is blank, the path ended with \ or was just a drive

  2108                                  .cd_search:

  2129                                  
  2130                                  .cd_found:
  2131 00000EE1 8B441A                  	mov	ax, [si+26]

  2139                                  
  2140                                  .cd_set_dir:

  2146 00000F06 A0[0D3E]                	mov	al, [resolved_drive]
  2147 00000F09 A2[083E]                	mov	[cur_drive], al
  2148                                  .cd_same_drive:

  2154                                  
  2155                                  	; If cluster is 0, we're at root — clear path
  2156 00000F18 833E[C23D]00            	cmp	word [cur_dir_cluster], 0

  2159 00000F24 C606[C63D]00            	mov	byte [cur_dir_path], 0
  2160 00000F29 E99FF1                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2161                                  
  2162                                  .cd_build_path:
  2163                                  	; Rebuild path from the original argument
  2164                                  	; Parse each component of the original argument and apply it
  2165 00000F2C BE[9F3C]                	mov	si, cmd_buffer
  2166 00000F2F E8F229                  	call	skip_spaces
  2167                                  	; Skip "CD "
  2168 00000F32 83C602                  	add	si, 2
  2169 00000F35 E8EC29                  	call	skip_spaces
  2170                                  
  2171                                  	; Strip drive letter if present
  2172 00000F38 807C013A                	cmp	byte [si+1], ':'
  2173 00000F3C 7503                    	jne	.cd_no_drv_in_path

  2175                                  .cd_no_drv_in_path:
  2176                                  
  2177                                  	; Check for absolute path
  2178 00000F41 803C5C                  	cmp	byte [si], '\'
  2179 00000F44 750B                    	jne	.cd_process_components

  2182 00000F47 C606[073E]00            	mov	byte [cur_dir_pathlen], 0
  2183 00000F4C C606[C63D]00            	mov	byte [cur_dir_path], 0
  2184                                  
  2185                                  .cd_process_components:
  2186                                  	; Process each path component separated by '\'
  2187 00000F51 803C00                  	cmp	byte [si], 0
  2188 00000F54 7503E9F000              	je	.cd_path_final
  2189 00000F59 803C20                  	cmp	byte [si], ' '
  2190 00000F5C 7503E9E800              	je	.cd_path_final
  2191                                  
  2192                                  	; Check for ".."
  2193 00000F61 803C2E                  	cmp	byte [si], '.'
  2194 00000F64 7403E99500              	jne	.cd_comp_name
  2195 00000F69 807C012E                	cmp	byte [si+1], '.'
  2196 00000F6D 7514                    	jne	.cd_check_single_dot
  2197                                  	; Verify ".." is followed by \, null, or space
  2198 00000F6F 807C025C                	cmp	byte [si+2], '\'
  2199 00000F73 742B                    	je	.cd_do_dotdot
  2200 00000F75 807C0200                	cmp	byte [si+2], 0
  2201 00000F79 7425                    	je	.cd_do_dotdot
  2202 00000F7B 807C0220                	cmp	byte [si+2], ' '
  2203 00000F7F 741F                    	je	.cd_do_dotdot
  2204 00000F81 EB7B                    	jmp	.cd_comp_name		; Not ".." — regular name
  2205                                  
  2206                                  .cd_check_single_dot:
  2207                                  	; "." — skip it
  2208 00000F83 807C015C                	cmp	byte [si+1], '\'
  2209 00000F87 740E                    	je	.cd_skip_dot
  2210 00000F89 807C0100                	cmp	byte [si+1], 0
  2211 00000F8D 740D                    	je	.cd_skip_dot_end
  2212 00000F8F 807C0120                	cmp	byte [si+1], ' '
  2213 00000F93 7407                    	je	.cd_skip_dot_end
  2214 00000F95 EB67                    	jmp	.cd_comp_name		; Not "." alone
  2215                                  .cd_skip_dot:
  2216 00000F97 83C602                  	add	si, 2			; skip ".\\"
  2217 00000F9A EBB5                    	jmp	.cd_process_components
  2218                                  .cd_skip_dot_end:
  2219 00000F9C 46                      	inc	si			; skip "."
  2220 00000F9D E9A900                  	jmp	.cd_path_final
  2221                                  
  2222                                  .cd_do_dotdot:
  2223                                  	; Remove last component from cur_dir_path
  2224 00000FA0 803E[073E]00            	cmp	byte [cur_dir_pathlen], 0
  2225 00000FA5 7428                    	je	.cd_dotdot_at_root
  2226 00000FA7 BF[C63D]                	mov	di, cur_dir_path
  2227 00000FAA 8A0E[073E]              	mov	cl, [cur_dir_pathlen]
  2228 00000FAE 30ED                    	xor	ch, ch
  2229 00000FB0 01CF                    	add	di, cx
  2230 00000FB2 4F                      	dec	di
  2231                                  .cd_trim:
  2232 00000FB3 81FF[C63D]              	cmp	di, cur_dir_path
  2233 00000FB7 7216                    	jb	.cd_dotdot_at_root
  2234 00000FB9 7408                    	je	.cd_dotdot_at_root2
  2235 00000FBB 803D5C                  	cmp	byte [di], '\'
  2236 00000FBE 741B                    	je	.cd_trim_done
  2237 00000FC0 4F                      	dec	di
  2238 00000FC1 EBF0                    	jmp	.cd_trim
  2239                                  .cd_dotdot_at_root2:
  2240                                  	; Only one component left — clear it
  2241 00000FC3 C606[C63D]00            	mov	byte [cur_dir_path], 0
  2242 00000FC8 C606[073E]00            	mov	byte [cur_dir_pathlen], 0
  2243 00000FCD EB0F                    	jmp	.cd_dotdot_advance
  2244                                  .cd_dotdot_at_root:
  2245 00000FCF C606[073E]00            	mov	byte [cur_dir_pathlen], 0
  2246 00000FD4 C606[C63D]00            	mov	byte [cur_dir_path], 0
  2247 00000FD9 EB03                    	jmp	.cd_dotdot_advance
  2248                                  .cd_trim_done:
  2249 00000FDB C60500                  	mov	byte [di], 0
  2250                                  .cd_dotdot_advance:
  2251                                  	; Skip ".." and optional trailing '\'
  2252 00000FDE 83C602                  	add	si, 2
  2253 00000FE1 803C5C                  	cmp	byte [si], '\'
  2254 00000FE4 7501                    	jne	.cd_dotdot_recount
  2255 00000FE6 46                      	inc	si
  2256                                  .cd_dotdot_recount:
  2257                                  	; Recount path length
  2258 00000FE7 56                      	push	si
  2259 00000FE8 BE[C63D]                	mov	si, cur_dir_path
  2260 00000FEB 31C9                    	xor	cx, cx
  2261                                  .cd_dotdot_cnt:
  2262 00000FED 803C00                  	cmp	byte [si], 0
  2263 00000FF0 7404                    	je	.cd_dotdot_cnt_done
  2264 00000FF2 41                      	inc	cx
  2265 00000FF3 46                      	inc	si
  2266 00000FF4 EBF7                    	jmp	.cd_dotdot_cnt
  2267                                  .cd_dotdot_cnt_done:
  2268 00000FF6 880E[073E]              	mov	[cur_dir_pathlen], cl
  2269 00000FFA 5E                      	pop	si
  2270 00000FFB E953FF                  	jmp	.cd_process_components
  2271                                  
  2272                                  .cd_comp_name:
  2273                                  	; Regular directory name — append to cur_dir_path
  2274 00000FFE BF[C63D]                	mov	di, cur_dir_path
  2275 00001001 8A0E[073E]              	mov	cl, [cur_dir_pathlen]
  2276 00001005 30ED                    	xor	ch, ch
  2277 00001007 01CF                    	add	di, cx
  2278                                  	; Add separator if path is not empty
  2279 00001009 83F900                  	cmp	cx, 0
  2280 0000100C 7405                    	je	.cd_comp_copy
  2281 0000100E C6055C                  	mov	byte [di], '\'
  2282 00001011 47                      	inc	di
  2283 00001012 41                      	inc	cx
  2284                                  .cd_comp_copy:
  2285                                  	; Bounds check: cur_dir_path is 65 bytes
  2286 00001013 83F93F                  	cmp	cx, 63
  2287 00001016 7331                    	jae	.cd_path_final		; Overflow — stop appending
  2288 00001018 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  2289 0000101A 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  2290 0000101C 7424                    	je	.cd_comp_end
  2291 0000101E 3C20                    	cmp	al, ' '
  2292 00001020 7420                    	je	.cd_comp_end
  2293 00001022 3C5C                    	cmp	al, '\'
  2294 00001024 7411                    	je	.cd_comp_sep
  2295                                  	; Uppercase
  2296 00001026 3C61                    	cmp	al, 'a'
  2297 00001028 7206                    	jb	.cd_comp_store
  2298 0000102A 3C7A                    	cmp	al, 'z'
  2299 0000102C 7702                    	ja	.cd_comp_store
  2300 0000102E 2C20                    	sub	al, 0x20
  2301                                  .cd_comp_store:
  2302 00001030 8805                    	mov	[di], al
  2303 00001032 46                      	inc	si
  2304 00001033 47                      	inc	di
  2305 00001034 41                      	inc	cx
  2306 00001035 EBDC                    	jmp	.cd_comp_copy
  2307                                  .cd_comp_sep:
  2308 00001037 46                      	inc	si			; skip '\'
  2309 00001038 C60500                  	mov	byte [di], 0		; terminate current path
  2310 0000103B 880E[073E]              	mov	[cur_dir_pathlen], cl
  2311 0000103F E90FFF                  	jmp	.cd_process_components
  2312                                  .cd_comp_end:
  2313 00001042 C60500                  	mov	byte [di], 0
  2314 00001045 880E[073E]              	mov	[cur_dir_pathlen], cl
  2315                                  
  2316                                  .cd_path_final:
  2317                                  	; Recount for safety
  2318 00001049 BE[C63D]                	mov	si, cur_dir_path
  2319 0000104C 31C9                    	xor	cx, cx
  2320                                  .cd_recount_loop:
  2321 0000104E AC                      	lodsb
  2322 0000104F 08C0                    	or	al, al
  2323 00001051 7403                    	jz	.cd_recount_done
  2324 00001053 41                      	inc	cx
  2325 00001054 EBF8                    	jmp	.cd_recount_loop
  2326                                  .cd_recount_done:
  2327 00001056 880E[073E]              	mov	[cur_dir_pathlen], cl
  2328 0000105A E89D02                  	call	save_drive_state	; Persist to per-drive slot
  2329 0000105D E96BF0                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2330                                  
  2331                                  .cd_not_found:
  2332 00001060 BE[713A]                	mov	si, msg_invalid_dir
  2333 00001063 E85C28                  	call	print_string
  2334 00001066 E962F0                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2335                                  
  2336                                  .cd_disk_err:
  2337 00001069 BE[853A]                	mov	si, msg_disk_err
  2338 0000106C E85328                  	call	print_string
  2339 0000106F E959F0                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2340                                  
  2341                                  ; ============================================================================
  2342                                  ; MKDIR — create a new subdirectory
  2343                                  ; ============================================================================
  2344                                  do_mkdir:
  2345 00001072 E8AF28                  	call	skip_spaces
  2346 00001075 803C00                  	cmp	byte [si], 0
  2347 00001078 7509                    	jne	.mkdir_has_name
  2348 0000107A BE[973A]                	mov	si, msg_need_fname
  2349 0000107D E84228                  	call	print_string
  2350 00001080 E948F0                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2351                                  .mkdir_has_name:
  2352 00001083 E8BE03                  	call	resolve_path
  2353 00001086 7303E94D01              	jc	.mkdir_disk_err
  2354                                  
  2355                                  	; Read resolved directory
  2356 0000108B E8D304                  	call	read_resolved_dir
  2357 0000108E 7303E94501              	jc	.mkdir_disk_err
  2358                                  
  2359                                  	; Check name doesn't exist
  2360 00001093 BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  2361 00001096 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  2362                                  .mkdir_check_dup:
  2363 0000109A 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  2364 0000109C 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  2365 0000109E 741B                    	je	.mkdir_dup_ok
  2366 000010A0 3CE5                    	cmp	al, 0xE5
  2367 000010A2 7411                    	je	.mkdir_dup_next
  2368 000010A4 51                      	push	cx
  2369 000010A5 56                      	push	si
  2370 000010A6 BF[F03C]                	mov	di, exec_fname
  2371 000010A9 B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  2372 000010AC F3A6                    	repe	cmpsb
  2373 000010AE 5E                      	pop	si
  2374 000010AF 59                      	pop	cx
  2375 000010B0 7503E91101              	je	.mkdir_exists
  2376                                  .mkdir_dup_next:
  2377 000010B5 83C620                  	add	si, 32
  2378 000010B8 49                      	dec	cx
  2379 000010B9 75DF                    	jnz	.mkdir_check_dup
  2380                                  .mkdir_dup_ok:
  2381                                  
  2382                                  	; Find free directory entry
  2383 000010BB BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  2384 000010BE 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  2385                                  .mkdir_find_free:
  2386 000010C2 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  2387 000010C4 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  2388 000010C6 7413                    	je	.mkdir_free_found
  2389 000010C8 3CE5                    	cmp	al, 0xE5
  2390 000010CA 740F                    	je	.mkdir_free_found
  2391 000010CC 83C620                  	add	si, 32
  2392 000010CF 49                      	dec	cx
  2393 000010D0 75F0                    	jnz	.mkdir_find_free
  2394 000010D2 BE[833B]                	mov	si, msg_dir_full
  2395 000010D5 E8EA27                  	call	print_string
  2396 000010D8 E9F0EF                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2397                                  .mkdir_free_found:
  2398 000010DB 89F0                    	mov	ax, si
  2399 000010DD 2D0040                  	sub	ax, dir_buffer
  2400 000010E0 A3[1E3D]                	mov	[copy_dest_dir], ax	; Save offset, not raw pointer
  2401                                  
  2402                                  	; Load FAT
  2403 000010E3 E81703                  	call	read_fat
  2404 000010E6 7303E9ED00              	jc	.mkdir_disk_err
  2405                                  
  2406                                  	; Find a free cluster
  2407 000010EB B80200                  	mov	ax, 2
  2408                                  .mkdir_find_cl:
  2409 000010EE 3DD002                  	cmp	ax, 720
  2410 000010F1 7203E9D900              	jae	.mkdir_full
  2411 000010F6 50                      	push	ax
  2412 000010F7 E8FEFC                  	call	fat12_read_cluster
  2413 000010FA 83F800                  	cmp	ax, 0
  2414 000010FD 58                      	pop	ax
  2415 000010FE 7403                    	je	.mkdir_got_cl
  2416 00001100 40                      	inc	ax
  2417 00001101 EBEB                    	jmp	.mkdir_find_cl
  2418                                  .mkdir_got_cl:
  2419 00001103 A3[183D]                	mov	[copy_dest_cl], ax	; Save allocated cluster
  2420                                  
  2421                                  	; Mark cluster as EOF
  2422 00001106 BBFF0F                  	mov	bx, 0xFFF
  2423 00001109 E817FD                  	call	fat12_write_cluster
  2424                                  
  2425                                  	; Write FAT back
  2426 0000110C E80703                  	call	write_fat
  2427 0000110F 7303E9C400              	jc	.mkdir_disk_err
  2428                                  
  2429                                  	; Get current timestamp for the new directory entries
  2430 00001114 E84526                  	call	get_fat_timestamp
  2431                                  
  2432                                  	; Initialize the new directory cluster with "." and ".." entries
  2433                                  	; Clear dir_buffer first (reuse as temp for the new directory data)
  2434 00001117 BF0040                  	mov	di, dir_buffer

  2436 0000111D 30C0                    	xor	al, al
  2437 0000111F F3AA                    	rep	stosb
  2438                                  
  2439                                  	; "." entry — points to itself
  2440 00001121 BF0040                  	mov	di, dir_buffer
  2441 00001124 C6052E                  	mov	byte [di+0], '.'
  2442 00001127 B90A00                  	mov	cx, 10
  2443 0000112A B020                    	mov	al, ' '
  2444 0000112C 57                      	push	di
  2445 0000112D 83C701                  	add	di, 1
  2446 00001130 F3AA                    	rep	stosb
  2447 00001132 5F                      	pop	di
  2448 00001133 C6450B10                	mov	byte [di+11], 0x10	; Directory attribute
  2449 00001137 A1[4F38]                	mov	ax, [cur_fat_time]
  2450 0000113A 894516                  	mov	[di+22], ax
  2451 0000113D A1[5138]                	mov	ax, [cur_fat_date]
  2452 00001140 894518                  	mov	[di+24], ax
  2453 00001143 A1[183D]                	mov	ax, [copy_dest_cl]
  2454 00001146 89451A                  	mov	[di+26], ax		; Starting cluster = self
  2455                                  
  2456                                  	; ".." entry — points to parent
  2457 00001149 83C720                  	add	di, 32
  2458 0000114C C6052E                  	mov	byte [di+0], '.'
  2459 0000114F C645012E                	mov	byte [di+1], '.'
  2460 00001153 B90900                  	mov	cx, 9
  2461 00001156 B020                    	mov	al, ' '
  2462 00001158 57                      	push	di
  2463 00001159 83C702                  	add	di, 2
  2464 0000115C F3AA                    	rep	stosb
  2465 0000115E 5F                      	pop	di
  2466 0000115F C6450B10                	mov	byte [di+11], 0x10	; Directory attribute
  2467 00001163 A1[4F38]                	mov	ax, [cur_fat_time]
  2468 00001166 894516                  	mov	[di+22], ax
  2469 00001169 A1[5138]                	mov	ax, [cur_fat_date]
  2470 0000116C 894518                  	mov	[di+24], ax
  2471 0000116F A1[093E]                	mov	ax, [resolved_dir_cluster]
  2472 00001172 89451A                  	mov	[di+26], ax		; Starting cluster = parent
  2473                                  
  2474                                  	; Write the new directory data to disk
  2475 00001175 A1[183D]                	mov	ax, [copy_dest_cl]
  2476 00001178 E857FC                  	call	cluster_to_chs
  2477 0000117B B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  2478 0000117E 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  2479 00001180 BB0040                  	mov	bx, dir_buffer
  2480 00001183 B403                    	mov	ah, 0x03
  2481 00001185 B002                    	mov	al, SECS_PER_CLUST
  2482 00001187 8A16[0D3E]              	mov	dl, [resolved_drive]
  2483 0000118B CD13                    	int	0x13
  2484 0000118D 7249                    	jc	.mkdir_disk_err
  2485                                  
  2486                                  	; Now re-read the resolved directory to add the entry
  2487 0000118F E8CF03                  	call	read_resolved_dir
  2488 00001192 7244                    	jc	.mkdir_disk_err
  2489                                  
  2490                                  	; Write the directory entry (reconstruct pointer from offset)
  2491 00001194 BF0040                  	mov	di, dir_buffer
  2492 00001197 033E[1E3D]              	add	di, [copy_dest_dir]
  2493 0000119B BE[F03C]                	mov	si, exec_fname
  2494 0000119E B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  2495 000011A1 F3A4                    	rep	movsb
  2496 000011A3 C60510                  	mov	byte [di], 0x10		; Directory attribute
  2497 000011A6 47                      	inc	di			; DI now at offset 12
  2498 000011A7 B90A00                  	mov	cx, 10
  2499 000011AA 30C0                    	xor	al, al
  2500 000011AC F3AA                    	rep	stosb			; Zero offsets 12-21
  2501 000011AE A1[4F38]                	mov	ax, [cur_fat_time]
  2502 000011B1 AB                      	stosw				; Offset 22: write time
  2503 000011B2 A1[5138]                	mov	ax, [cur_fat_date]
  2504 000011B5 AB                      	stosw				; Offset 24: write date
  2505 000011B6 A1[183D]                	mov	ax, [copy_dest_cl]
  2506 000011B9 AB                      	stosw				; Offset 26: starting cluster
  2507 000011BA 31C0                    	xor	ax, ax
  2508 000011BC AB                      	stosw				; Offset 28: size low = 0
  2509 000011BD AB                      	stosw				; Offset 30: size high = 0
  2510                                  
  2511                                  	; Write resolved directory back
  2512 000011BE E8D903                  	call	write_resolved_dir
  2513 000011C1 7215                    	jc	.mkdir_disk_err
  2514                                  
  2515 000011C3 E905EF                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2516                                  
  2517                                  .mkdir_exists:
  2518 000011C6 BE[173B]                	mov	si, msg_mkdir_exists
  2519 000011C9 E8F626                  	call	print_string
  2520 000011CC E9FCEE                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2521                                  
  2522                                  .mkdir_full:

  2526                                  
  2527                                  .mkdir_disk_err:
