  2530 000011DE E9EAEE                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2531                                  
  2532                                  ; ============================================================================
  2533                                  ; RMDIR — remove an empty directory
  2534                                  ; ============================================================================
  2535                                  do_rmdir:
  2536 000011E1 E84027                  	call	skip_spaces
  2537 000011E4 803C00                  	cmp	byte [si], 0
  2538 000011E7 7509                    	jne	.rmdir_has_name
  2539 000011E9 BE[973A]                	mov	si, msg_need_fname
  2540 000011EC E8D326                  	call	print_string
  2541 000011EF E9D9EE                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2542                                  .rmdir_has_name:
  2543 000011F2 E84F02                  	call	resolve_path
  2544 000011F5 7233                    	jc	.rmdir_not_found
  2545                                  
  2546                                  	; Read the parent directory (where the dir entry lives)
  2547 000011F7 E86703                  	call	read_resolved_dir
  2548 000011FA 7303E9F200              	jc	.rmdir_disk_err
  2549                                  
  2550                                  	; Find the directory entry
  2551 000011FF BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  2552 00001202 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  2553                                  .rmdir_search:
  2554 00001206 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  2555 00001208 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  2556 0000120A 741E                    	je	.rmdir_not_found
  2557 0000120C 3CE5                    	cmp	al, 0xE5
  2558 0000120E 7414                    	je	.rmdir_search_next
  2559 00001210 F6440B10                	test	byte [si+11], 0x10	; Directory?
  2560 00001214 740E                    	jz	.rmdir_search_next
  2561 00001216 51                      	push	cx
  2562 00001217 56                      	push	si
  2563 00001218 BF[F03C]                	mov	di, exec_fname
  2564 0000121B B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  2565 0000121E F3A6                    	repe	cmpsb
  2566 00001220 5E                      	pop	si
  2567 00001221 59                      	pop	cx
  2568 00001222 740F                    	je	.rmdir_found
  2569                                  .rmdir_search_next:
  2570 00001224 83C620                  	add	si, 32
  2571 00001227 49                      	dec	cx
  2572 00001228 75DC                    	jnz	.rmdir_search
  2573                                  
  2574                                  .rmdir_not_found:
  2575 0000122A BE[453A]                	mov	si, msg_not_found
  2576 0000122D E89226                  	call	print_string
  2577 00001230 E998EE                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2578                                  
  2579                                  .rmdir_found:
  2580                                  	; Save the entry offset and cluster
  2581 00001233 89F0                    	mov	ax, si
  2582 00001235 2D0040                  	sub	ax, dir_buffer
  2583 00001238 A3[1E3D]                	mov	[copy_dest_dir], ax	; Save offset, not raw pointer
  2584 0000123B 8B441A                  	mov	ax, [si+26]
  2585 0000123E A3[183D]                	mov	[copy_dest_cl], ax	; Cluster of the directory to remove
  2586                                  
  2587                                  	; Don't allow removing "." or ".."
  2588 00001241 803C2E                  	cmp	byte [si], '.'
  2589 00001244 7518                    	jne	.rmdir_not_dotentry
  2590 00001246 807C0120                	cmp	byte [si+1], ' '
  2591 0000124A 7503E99700              	je	.rmdir_invalid
  2592 0000124F 807C012E                	cmp	byte [si+1], '.'
  2593 00001253 7509                    	jne	.rmdir_not_dotentry
  2594 00001255 807C0220                	cmp	byte [si+2], ' '
  2595 00001259 7503E98800              	je	.rmdir_invalid
  2596                                  .rmdir_not_dotentry:
  2597                                  
  2598                                  	; Check the directory is empty — read its cluster
  2599 0000125E FF36[093E]              	push	word [resolved_dir_cluster]
  2600 00001262 FF36[0B3E]              	push	word [resolved_dir_entries]
  2601 00001266 A1[183D]                	mov	ax, [copy_dest_cl]
  2602 00001269 A3[093E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_cluster], ax
  2603 0000126C C706[0B3E]2000          	mov	word [resolved_dir_entries], SECS_PER_CLUST * 512 / 32
  2604 00001272 E8EC02                  	call	read_resolved_dir
  2605 00001275 7278                    	jc	.rmdir_disk_err_pop
  2606                                  
  2607                                  	; Check entries — only "." and ".." should exist
  2608 00001277 BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  2609 0000127A B92000                  	mov	cx, SECS_PER_CLUST * 512 / 32
  2610                                  .rmdir_check_empty:
  2611 0000127D 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  2612 0000127F 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0			; End of directory
  2613 00001281 742B                    	je	.rmdir_is_empty
  2614 00001283 3CE5                    	cmp	al, 0xE5		; Deleted
  2615 00001285 7421                    	je	.rmdir_check_next
  2616                                  	; Check for exact "." or ".." entries
  2617 00001287 3C2E                    	cmp	al, '.'
  2618 00001289 7512                    	jne	.rmdir_not_dot
  2619 0000128B 807C0120                	cmp	byte [si+1], ' '	; "." followed by spaces
  2620 0000128F 7417                    	je	.rmdir_check_next
  2621 00001291 807C012E                	cmp	byte [si+1], '.'	; ".." ?
  2622 00001295 7506                    	jne	.rmdir_not_dot
  2623 00001297 807C0220                	cmp	byte [si+2], ' '	; ".." followed by spaces
  2624 0000129B 740B                    	je	.rmdir_check_next
  2625                                  .rmdir_not_dot:
  2626                                  	; Found a real entry — not empty
  2627 0000129D 58                      	pop	ax
  2628 0000129E 58                      	pop	ax
  2629 0000129F BE[BC3B]                	mov	si, msg_rmdir_not_empty
  2630 000012A2 E81D26                  	call	print_string
  2631 000012A5 E923EE                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2632                                  .rmdir_check_next:
  2633 000012A8 83C620                  	add	si, 32
  2634 000012AB 49                      	dec	cx
  2635 000012AC 75CF                    	jnz	.rmdir_check_empty
  2636                                  
  2637                                  .rmdir_is_empty:
  2638                                  	; Restore parent directory context
  2639 000012AE 58                      	pop	ax
  2640 000012AF A3[0B3E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_entries], ax
  2641 000012B2 58                      	pop	ax
  2642 000012B3 A3[093E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_cluster], ax
  2643                                  
  2644                                  	; Free the directory's cluster in FAT
  2645 000012B6 E84401                  	call	read_fat
  2646 000012B9 7236                    	jc	.rmdir_disk_err
  2647 000012BB A1[183D]                	mov	ax, [copy_dest_cl]
  2648 000012BE BB0000                  	mov	bx, 0x000		; Free cluster
  2649 000012C1 E85FFB                  	call	fat12_write_cluster
  2650 000012C4 E84F01                  	call	write_fat
  2651 000012C7 7228                    	jc	.rmdir_disk_err
  2652                                  
  2653                                  	; Re-read parent directory and mark entry as deleted
  2654 000012C9 E89502                  	call	read_resolved_dir
  2655 000012CC 7223                    	jc	.rmdir_disk_err
  2656 000012CE BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  2657 000012D1 0336[1E3D]              	add	si, [copy_dest_dir]	; Reconstruct pointer from offset
  2658 000012D5 C604E5                  	mov	byte [si], 0xE5		; Mark as deleted
  2659 000012D8 E8BF02                  	call	write_resolved_dir
  2660 000012DB 7214                    	jc	.rmdir_disk_err
  2661                                  
  2662 000012DD BE[A83B]                	mov	si, msg_rmdir_ok
  2663 000012E0 E8DF25                  	call	print_string
  2664 000012E3 E9E5ED                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2665                                  
  2666                                  .rmdir_invalid:
  2667 000012E6 BE[453A]                	mov	si, msg_not_found
  2668 000012E9 E8D625                  	call	print_string
  2669 000012EC E9DCED                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2670                                  
  2671                                  .rmdir_disk_err_pop:
  2672 000012EF 58                      	pop	ax
  2673 000012F0 58                      	pop	ax
  2674                                  .rmdir_disk_err:
  2675 000012F1 BE[853A]                	mov	si, msg_disk_err
  2676 000012F4 E8CB25                  	call	print_string
  2677 000012F7 E9D1ED                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  2678                                  
  2679                                  ; ============================================================================
  2680                                  ; save_drive_state — Save cur_dir_* to the current drive's slot
  2681                                  ; ============================================================================
  2682                                  save_drive_state:
  2683 000012FA 56                      	push	si
  2684 000012FB 57                      	push	di
  2685 000012FC 51                      	push	cx
  2686 000012FD 803E[083E]00            	cmp	byte [cur_drive], 0
  2687 00001302 751F                    	jne	.sds_b
  2688                                  	; Save to drive A
  2689 00001304 A1[C23D]                	mov	ax, [cur_dir_cluster]
  2690 00001307 A3[363D]                	mov	[drv_a_cluster], ax
  2691 0000130A A1[C43D]                	mov	ax, [cur_dir_entries]
  2692 0000130D A3[383D]                	mov	[drv_a_entries], ax
  2693 00001310 A0[073E]                	mov	al, [cur_dir_pathlen]
  2694 00001313 A2[7B3D]                	mov	[drv_a_pathlen], al
  2695 00001316 BE[C63D]                	mov	si, cur_dir_path
  2696 00001319 BF[3A3D]                	mov	di, drv_a_path
  2697 0000131C B94100                  	mov	cx, 65
  2698 0000131F F3A4                    	rep	movsb
  2699 00001321 EB1D                    	jmp	.sds_done
  2700                                  .sds_b:
  2701 00001323 A1[C23D]                	mov	ax, [cur_dir_cluster]
  2702 00001326 A3[7C3D]                	mov	[drv_b_cluster], ax
  2703 00001329 A1[C43D]                	mov	ax, [cur_dir_entries]
  2704 0000132C A3[7E3D]                	mov	[drv_b_entries], ax
  2705 0000132F A0[073E]                	mov	al, [cur_dir_pathlen]
  2706 00001332 A2[C13D]                	mov	[drv_b_pathlen], al
  2707 00001335 BE[C63D]                	mov	si, cur_dir_path
  2708 00001338 BF[803D]                	mov	di, drv_b_path
  2709 0000133B B94100                  	mov	cx, 65
  2710 0000133E F3A4                    	rep	movsb
  2711                                  .sds_done:
  2712 00001340 59                      	pop	cx
  2713 00001341 5F                      	pop	di
  2714 00001342 5E                      	pop	si
  2715 00001343 C3                      	ret
  2716                                  
  2717                                  ; ============================================================================
  2718                                  ; load_drive_state — Load cur_dir_* from drive A's slot (al=0) or B's (al=1)
  2719                                  ; ============================================================================
  2720                                  ; Input: AL = drive number (0=A, 1=B)
  2721                                  ;
  2722                                  load_drive_state:
  2723 00001344 56                      	push	si
  2724 00001345 57                      	push	di
  2725 00001346 51                      	push	cx
  2726 00001347 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  2727 00001349 751F                    	jne	.lds_b
  2728 0000134B A1[363D]                	mov	ax, [drv_a_cluster]
  2729 0000134E A3[C23D]                	mov	[cur_dir_cluster], ax
  2730 00001351 A1[383D]                	mov	ax, [drv_a_entries]
  2731 00001354 A3[C43D]                	mov	[cur_dir_entries], ax
  2732 00001357 A0[7B3D]                	mov	al, [drv_a_pathlen]
  2733 0000135A A2[073E]                	mov	[cur_dir_pathlen], al
  2734 0000135D BE[3A3D]                	mov	si, drv_a_path
  2735 00001360 BF[C63D]                	mov	di, cur_dir_path
  2736 00001363 B94100                  	mov	cx, 65
  2737 00001366 F3A4                    	rep	movsb
  2738 00001368 EB1D                    	jmp	.lds_done
  2739                                  .lds_b:
  2740 0000136A A1[7C3D]                	mov	ax, [drv_b_cluster]
  2741 0000136D A3[C23D]                	mov	[cur_dir_cluster], ax
  2742 00001370 A1[7E3D]                	mov	ax, [drv_b_entries]
  2743 00001373 A3[C43D]                	mov	[cur_dir_entries], ax
  2744 00001376 A0[C13D]                	mov	al, [drv_b_pathlen]
  2745 00001379 A2[073E]                	mov	[cur_dir_pathlen], al
  2746 0000137C BE[803D]                	mov	si, drv_b_path
  2747 0000137F BF[C63D]                	mov	di, cur_dir_path
  2748 00001382 B94100                  	mov	cx, 65
  2749 00001385 F3A4                    	rep	movsb
  2750                                  .lds_done:
  2751 00001387 59                      	pop	cx
  2752 00001388 5F                      	pop	di
  2753 00001389 5E                      	pop	si
  2754 0000138A C3                      	ret
  2755                                  
  2756                                  ; ============================================================================
  2757                                  ; read_cur_dir — Read current directory into dir_buffer
  2758                                  ; ============================================================================
  2759                                  ; Output: carry set on error
  2760                                  ;
  2761                                  read_cur_dir:
  2762 0000138B B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  2763 0000138E 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  2764 00001390 BB0040                  	mov	bx, dir_buffer
  2765 00001393 833E[C23D]00            	cmp	word [cur_dir_cluster], 0
  2766 00001398 7511                    	jne	.rcd_subdir
  2767 0000139A B402                    	mov	ah, 0x02
  2768 0000139C B007                    	mov	al, ROOT_DIR_SECS
  2769 0000139E B500                    	mov	ch, 0
  2770 000013A0 B106                    	mov	cl, ROOT_DIR_SEC + 1
  2771 000013A2 B600                    	mov	dh, 0
  2772 000013A4 8A16[083E]              	mov	dl, [cur_drive]
  2773 000013A8 CD13                    	int	0x13
  2774 000013AA C3                      	ret
  2775                                  .rcd_subdir:
  2776 000013AB A1[C23D]                	mov	ax, [cur_dir_cluster]
  2777 000013AE E821FA                  	call	cluster_to_chs
  2778 000013B1 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  2779 000013B4 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  2780 000013B6 BB0040                  	mov	bx, dir_buffer
  2781 000013B9 B402                    	mov	ah, 0x02
  2782 000013BB B002                    	mov	al, SECS_PER_CLUST
  2783 000013BD 8A16[083E]              	mov	dl, [cur_drive]
  2784 000013C1 CD13                    	int	0x13
  2785 000013C3 C3                      	ret
  2786                                  
  2787                                  ; ============================================================================
  2788                                  ; write_cur_dir — Write dir_buffer back to current directory
  2789                                  ; ============================================================================
  2790                                  ; Output: carry set on error
  2791                                  ;
  2792                                  write_cur_dir:
  2793 000013C4 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  2794 000013C7 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  2795 000013C9 BB0040                  	mov	bx, dir_buffer
  2796 000013CC 833E[C23D]00            	cmp	word [cur_dir_cluster], 0
  2797 000013D1 7511                    	jne	.wcd_subdir
  2798 000013D3 B403                    	mov	ah, 0x03
  2799 000013D5 B007                    	mov	al, ROOT_DIR_SECS
  2800 000013D7 B500                    	mov	ch, 0
  2801 000013D9 B106                    	mov	cl, ROOT_DIR_SEC + 1
  2802 000013DB B600                    	mov	dh, 0
  2803 000013DD 8A16[083E]              	mov	dl, [cur_drive]
  2804 000013E1 CD13                    	int	0x13
  2805 000013E3 C3                      	ret
  2806                                  .wcd_subdir:
  2807 000013E4 A1[C23D]                	mov	ax, [cur_dir_cluster]
  2808 000013E7 E8E8F9                  	call	cluster_to_chs
  2809 000013EA B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  2810 000013ED 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  2811 000013EF BB0040                  	mov	bx, dir_buffer
  2812 000013F2 B403                    	mov	ah, 0x03
  2813 000013F4 B002                    	mov	al, SECS_PER_CLUST
  2814 000013F6 8A16[083E]              	mov	dl, [cur_drive]
  2815 000013FA CD13                    	int	0x13
  2816 000013FC C3                      	ret
  2817                                  
  2818                                  ; ============================================================================
  2819                                  ; read_fat — Read FAT into fat_buffer
  2820                                  ; ============================================================================
  2821                                  read_fat:
  2822 000013FD B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  2823 00001400 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  2824 00001402 BB004E                  	mov	bx, fat_buffer
  2825 00001405 B402                    	mov	ah, 0x02
  2826 00001407 B002                    	mov	al, 2
  2827 00001409 B500                    	mov	ch, 0
  2828 0000140B B102                    	mov	cl, FAT_SEC + 1
  2829 0000140D B600                    	mov	dh, 0
  2830 0000140F 8A16[0D3E]              	mov	dl, [resolved_drive]
  2831 00001413 CD13                    	int	0x13
  2832 00001415 C3                      	ret
  2833                                  
  2834                                  ; ============================================================================
  2835                                  ; write_fat — Write fat_buffer to both FAT copies
  2836                                  ; ============================================================================
  2837                                  write_fat:
  2838 00001416 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  2839 00001419 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  2840 0000141B BB004E                  	mov	bx, fat_buffer
  2841 0000141E B403                    	mov	ah, 0x03
  2842 00001420 B002                    	mov	al, 2
  2843 00001422 B500                    	mov	ch, 0
  2844 00001424 B102                    	mov	cl, FAT_SEC + 1
  2845 00001426 B600                    	mov	dh, 0
  2846 00001428 8A16[0D3E]              	mov	dl, [resolved_drive]
  2847 0000142C CD13                    	int	0x13
  2848 0000142E 7213                    	jc	.wf_done
  2849 00001430 BB004E                  	mov	bx, fat_buffer
  2850 00001433 B403                    	mov	ah, 0x03
  2851 00001435 B002                    	mov	al, 2
  2852 00001437 B500                    	mov	ch, 0
  2853 00001439 B104                    	mov	cl, FAT_SEC + 3
  2854 0000143B B600                    	mov	dh, 0
  2855 0000143D 8A16[0D3E]              	mov	dl, [resolved_drive]
  2856 00001441 CD13                    	int	0x13
  2857                                  .wf_done:
  2858 00001443 C3                      	ret
  2859                                  
  2860                                  ; ============================================================================
  2861                                  ; resolve_path — Resolve a path string to directory cluster + filename
  2862                                  ; ============================================================================
  2863                                  ; Input:  SI = pointer to path string (e.g., "SUBDIR\FILE.TXT" or "\DIR\FILE")
  2864                                  ; Output: resolved_dir_cluster = cluster of directory containing the file
  2865                                  ;         resolved_dir_entries = max entries in that directory
  2866                                  ;         exec_fname = parsed 8.3 filename of the final component
  2867                                  ;         carry set = error (directory not found)
  2868                                  ;         carry clear = success
  2869                                  ;
  2870                                  ; Handles: absolute paths (\DIR\FILE), relative paths (DIR\FILE),
  2871                                  ;          plain filenames (FILE.TXT), ".." components
  2872                                  ;
  2873                                  resolve_path:
  2874 00001444 53                      	push	bx
  2875 00001445 51                      	push	cx
  2876 00001446 52                      	push	dx
  2877                                  
  2878                                  	; Default to current drive
  2879 00001447 A0[083E]                	mov	al, [cur_drive]
  2880 0000144A A2[0D3E]                	mov	[resolved_drive], al
  2881                                  
  2882                                  	; Check for drive letter prefix (e.g., "A:" or "a:")
  2883 0000144D 807C013A                	cmp	byte [si+1], ':'
  2884 00001451 7544                    	jne	.rp_no_drive
  2885 00001453 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  2886                                  	; Uppercase
  2887 00001455 3C61                    	cmp	al, 'a'
  2888 00001457 7206                    	jb	.rp_drive_upper
  2889 00001459 3C7A                    	cmp	al, 'z'
  2890 0000145B 773A                    	ja	.rp_no_drive
  2891 0000145D 2C20                    	sub	al, 0x20
  2892                                  .rp_drive_upper:
  2893 0000145F 3C41                    	cmp	al, 'A'
  2894 00001461 7234                    	jb	.rp_no_drive
  2895 00001463 3C42                    	cmp	al, 'B'
  2896 00001465 7730                    	ja	.rp_no_drive
  2897 00001467 2C41                    	sub	al, 'A'			; 0=A, 1=B
  2898 00001469 A2[0D3E]                	mov	[resolved_drive], al
  2899 0000146C 83C602                  	add	si, 2			; Skip "X:"
  2900                                  	; Drive letter with \ = absolute from root
  2901                                  	; Drive letter without \ = relative to that drive's current dir
  2902 0000146F 803C5C                  	cmp	byte [si], '\'
  2903 00001472 7428                    	je	.rp_absolute
  2904                                  	; No backslash — relative to specified drive's current dir
  2905 00001474 803E[0D3E]00            	cmp	byte [resolved_drive], 0
  2906 00001479 750E                    	jne	.rp_drv_b_rel
  2907 0000147B A1[363D]                	mov	ax, [drv_a_cluster]
  2908 0000147E A3[093E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_cluster], ax
  2909 00001481 A1[383D]                	mov	ax, [drv_a_entries]
  2910 00001484 A3[0B3E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_entries], ax
  2911 00001487 EB2E                    	jmp	.rp_parse_component
  2912                                  .rp_drv_b_rel:
  2913 00001489 A1[7C3D]                	mov	ax, [drv_b_cluster]
  2914 0000148C A3[093E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_cluster], ax
  2915 0000148F A1[7E3D]                	mov	ax, [drv_b_entries]
  2916 00001492 A3[0B3E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_entries], ax
  2917 00001495 EB20                    	jmp	.rp_parse_component
  2918                                  .rp_no_drive:
  2919                                  
  2920                                  	; Start from current directory or root
  2921 00001497 803C5C                  	cmp	byte [si], '\'
  2922 0000149A 750F                    	jne	.rp_relative
  2923                                  .rp_absolute:
  2924                                  	; Absolute path — start from root
  2925 0000149C C706[093E]0000          	mov	word [resolved_dir_cluster], 0
  2926 000014A2 C706[0B3E]7000          	mov	word [resolved_dir_entries], MAX_DIR_ENTRIES
  2927 000014A8 46                      	inc	si			; Skip leading '\'
  2928 000014A9 EB0C                    	jmp	.rp_parse_component
  2929                                  .rp_relative:
  2930 000014AB A1[C23D]                	mov	ax, [cur_dir_cluster]
  2931 000014AE A3[093E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_cluster], ax
  2932 000014B1 A1[C43D]                	mov	ax, [cur_dir_entries]
  2933 000014B4 A3[0B3E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_entries], ax
  2934                                  
  2935                                  .rp_parse_component:
  2936                                  	; Check if we're at the end of the string
  2937 000014B7 803C00                  	cmp	byte [si], 0
  2938 000014BA 7503E99300              	je	.rp_no_file		; Path ends with no filename
  2939 000014BF 803C20                  	cmp	byte [si], ' '
  2940 000014C2 7503E98B00              	je	.rp_no_file
  2941                                  
  2942                                  	; Parse next component into exec_fname
  2943 000014C7 BF[F03C]                	mov	di, exec_fname
  2944 000014CA E86E03                  	call	parse_83_filename
  2945                                  
  2946                                  	; Check if there's more path after this component
  2947                                  	; SI was advanced by parse_83_filename
  2948                                  	; Check if we stopped at a '\'
  2949 000014CD 803C5C                  	cmp	byte [si], '\'
  2950 000014D0 7404                    	je	.rp_descend
  2951                                  	; No more '\' — this is the final filename
  2952                                  	; resolved_dir_cluster and exec_fname are set
  2953 000014D2 F8                      	clc
  2954 000014D3 E98700                  	jmp	.rp_done
  2955                                  
  2956                                  .rp_descend:
  2957 000014D6 46                      	inc	si			; Skip the '\'
  2958                                  
  2959                                  	; Handle "." (current dir) — skip it, no directory lookup needed
  2960 000014D7 803E[F03C]2E            	cmp	byte [exec_fname], '.'
  2961 000014DC 751E                    	jne	.rp_not_dot
  2962 000014DE 803E[F13C]20            	cmp	byte [exec_fname+1], ' '
  2963 000014E3 74D2                    	je	.rp_parse_component	; "." — stay in current dir, continue parsing
  2964                                  
  2965                                  	; Handle ".." — look up ".." entry (works in subdirs)
  2966                                  	; For root dir (cluster 0), ".." stays at root
  2967 000014E5 803E[F13C]2E            	cmp	byte [exec_fname+1], '.'
  2968 000014EA 7510                    	jne	.rp_not_dot
  2969 000014EC 803E[F23C]20            	cmp	byte [exec_fname+2], ' '
  2970 000014F1 7509                    	jne	.rp_not_dot
  2971 000014F3 833E[093E]00            	cmp	word [resolved_dir_cluster], 0
  2972 000014F8 7502                    	jne	.rp_not_dot		; Not root — normal lookup will find ".."
  2973                                  	; At root, ".." stays at root
  2974 000014FA EBBB                    	jmp	.rp_parse_component
  2975                                  
  2976                                  .rp_not_dot:
  2977                                  	; Look up this component in the current resolved directory
  2978                                  	; Save SI (rest of path)
  2979 000014FC 56                      	push	si
  2980                                  
  2981                                  	; Read the resolved directory
  2982 000014FD E86100                  	call	read_resolved_dir
  2983 00001500 722F                    	jc	.rp_err_pop
  2984                                  
  2985                                  	; Search for the component with directory attribute
  2986 00001502 BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  2987 00001505 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  2988                                  .rp_search:
  2989 00001509 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  2990 0000150B 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  2991 0000150D 741E                    	je	.rp_not_found_pop
  2992 0000150F 3CE5                    	cmp	al, 0xE5
  2993 00001511 7414                    	je	.rp_search_next
  2994 00001513 F6440B10                	test	byte [si+11], 0x10	; Directory?
  2995 00001517 740E                    	jz	.rp_search_next
  2996 00001519 51                      	push	cx
  2997 0000151A 56                      	push	si
  2998 0000151B BF[F03C]                	mov	di, exec_fname
  2999 0000151E B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  3000 00001521 F3A6                    	repe	cmpsb
  3001 00001523 5E                      	pop	si
  3002 00001524 59                      	pop	cx
  3003 00001525 740E                    	je	.rp_found_dir
  3004                                  .rp_search_next:
  3005 00001527 83C620                  	add	si, 32
  3006 0000152A 49                      	dec	cx
  3007 0000152B 75DC                    	jnz	.rp_search
  3008                                  
  3009                                  .rp_not_found_pop:
  3010 0000152D 5E                      	pop	si
  3011 0000152E F9                      	stc
  3012 0000152F EB2C                    	jmp	.rp_done
  3013                                  
  3014                                  .rp_err_pop:
  3015 00001531 5E                      	pop	si
  3016 00001532 F9                      	stc
  3017 00001533 EB28                    	jmp	.rp_done
  3018                                  
  3019                                  .rp_found_dir:
  3020                                  	; Update resolved directory to this subdirectory
  3021 00001535 8B441A                  	mov	ax, [si+26]
  3022 00001538 A3[093E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_cluster], ax
  3023 0000153B 83F800                  	cmp	ax, 0
  3024 0000153E 7508                    	jne	.rp_is_sub
  3025 00001540 C706[0B3E]7000          	mov	word [resolved_dir_entries], MAX_DIR_ENTRIES
  3026 00001546 EB06                    	jmp	.rp_restored
  3027                                  .rp_is_sub:
  3028 00001548 C706[0B3E]2000          	mov	word [resolved_dir_entries], SECS_PER_CLUST * 512 / 32
  3029                                  .rp_restored:
  3030 0000154E 5E                      	pop	si			; Restore rest of path
  3031 0000154F E965FF                  	jmp	.rp_parse_component
  3032                                  
  3033                                  .rp_no_file:
  3034                                  	; Path was just a directory path with no filename
  3035                                  	; Put empty filename in exec_fname
  3036 00001552 BF[F03C]                	mov	di, exec_fname
  3037 00001555 B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  3038 00001558 B020                    	mov	al, ' '
  3039 0000155A F3AA                    	rep	stosb
  3040 0000155C F8                      	clc
  3041                                  
  3042                                  .rp_done:
  3043 0000155D 5A                      	pop	dx
  3044 0000155E 59                      	pop	cx
  3045 0000155F 5B                      	pop	bx
  3046 00001560 C3                      	ret
  3047                                  
  3048                                  ; ============================================================================
  3049                                  ; read_resolved_dir — Read directory at resolved_dir_cluster into dir_buffer
  3050                                  ; ============================================================================
  3051                                  read_resolved_dir:
  3052 00001561 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  3053 00001564 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  3054 00001566 BB0040                  	mov	bx, dir_buffer
  3055 00001569 833E[093E]00            	cmp	word [resolved_dir_cluster], 0
  3056 0000156E 7511                    	jne	.rrd_subdir
  3057 00001570 B402                    	mov	ah, 0x02
  3058 00001572 B007                    	mov	al, ROOT_DIR_SECS
  3059 00001574 B500                    	mov	ch, 0
  3060 00001576 B106                    	mov	cl, ROOT_DIR_SEC + 1
  3061 00001578 B600                    	mov	dh, 0
  3062 0000157A 8A16[0D3E]              	mov	dl, [resolved_drive]
  3063 0000157E CD13                    	int	0x13
  3064 00001580 C3                      	ret
  3065                                  .rrd_subdir:
  3066 00001581 A1[093E]                	mov	ax, [resolved_dir_cluster]
  3067 00001584 E84BF8                  	call	cluster_to_chs
  3068 00001587 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  3069 0000158A 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  3070 0000158C BB0040                  	mov	bx, dir_buffer
  3071 0000158F B402                    	mov	ah, 0x02
  3072 00001591 B002                    	mov	al, SECS_PER_CLUST
  3073 00001593 8A16[0D3E]              	mov	dl, [resolved_drive]
  3074 00001597 CD13                    	int	0x13
  3075 00001599 C3                      	ret
  3076                                  
  3077                                  ; ============================================================================
  3078                                  ; write_resolved_dir — Write dir_buffer to resolved_dir_cluster
  3079                                  ; ============================================================================
  3080                                  write_resolved_dir:
  3081 0000159A B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  3082 0000159D 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  3083 0000159F BB0040                  	mov	bx, dir_buffer
  3084 000015A2 833E[093E]00            	cmp	word [resolved_dir_cluster], 0
  3085 000015A7 7511                    	jne	.wrd_subdir
  3086 000015A9 B403                    	mov	ah, 0x03
  3087 000015AB B007                    	mov	al, ROOT_DIR_SECS
  3088 000015AD B500                    	mov	ch, 0
  3089 000015AF B106                    	mov	cl, ROOT_DIR_SEC + 1
  3090 000015B1 B600                    	mov	dh, 0
  3091 000015B3 8A16[0D3E]              	mov	dl, [resolved_drive]
  3092 000015B7 CD13                    	int	0x13
  3093 000015B9 C3                      	ret
  3094                                  .wrd_subdir:
  3095 000015BA A1[093E]                	mov	ax, [resolved_dir_cluster]
  3096 000015BD E812F8                  	call	cluster_to_chs
  3097 000015C0 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  3098 000015C3 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  3099 000015C5 BB0040                  	mov	bx, dir_buffer
  3100 000015C8 B403                    	mov	ah, 0x03
  3101 000015CA B002                    	mov	al, SECS_PER_CLUST
  3102 000015CC 8A16[0D3E]              	mov	dl, [resolved_drive]
  3103 000015D0 CD13                    	int	0x13
  3104 000015D2 C3                      	ret
  3105                                  
  3106                                  ; ============================================================================
  3107                                  ; run_batch — Load and execute a batch file
  3108                                  ; ============================================================================
  3109                                  ; Input: SI = pointer to filename string (e.g., "AUTOEXEC.BAT")
  3110                                  ; Silently does nothing if file not found.
  3111                                  ; Sets batch_active=1 and batch_ptr, then returns to cmd_loop which
  3112                                  ; will read lines from the batch buffer instead of the keyboard.
  3113                                  ;
  3114                                  run_batch:
  3115                                  	; Resolve the filename
  3116 000015D3 E86EFE                  	call	resolve_path
  3117 000015D6 722A                    	jc	.rb_not_found
  3118                                  
  3119                                  	; Read resolved directory
  3120 000015D8 E886FF                  	call	read_resolved_dir
  3121 000015DB 7225                    	jc	.rb_not_found
  3122                                  
  3123                                  	; Search for the file
  3124 000015DD BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  3125 000015E0 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  3126                                  .rb_search:
  3127 000015E4 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  3128 000015E6 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  3129 000015E8 7418                    	je	.rb_not_found
  3130 000015EA 3CE5                    	cmp	al, 0xE5
  3131 000015EC 740E                    	je	.rb_search_next
  3132 000015EE 51                      	push	cx
  3133 000015EF 56                      	push	si
  3134 000015F0 BF[F03C]                	mov	di, exec_fname
  3135 000015F3 B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  3136 000015F6 F3A6                    	repe	cmpsb
  3137 000015F8 5E                      	pop	si
  3138 000015F9 59                      	pop	cx
  3139 000015FA 7407                    	je	.rb_found
  3140                                  .rb_search_next:
  3141 000015FC 83C620                  	add	si, 32
  3142 000015FF 49                      	dec	cx
  3143 00001600 75E2                    	jnz	.rb_search
  3144                                  
  3145                                  .rb_not_found:
  3146 00001602 C3                      	ret
  3147                                  
  3148                                  .rb_found:
  3149                                  	; Get cluster and size
  3150 00001603 8B441A                  	mov	ax, [si+26]
  3151 00001606 A3[163E]                	mov	[exec_cluster], ax
  3152 00001609 8B441C                  	mov	ax, [si+28]
  3153 0000160C A3[183E]                	mov	[exec_size], ax
  3154 0000160F 8B441E                  	mov	ax, [si+30]
  3155 00001612 A3[1A3E]                	mov	[exec_size+2], ax
  3156                                  
  3157                                  	; Load FAT
  3158 00001615 E8E5FD                  	call	read_fat
  3159 00001618 72E8                    	jc	.rb_not_found
  3160                                  
  3161                                  	; Load file data into batch_buffer
  3162 0000161A BB0052                  	mov	bx, batch_buffer
  3163 0000161D A1[163E]                	mov	ax, [exec_cluster]
  3164                                  
  3165                                  .rb_load_cluster:
  3166 00001620 50                      	push	ax
  3167 00001621 E8AEF7                  	call	cluster_to_chs
  3168 00001624 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  3169 00001627 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  3170 00001629 B402                    	mov	ah, 0x02
  3171 0000162B B002                    	mov	al, SECS_PER_CLUST
  3172 0000162D 8A16[0D3E]              	mov	dl, [resolved_drive]
  3173 00001631 CD13                    	int	0x13
  3174 00001633 58                      	pop	ax
  3175 00001634 72CC                    	jc	.rb_not_found
  3176                                  
  3177 00001636 81C30004                	add	bx, SECS_PER_CLUST * 512
  3178 0000163A E8BE06                  	call	fat12_next_cluster
  3179 0000163D 3DF80F                  	cmp	ax, 0xFF8
  3180 00001640 72DE                    	jb	.rb_load_cluster
  3181                                  
  3182                                  	; Set up batch execution
  3183 00001642 B80052                  	mov	ax, batch_buffer
  3184 00001645 0306[183E]              	add	ax, [exec_size]
  3185 00001649 A3[113E]                	mov	[batch_end], ax
  3186 0000164C C706[0F3E]0052          	mov	word [batch_ptr], batch_buffer
  3187 00001652 C606[0E3E]01            	mov	byte [batch_active], 1
  3188 00001657 C606[133E]01            	mov	byte [batch_echo], 1	; Echo on by default
  3189 0000165C C3                      	ret
  3190                                  
  3191                                  ; ============================================================================
  3192                                  ; batch_next_line — Get next line from batch buffer into cmd_buffer
  3193                                  ; ============================================================================
  3194                                  ; Called from cmd_loop when batch_active is set.
  3195                                  ; Copies one line, handles @, REM, PAUSE, then falls through to command dispatch.
  3196                                  ;
  3197                                  batch_next_line:
  3198 0000165D 8B36[0F3E]              	mov	si, [batch_ptr]
  3199 00001661 BF[9F3C]                	mov	di, cmd_buffer
  3200 00001664 B95000                  	mov	cx, MAX_CMD_LEN
  3201                                  
  3202                                  .bnl_copy:
  3203 00001667 3B36[113E]              	cmp	si, [batch_end]
  3204 0000166B 7203E9DD00              	jae	.bnl_eof
  3205 00001670 AC                      	lodsb
  3206 00001671 3C0A                    	cmp	al, 0x0A		; LF = end of line
  3207 00001673 740F                    	je	.bnl_line_done
  3208 00001675 3C0D                    	cmp	al, 0x0D		; CR = skip
  3209 00001677 74EE                    	je	.bnl_copy
  3210 00001679 3C1A                    	cmp	al, 0x1A		; Ctrl-Z = EOF
  3211 0000167B 7503E9CD00              	je	.bnl_eof
  3212 00001680 AA                      	stosb
  3213 00001681 49                      	dec	cx
  3214 00001682 75E3                    	jnz	.bnl_copy
  3215                                  
  3216                                  .bnl_line_done:
  3217 00001684 C60500                  	mov	byte [di], 0
  3218 00001687 8936[0F3E]              	mov	[batch_ptr], si
  3219                                  
  3220                                  	; Skip empty lines
  3221 0000168B BE[9F3C]                	mov	si, cmd_buffer
  3222 0000168E E89322                  	call	skip_spaces
  3223 00001691 803C00                  	cmp	byte [si], 0
  3224 00001694 7503E932EA              	je	cmd_loop		; Empty line — get next
  3225                                  
  3226                                  	; Check for @ prefix — suppress echo for this line
  3227 00001699 C606FF5100              	mov	byte [batch_buffer - 1], 0  ; temp: this_line_silent flag (reuse byte before buffer)
  3228 0000169E 803C40                  	cmp	byte [si], '@'
  3229 000016A1 750F                    	jne	.bnl_check_echo_state
  3230 000016A3 C606FF5101              	mov	byte [batch_buffer - 1], 1  ; This line is silent
  3231                                  	; Strip @ from buffer
  3232 000016A8 46                      	inc	si
  3233 000016A9 BF[9F3C]                	mov	di, cmd_buffer
  3234                                  .bnl_shift:
  3235 000016AC AC                      	lodsb
  3236 000016AD AA                      	stosb
  3237 000016AE 08C0                    	or	al, al
  3238 000016B0 75FA                    	jnz	.bnl_shift
  3239                                  
  3240                                  .bnl_check_echo_state:
  3241                                  	; Check for ECHO OFF / ECHO ON
  3242 000016B2 BE[9F3C]                	mov	si, cmd_buffer
  3243 000016B5 E86C22                  	call	skip_spaces
  3244 000016B8 56                      	push	si
  3245 000016B9 BF[713C]                	mov	di, cmd_echo
  3246 000016BC E86E22                  	call	str_compare_cmd
  3247 000016BF 752E                    	jne	.bnl_not_echo_cmd
  3248                                  	; It's an ECHO command — check for OFF/ON
  3249 000016C1 E86022                  	call	skip_spaces
  3250 000016C4 56                      	push	si
  3251 000016C5 BF[3418]                	mov	di, str_off
  3252 000016C8 E86222                  	call	str_compare_cmd
  3253 000016CB 740E                    	je	.bnl_echo_off
  3254 000016CD 5E                      	pop	si
  3255 000016CE 56                      	push	si
  3256 000016CF BF[3818]                	mov	di, str_on
  3257 000016D2 E85822                  	call	str_compare_cmd
  3258 000016D5 740E                    	je	.bnl_echo_on
  3259 000016D7 5E                      	pop	si
  3260 000016D8 5E                      	pop	si			; Discard saved SI from echo check
  3261 000016D9 EB15                    	jmp	.bnl_do_echo_line	; Regular ECHO with text
  3262                                  
  3263                                  .bnl_echo_off:
  3264 000016DB 5E                      	pop	si
  3265 000016DC 5E                      	pop	si
  3266 000016DD C606[133E]00            	mov	byte [batch_echo], 0
  3267 000016E2 E9E6E9                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  3268                                  .bnl_echo_on:
  3269 000016E5 5E                      	pop	si
  3270 000016E6 5E                      	pop	si
  3271 000016E7 C606[133E]01            	mov	byte [batch_echo], 1
  3272 000016EC E9DCE9                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  3273                                  
  3274                                  .bnl_not_echo_cmd:
  3275 000016EF 5E                      	pop	si
  3276                                  
  3277                                  .bnl_do_echo_line:
  3278                                  	; Echo the line if echo is on AND line is not @-prefixed
  3279 000016F0 803EFF5101              	cmp	byte [batch_buffer - 1], 1
  3280 000016F5 741B                    	je	.bnl_skip_echo		; @ prefix — don't echo
  3281 000016F7 803E[133E]00            	cmp	byte [batch_echo], 0
  3282 000016FC 7414                    	je	.bnl_skip_echo		; Echo off — don't echo
  3283                                  	; Echo the line
  3284 000016FE 56                      	push	si
  3285 000016FF BE[9F3C]                	mov	si, cmd_buffer
  3286 00001702 E8BD21                  	call	print_string
  3287 00001705 B00D                    	mov	al, 0x0D
  3288 00001707 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  3289 00001709 CD10                    	int	0x10
  3290 0000170B B00A                    	mov	al, 0x0A
  3291 0000170D B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  3292 0000170F CD10                    	int	0x10
  3293 00001711 5E                      	pop	si
  3294                                  .bnl_skip_echo:
  3295                                  
  3296                                  	; Check for REM (comment) — skip
  3297 00001712 BE[9F3C]                	mov	si, cmd_buffer
  3298 00001715 E80C22                  	call	skip_spaces
  3299 00001718 56                      	push	si
  3300 00001719 BF[2A18]                	mov	di, cmd_rem
  3301 0000171C E80E22                  	call	str_compare_cmd
  3302 0000171F 740E                    	je	.bnl_skip_rem
  3303                                  
  3304                                  	; Check for PAUSE
  3305 00001721 5E                      	pop	si
  3306 00001722 56                      	push	si
  3307 00001723 BF[2E18]                	mov	di, cmd_pause
  3308 00001726 E80422                  	call	str_compare_cmd
  3309 00001729 7408                    	je	.bnl_do_pause
  3310                                  
  3311 0000172B 5E                      	pop	si
  3312                                  	; Fall through to normal command dispatch
  3313 0000172C E9F9E9                  	jmp	cmd_dispatch
  3314                                  
  3315                                  .bnl_skip_rem:
  3316 0000172F 5E                      	pop	si
  3317 00001730 E998E9                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  3318                                  
  3319                                  .bnl_do_pause:
  3320 00001733 5E                      	pop	si
  3321 00001734 BE[D23B]                	mov	si, msg_pause
  3322 00001737 E88821                  	call	print_string
  3323 0000173A B400                    	mov	ah, 0x00
  3324 0000173C CD16                    	int	0x16
  3325 0000173E B00D                    	mov	al, 0x0D
  3326 00001740 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  3327 00001742 CD10                    	int	0x10
  3328 00001744 B00A                    	mov	al, 0x0A
  3329 00001746 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  3330 00001748 CD10                    	int	0x10
  3331 0000174A E97EE9                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  3332                                  
  3333                                  .bnl_eof:
  3334 0000174D C606[0E3E]00            	mov	byte [batch_active], 0
  3335 00001752 E976E9                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  3336                                  
  3337                                  ; ============================================================================
  3338                                  ; print_2digit — Print AX as 2-digit number with leading zero
  3339                                  ; ============================================================================
  3340                                  print_2digit:
  3341 00001755 50                      	push	ax
  3342 00001756 53                      	push	bx
  3343 00001757 30E4                    	xor	ah, ah
  3344 00001759 B30A                    	mov	bl, 10
  3345 0000175B F6F3                    	div	bl			; AL = tens, AH = ones
  3346 0000175D 50                      	push	ax
  3347 0000175E 0430                    	add	al, '0'
  3348 00001760 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  3349 00001762 CD10                    	int	0x10
  3350 00001764 58                      	pop	ax
  3351 00001765 88E0                    	mov	al, ah
  3352 00001767 0430                    	add	al, '0'
  3353 00001769 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  3354 0000176B CD10                    	int	0x10
  3355 0000176D 5B                      	pop	bx
  3356 0000176E 58                      	pop	ax
  3357 0000176F C3                      	ret
  3358                                  
  3359                                  ; ============================================================================
  3360                                  ; print_2digit_space — Print AX as 2-digit with leading space (not zero)
  3361                                  ; ============================================================================
  3362                                  print_2digit_space:
  3363 00001770 50                      	push	ax
  3364 00001771 53                      	push	bx
  3365 00001772 30E4                    	xor	ah, ah
  3366 00001774 B30A                    	mov	bl, 10
  3367 00001776 F6F3                    	div	bl			; AL = tens, AH = ones
  3368 00001778 50                      	push	ax
  3369 00001779 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  3370 0000177B 7504                    	jne	.p2ds_tens
  3371 0000177D B020                    	mov	al, ' '			; Space instead of '0'
  3372 0000177F EB02                    	jmp	.p2ds_print_tens
  3373                                  .p2ds_tens:
  3374 00001781 0430                    	add	al, '0'
  3375                                  .p2ds_print_tens:
  3376 00001783 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  3377 00001785 CD10                    	int	0x10
  3378 00001787 58                      	pop	ax
  3379 00001788 88E0                    	mov	al, ah
  3380 0000178A 0430                    	add	al, '0'
  3381 0000178C B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  3382 0000178E CD10                    	int	0x10
  3383 00001790 5B                      	pop	bx
  3384 00001791 58                      	pop	ax
  3385 00001792 C3                      	ret
  3386                                  
  3387                                  ; ============================================================================
  3388                                  ; print_size_padded — Print DX:AX as right-aligned number in 10 chars
  3389                                  ; ============================================================================
  3390                                  print_size_padded:
  3391 00001793 50                      	push	ax
  3392 00001794 53                      	push	bx
  3393 00001795 51                      	push	cx
  3394 00001796 52                      	push	dx
  3395                                  
  3396                                  	; Count digits first
  3397 00001797 50                      	push	ax
  3398 00001798 52                      	push	dx
  3399 00001799 B90000                  	mov	cx, 0
  3400 0000179C BB0A00                  	mov	bx, 10
  3401                                  .psp_count:
  3402 0000179F 50                      	push	ax
  3403 000017A0 89D0                    	mov	ax, dx
  3404 000017A2 31D2                    	xor	dx, dx
  3405 000017A4 F7F3                    	div	bx
  3406 000017A6 A3[DE17]                	mov	word [.psp_tmp], ax
  3407 000017A9 58                      	pop	ax
  3408 000017AA F7F3                    	div	bx
  3409 000017AC 52                      	push	dx
  3410 000017AD 8B16[DE17]              	mov	dx, [.psp_tmp]
  3411 000017B1 41                      	inc	cx
  3412 000017B2 09C0                    	or	ax, ax
  3413 000017B4 75E9                    	jnz	.psp_count
  3414 000017B6 09D2                    	or	dx, dx
  3415 000017B8 75E5                    	jnz	.psp_count
  3416                                  
  3417                                  	; Print leading spaces (10 - digit_count)
  3418 000017BA 89CB                    	mov	bx, cx		; Save digit count
  3419 000017BC B80A00                  	mov	ax, 10
  3420 000017BF 29C8                    	sub	ax, cx
  3421 000017C1 89C1                    	mov	cx, ax
  3422 000017C3 E309                    	jcxz	.psp_no_pad
  3423                                  .psp_pad:
  3424 000017C5 B020                    	mov	al, ' '
  3425 000017C7 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  3426 000017C9 CD10                    	int	0x10
  3427 000017CB 49                      	dec	cx
  3428 000017CC 75F7                    	jnz	.psp_pad
  3429                                  .psp_no_pad:
  3430                                  	; Discard counted digits from stack
  3431 000017CE 89D9                    	mov	cx, bx
  3432                                  .psp_discard:
  3433 000017D0 58                      	pop	ax
  3434 000017D1 49                      	dec	cx
  3435 000017D2 75FC                    	jnz	.psp_discard
  3436 000017D4 5A                      	pop	dx
  3437 000017D5 58                      	pop	ax
  3438                                  
  3439                                  	; Now print the actual number
  3440 000017D6 E88921                  	call	print_decimal_32
  3441                                  
  3442 000017D9 5A                      	pop	dx
  3443 000017DA 59                      	pop	cx
  3444 000017DB 5B                      	pop	bx
  3445 000017DC 58                      	pop	ax
  3446 000017DD C3                      	ret
  3447 000017DE 0000                    .psp_tmp	dw	0
  3448                                  
  3449                                  ; ============================================================================
  3450                                  ; print_rpad_dec — Print DX:AX right-aligned in CX character width
  3451                                  ; ============================================================================
  3452                                  print_rpad_dec:
  3453 000017E0 50                      	push	ax
  3454 000017E1 53                      	push	bx
  3455 000017E2 51                      	push	cx
  3456 000017E3 52                      	push	dx
  3457                                  	; Use print_size_padded logic but with variable width
  3458                                  	; For simplicity, just print spaces then the number
  3459                                  	; Count digits
  3460 000017E4 50                      	push	ax
  3461 000017E5 52                      	push	dx
  3462 000017E6 51                      	push	cx			; Save width
  3463 000017E7 B90000                  	mov	cx, 0
  3464 000017EA BB0A00                  	mov	bx, 10
  3465                                  .prpd_count:
  3466 000017ED 50                      	push	ax
  3467 000017EE 89D0                    	mov	ax, dx
  3468 000017F0 31D2                    	xor	dx, dx
  3469 000017F2 F7F3                    	div	bx
  3470 000017F4 A3[2818]                	mov	[.prpd_tmp], ax
  3471 000017F7 58                      	pop	ax
  3472 000017F8 F7F3                    	div	bx
  3473 000017FA 52                      	push	dx
  3474 000017FB 8B16[2818]              	mov	dx, [.prpd_tmp]
  3475 000017FF 41                      	inc	cx
  3476 00001800 09C0                    	or	ax, ax
  3477 00001802 75E9                    	jnz	.prpd_count
  3478 00001804 09D2                    	or	dx, dx
  3479 00001806 75E5                    	jnz	.prpd_count
  3480 00001808 89CB                    	mov	bx, cx			; BX = digit count
  3481                                  	; Discard digits from stack
  3482                                  .prpd_pop:
  3483 0000180A 58                      	pop	ax
  3484 0000180B 49                      	dec	cx
  3485 0000180C 75FC                    	jnz	.prpd_pop

  3487 0000180F 5A                      	pop	dx

  3491 00001813 7E0B                    	jle	.prpd_no_pad
  3492                                  .prpd_pad:

  3494 00001816 B020                    	mov	al, ' '
  3495 00001818 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  3496 0000181A CD10                    	int	0x10
  3497 0000181C 58                      	pop	ax
  3498 0000181D 49                      	dec	cx
  3499 0000181E 75F5                    	jnz	.prpd_pad
  3500                                  .prpd_no_pad:

  3502 00001823 5A                      	pop	dx

  3506 00001827 C3                      	ret

  3514                                  ; ============================================================================
  3515                                  ; parse_83_filename — Parse filename at DS:SI into 8.3 format at ES:DI
  3516                                  ; ============================================================================
  3517                                  ; Input:  SI = pointer to filename string (null/space terminated)
  3518                                  ;         DI = pointer to 11-byte output buffer
  3519                                  ; Output: DI buffer filled with 8.3 name (space padded)
  3520                                  ;         SI advanced past the filename
  3521                                  ;
  3522                                  parse_83_filename:
  3523 0000183B 50                      	push	ax
  3524 0000183C 51                      	push	cx
  3525 0000183D 57                      	push	di
  3526                                  	; Fill with spaces
  3527 0000183E 57                      	push	di
  3528 0000183F B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  3529 00001842 B020                    	mov	al, ' '
  3530 00001844 F3AA                    	rep	stosb
  3531 00001846 5F                      	pop	di
  3532                                  
  3533                                  	; Special case: "." and ".." are stored as-is, not as name.ext
  3534 00001847 803C2E                  	cmp	byte [si], '.'
  3535 0000184A 7541                    	jne	.p83_normal
  3536 0000184C 807C012E                	cmp	byte [si+1], '.'
  3537 00001850 741B                    	je	.p83_dotdot
  3538                                  	; Check if "." is alone (followed by \, space, or null)
  3539 00001852 807C015C                	cmp	byte [si+1], '\'
  3540 00001856 740E                    	je	.p83_single_dot
  3541 00001858 807C0120                	cmp	byte [si+1], ' '
  3542 0000185C 7408                    	je	.p83_single_dot
  3543 0000185E 807C0100                	cmp	byte [si+1], 0
  3544 00001862 7402                    	je	.p83_single_dot
  3545 00001864 EB27                    	jmp	.p83_normal		; "." followed by something else = has extension
  3546                                  .p83_single_dot:
  3547 00001866 C6052E                  	mov	byte [di], '.'
  3548 00001869 46                      	inc	si
  3549 0000186A E98300                  	jmp	.p83_done
  3550                                  .p83_dotdot:
  3551                                  	; Check ".." is alone
  3552 0000186D 807C025C                	cmp	byte [si+2], '\'
  3553 00001871 740E                    	je	.p83_is_dotdot
  3554 00001873 807C0220                	cmp	byte [si+2], ' '
  3555 00001877 7408                    	je	.p83_is_dotdot
  3556 00001879 807C0200                	cmp	byte [si+2], 0
  3557 0000187D 7402                    	je	.p83_is_dotdot
  3558 0000187F EB0C                    	jmp	.p83_normal
  3559                                  .p83_is_dotdot:
  3560 00001881 C6052E                  	mov	byte [di], '.'
  3561 00001884 C645012E                	mov	byte [di+1], '.'
  3562 00001888 83C602                  	add	si, 2
  3563 0000188B EB63                    	jmp	.p83_done
  3564                                  
  3565                                  .p83_normal:
  3566                                  	; Copy name part (up to 8 chars)
  3567 0000188D B90800                  	mov	cx, 8
  3568                                  .p83_name:
  3569 00001890 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  3570 00001892 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  3571 00001894 745A                    	je	.p83_done
  3572 00001896 3C20                    	cmp	al, ' '
  3573 00001898 7456                    	je	.p83_done
  3574 0000189A 3C5C                    	cmp	al, '\'
  3575 0000189C 7452                    	je	.p83_done
  3576 0000189E 3C2E                    	cmp	al, '.'
  3577 000018A0 7426                    	je	.p83_dot
  3578 000018A2 3C61                    	cmp	al, 'a'
  3579 000018A4 7206                    	jb	.p83_no_upper
  3580 000018A6 3C7A                    	cmp	al, 'z'
  3581 000018A8 7702                    	ja	.p83_no_upper
  3582 000018AA 2C20                    	sub	al, 0x20
  3583                                  .p83_no_upper:
  3584 000018AC 8805                    	mov	[di], al
  3585 000018AE 46                      	inc	si
  3586 000018AF 47                      	inc	di
  3587 000018B0 49                      	dec	cx
  3588 000018B1 75DD                    	jnz	.p83_name
  3589                                  	; Skip to dot or end
  3590                                  .p83_skip:
  3591 000018B3 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  3592 000018B5 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  3593 000018B7 7437                    	je	.p83_done
  3594 000018B9 3C20                    	cmp	al, ' '
  3595 000018BB 7433                    	je	.p83_done
  3596 000018BD 3C5C                    	cmp	al, '\'
  3597 000018BF 742F                    	je	.p83_done
  3598 000018C1 3C2E                    	cmp	al, '.'
  3599 000018C3 7403                    	je	.p83_dot
  3600 000018C5 46                      	inc	si
  3601 000018C6 EBEB                    	jmp	.p83_skip
  3602                                  .p83_dot:
  3603 000018C8 46                      	inc	si
  3604 000018C9 5F                      	pop	di
  3605 000018CA 57                      	push	di
  3606 000018CB 83C708                  	add	di, 8			; Extension at offset 8
  3607 000018CE B90300                  	mov	cx, 3
  3608                                  .p83_ext:
  3609 000018D1 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  3610 000018D3 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  3611 000018D5 7419                    	je	.p83_done
  3612 000018D7 3C20                    	cmp	al, ' '
  3613 000018D9 7415                    	je	.p83_done
  3614 000018DB 3C5C                    	cmp	al, '\'
  3615 000018DD 7411                    	je	.p83_done
  3616 000018DF 3C61                    	cmp	al, 'a'
  3617 000018E1 7206                    	jb	.p83_no_upper2
  3618 000018E3 3C7A                    	cmp	al, 'z'
  3619 000018E5 7702                    	ja	.p83_no_upper2
  3620 000018E7 2C20                    	sub	al, 0x20
  3621                                  .p83_no_upper2:
  3622 000018E9 8805                    	mov	[di], al
  3623 000018EB 46                      	inc	si
  3624 000018EC 47                      	inc	di
  3625 000018ED 49                      	dec	cx
  3626 000018EE 75E1                    	jnz	.p83_ext
  3627                                  .p83_done:
  3628 000018F0 5F                      	pop	di
  3629 000018F1 59                      	pop	cx
  3630 000018F2 58                      	pop	ax
  3631 000018F3 C3                      	ret

  3633                                  ; ============================================================================
  3634                                  ; parse_wildcard — parse filename with * and ? into 11-byte pattern
  3635                                  ; Input: SI = user string, DI = 11-byte buffer
  3636                                  ; '*' fills remaining name/ext positions with '?'
  3637                                  ; Output: SI advanced past parsed name
  3638                                  ;         Sets wild_active=1 if any wildcards found, else 0
  3639                                  ; ============================================================================
  3640                                  parse_wildcard:
  3641 000018F4 50                      	push	ax
  3642 000018F5 51                      	push	cx
  3643 000018F6 57                      	push	di
  3644 000018F7 C606[073D]00            	mov	byte [wild_active], 0
  3645                                  	; Fill with spaces
  3646 000018FC 57                      	push	di
  3647 000018FD B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  3648 00001900 B020                    	mov	al, ' '
  3649 00001902 F3AA                    	rep	stosb
  3650 00001904 5F                      	pop	di
  3651                                  
  3652                                  	; Name part (up to 8 chars)
  3653 00001905 B90800                  	mov	cx, 8
  3654                                  .pw_name:

  3656 0000190A 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  3657 0000190C 7503E9AB00              	je	.pw_done
  3658 00001911 3C20                    	cmp	al, ' '
  3659 00001913 7503E9A400              	je	.pw_done
  3660 00001918 3C5C                    	cmp	al, '\'
  3661 0000191A 7503E99D00              	je	.pw_done
  3662 0000191F 3C2E                    	cmp	al, '.'
  3663 00001921 7448                    	je	.pw_dot

  3665 00001925 741C                    	je	.pw_star_name
  3666 00001927 3C3F                    	cmp	al, '?'
  3667 00001929 7505                    	jne	.pw_name_char
  3668 0000192B C606[073D]01            	mov	byte [wild_active], 1
  3669                                  .pw_name_char:

  3671 00001932 7206                    	jb	.pw_name_store
  3672 00001934 3C7A                    	cmp	al, 'z'
  3673 00001936 7702                    	ja	.pw_name_store

  3681 00001941 EB13                    	jmp	.pw_skip_to_dot

  3684 00001943 C606[073D]01            	mov	byte [wild_active], 1
  3685                                  	; Fill rest of name with '?'
  3686 00001948 B03F                    	mov	al, '?'
  3687                                  .pw_fill_name:

  3689 0000194D 7406                    	je	.pw_star_name_done

  3691 00001951 47                      	inc	di
  3692 00001952 49                      	dec	cx
  3693 00001953 EBF5                    	jmp	.pw_fill_name
  3694                                  .pw_star_name_done:
  3695 00001955 46                      	inc	si		; skip the '*'
  3696                                  	; Skip to dot or end
  3697                                  .pw_skip_to_dot:
  3698 00001956 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  3699 00001958 3C2E                    	cmp	al, '.'
  3700 0000195A 740F                    	je	.pw_dot
  3701 0000195C 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  3702 0000195E 7442                    	je	.pw_star_ext	; No extension after * means match all extensions
  3703 00001960 3C20                    	cmp	al, ' '
  3704 00001962 743E                    	je	.pw_star_ext
  3705 00001964 3C5C                    	cmp	al, '\'
  3706 00001966 743A                    	je	.pw_star_ext
  3707 00001968 46                      	inc	si
  3708 00001969 EBEB                    	jmp	.pw_skip_to_dot
  3709                                  
  3710                                  .pw_dot:
  3711 0000196B 46                      	inc	si		; skip '.'
  3712 0000196C 5F                      	pop	di
  3713 0000196D 57                      	push	di
  3714 0000196E 83C708                  	add	di, 8		; extension part
  3715 00001971 B90300                  	mov	cx, 3
  3716                                  .pw_ext:
  3717 00001974 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  3718 00001976 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  3719 00001978 7442                    	je	.pw_done
  3720 0000197A 3C20                    	cmp	al, ' '
  3721 0000197C 743E                    	je	.pw_done
  3722 0000197E 3C5C                    	cmp	al, '\'
  3723 00001980 743A                    	je	.pw_done
  3724 00001982 3C2A                    	cmp	al, '*'
  3725 00001984 741C                    	je	.pw_star_ext

  3732 00001993 3C7A                    	cmp	al, 'z'

  3741 000019A0 EB1A                    	jmp	.pw_done
  3742                                  
  3743                                  .pw_star_ext:
  3744 000019A2 C606[073D]01            	mov	byte [wild_active], 1

  3765                                  ; ============================================================================
  3766                                  ; match_wildcard — check if dir entry matches wildcard pattern
  3767                                  ; Input: SI = pointer to dir entry (11-byte name), DI = 11-byte pattern
  3768                                  ; Output: ZF=1 if match, ZF=0 if no match
  3769                                  ; Preserves all registers
  3770                                  ; ============================================================================
  3771                                  match_wildcard:
  3772 000019C0 51                      	push	cx
  3773 000019C1 56                      	push	si
  3774 000019C2 57                      	push	di
  3775 000019C3 B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  3776                                  .mw_next:
  3777 000019C6 8A05                    	mov	al, [di]
  3778 000019C8 3C3F                    	cmp	al, '?'
  3779 000019CA 7404                    	je	.mw_skip		; '?' matches anything
  3780 000019CC 3A04                    	cmp	al, [si]
  3781 000019CE 750A                    	jne	.mw_no_match
  3782                                  .mw_skip:
  3783 000019D0 46                      	inc	si
  3784 000019D1 47                      	inc	di
  3785 000019D2 49                      	dec	cx
  3786 000019D3 75F1                    	jnz	.mw_next
  3787                                  	; All 11 matched
  3788 000019D5 5F                      	pop	di
  3789 000019D6 5E                      	pop	si
  3790 000019D7 59                      	pop	cx
  3791 000019D8 F8                      	clc			; CF=0 = match
  3792 000019D9 C3                      	ret
  3793                                  .mw_no_match:

  3795 000019DB 5E                      	pop	si
  3796 000019DC 59                      	pop	cx

  3798 000019DE C3                      	ret

  3800                                  ; ============================================================================
  3801                                  ; EXEC — load and execute .COM file
  3802                                  ; ============================================================================
  3803                                  do_exec:
  3804                                  	; SI points to the command (filename)
  3805                                  	; Resolve path
  3806 000019DF E862FA                  	call	resolve_path
  3807 000019E2 7303E98400              	jc	.exec_not_found
  3808                                  	; Save SI — it now points to the command tail (arguments)
  3809 000019E7 8936[2B3E]              	mov	[exec_cmdtail_ptr], si
  3810                                  
  3811                                  	; If no extension was given, try .COM → .EXE → .BAT
  3812 000019EB C606[2A3E]00            	mov	byte [exec_try_ext], 0
  3813 000019F0 803E[F83C]20            	cmp	byte [exec_fname+8], ' '
  3814 000019F5 7547                    	jne	.has_ext
  3815 000019F7 C606[F83C]43            	mov	byte [exec_fname+8], 'C'
  3816 000019FC C606[F93C]4F            	mov	byte [exec_fname+9], 'O'
  3817 00001A01 C606[FA3C]4D            	mov	byte [exec_fname+10], 'M'
  3818 00001A06 C606[2A3E]01            	mov	byte [exec_try_ext], 1	; 1=try EXE next, 2=try BAT next
  3819 00001A0B EB31                    	jmp	.has_ext
  3820                                  .exec_retry_ext:
  3821 00001A0D 803E[2A3E]01            	cmp	byte [exec_try_ext], 1
  3822 00001A12 7516                    	jne	.exec_retry_bat

  3824 00001A19 C606[F93C]58            	mov	byte [exec_fname+9], 'X'
  3825 00001A1E C606[FA3C]45            	mov	byte [exec_fname+10], 'E'
  3826 00001A23 C606[2A3E]02            	mov	byte [exec_try_ext], 2
  3827 00001A28 EB14                    	jmp	.has_ext
  3828                                  .exec_retry_bat:
  3829 00001A2A C606[F83C]42            	mov	byte [exec_fname+8], 'B'
  3830 00001A2F C606[F93C]41            	mov	byte [exec_fname+9], 'A'
  3831 00001A34 C606[FA3C]54            	mov	byte [exec_fname+10], 'T'
  3832 00001A39 C606[2A3E]00            	mov	byte [exec_try_ext], 0
  3833                                  .has_ext:
  3834                                  
  3835                                  	; Read resolved directory
  3836 00001A3E E820FB                  	call	read_resolved_dir

  3843                                  .search_entry:

  3860                                  .search_next:
  3861 00001A65 83C620                  	add	si, 32

  3863 00001A69 75E2                    	jnz	.search_entry

  3865                                  .exec_not_found:
  3866                                  	; Try next extension: .COM → .EXE → .BAT
  3867 00001A6B 803E[2A3E]00            	cmp	byte [exec_try_ext], 0
  3868 00001A70 7402                    	je	.exec_really_not_found
  3869 00001A72 EB99                    	jmp	.exec_retry_ext
  3870

  3880 00001A84 803E[F93C]41            	cmp	byte [exec_fname+9], 'A'

  3883 00001A90 7530                    	jne	.exec_not_bat

  3885 00001A92 BF[9F3C]                	mov	di, cmd_buffer

  3902 00001AB1 47                      	inc	di
  3903 00001AB2 C60554                  	mov	byte [di], 'T'
  3904 00001AB5 47                      	inc	di
