  3907 00001ABC E814FB                  	call	run_batch
  3908 00001ABF E909E6                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  3909                                  
  3910                                  .exec_not_bat:
  3911                                  	; SI points to the matching directory entry
  3912                                  	; Get starting cluster (offset 26)
  3913 00001AC2 8B441A                  	mov	ax, [si+26]
  3914 00001AC5 A3[163E]                	mov	[exec_cluster], ax
  3915                                  	; Get file size (offset 28)
  3916 00001AC8 8B441C                  	mov	ax, [si+28]
  3917 00001ACB A3[183E]                	mov	[exec_size], ax
  3918 00001ACE 8B441E                  	mov	ax, [si+30]
  3919 00001AD1 A3[1A3E]                	mov	[exec_size+2], ax
  3920                                  
  3921                                  	; Load FAT
  3922 00001AD4 E826F9                  	call	read_fat
  3923 00001AD7 7303E91602              	jc	.exec_disk_err
  3924                                  
  3925                                  	; Allocate memory for the program
  3926                                  	; Size in paragraphs = (file_size + 256 (PSP) + 15) / 16 + some stack
  3927                                  	; For .COM: allocate all available memory (like DOS)
  3928                                  	; For .EXE: allocate based on header
  3929 00001ADC BBFFFF                  	mov	bx, 0xFFFF		; Request maximum
  3930 00001ADF B448                    	mov	ah, 0x48
  3931 00001AE1 CD21                    	int	0x21			; Will fail but BX = largest block
  3932                                  	; Now allocate that largest block
  3933 00001AE3 B448                    	mov	ah, 0x48
  3934 00001AE5 CD21                    	int	0x21
  3935 00001AE7 7303E9F401              	jc	.exec_no_mem
  3936 00001AEC A3[1C3E]                	mov	[exec_seg], ax		; Save allocated segment
  3937                                  
  3938                                  	; Create PSP at allocated segment
  3939 00001AEF 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  3940                                  
  3941                                  	; Clear PSP area first
  3942 00001AF1 50                      	push	ax
  3943 00001AF2 51                      	push	cx
  3944 00001AF3 57                      	push	di
  3945 00001AF4 31FF                    	xor	di, di
  3946 00001AF6 31C0                    	xor	ax, ax
  3947 00001AF8 B98000                  	mov	cx, 128			; 256 bytes / 2
  3948 00001AFB F3AB                    	rep	stosw
  3949 00001AFD 5F                      	pop	di
  3950 00001AFE 59                      	pop	cx
  3951 00001AFF 58                      	pop	ax
  3952                                  
  3953                                  	; PSP:00 — INT 20h instruction
  3954 00001B00 26C6060000CD            	mov	byte [es:0x00], 0xCD	; INT
  3955 00001B06 26C606010020            	mov	byte [es:0x01], 0x20	; 20h
  3956                                  
  3957                                  	; PSP:02 — Memory top segment
  3958 00001B0C 26C706020000A0          	mov	word [es:0x02], 0xA000
  3959                                  
  3960                                  	; PSP:05 — FAR CALL to DOS (CP/M compat: CALL 5 → INT 21h)
  3961 00001B13 26C6060500CD            	mov	byte [es:0x05], 0xCD	; INT
  3962 00001B19 26C606060021            	mov	byte [es:0x06], 0x21	; 21h
  3963 00001B1F 26C6060700CB            	mov	byte [es:0x07], 0xCB	; RETF
  3964                                  
  3965                                  	; PSP:0A — Save parent's INT 22h (terminate handler)
  3966 00001B25 1E                      	push	ds
  3967 00001B26 31C0                    	xor	ax, ax
  3968 00001B28 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  3969 00001B2A 3EA18800                	mov	ax, [ds:0x88]		; INT 22h offset
  3970 00001B2E 26A30A00                	mov	[es:0x0A], ax
  3971 00001B32 3EA18A00                	mov	ax, [ds:0x8A]		; INT 22h segment
  3972 00001B36 26A30C00                	mov	[es:0x0C], ax
  3973                                  	; PSP:0E — Save parent's INT 23h (Ctrl-C handler)
  3974 00001B3A 3EA18C00                	mov	ax, [ds:0x8C]		; INT 23h offset
  3975 00001B3E 26A30E00                	mov	[es:0x0E], ax
  3976 00001B42 3EA18E00                	mov	ax, [ds:0x8E]		; INT 23h segment
  3977 00001B46 26A31000                	mov	[es:0x10], ax
  3978                                  	; PSP:12 — Save parent's INT 24h (critical error handler)
  3979 00001B4A 3EA19000                	mov	ax, [ds:0x90]		; INT 24h offset
  3980 00001B4E 26A31200                	mov	[es:0x12], ax
  3981 00001B52 3EA19200                	mov	ax, [ds:0x92]		; INT 24h segment
  3982 00001B56 26A31400                	mov	[es:0x14], ax
  3983 00001B5A 1F                      	pop	ds
  3984                                  
  3985                                  	; PSP:16 — Parent PSP segment (shell's own segment)
  3986 00001B5B 26C70616000008          	mov	word [es:0x16], SHELL_SEG
  3987                                  
  3988                                  	; PSP:18 — File handle table (20 bytes)
  3989 00001B62 26C606180001            	mov	byte [es:0x18], 0x01	; stdin
  3990 00001B68 26C606190001            	mov	byte [es:0x19], 0x01	; stdout
  3991 00001B6E 26C6061A0001            	mov	byte [es:0x1A], 0x01	; stderr
  3992 00001B74 26C6061B0000            	mov	byte [es:0x1B], 0x00	; stdaux
  3993 00001B7A 26C6061C0002            	mov	byte [es:0x1C], 0x02	; stdprn
  3994                                  	; Handles 5-19 already zeroed (closed)
  3995                                  
  3996                                  	; PSP:2C — Environment segment
  3997 00001B80 A1[2D3E]                	mov	ax, [env_seg]
  3998 00001B83 26A32C00                	mov	[es:0x2C], ax
  3999                                  
  4000                                  	; PSP:32 — Max file handles
  4001 00001B87 26C70632001400          	mov	word [es:0x32], 20
  4002                                  	; PSP:34 — Pointer to handle table (default: PSP:18)
  4003 00001B8E 26C70634001800          	mov	word [es:0x34], 0x18
  4004 00001B95 A1[1C3E]                	mov	ax, [exec_seg]
  4005 00001B98 26A33600                	mov	word [es:0x36], ax
  4006                                  
  4007                                  	; PSP:50 — INT 21h / RETF (for CP/M-style CALL PSP:50)
  4008 00001B9C 26C6065000CD            	mov	byte [es:0x50], 0xCD	; INT
  4009 00001BA2 26C606510021            	mov	byte [es:0x51], 0x21	; 21h
  4010 00001BA8 26C6065200CB            	mov	byte [es:0x52], 0xCB	; RETF
  4011                                  
  4012                                  	; PSP:5C — FCB #1 (parse first arg from command tail)
  4013                                  	; DS:SI = source string (shell seg), ES:DI = FCB in PSP
  4014 00001BAE 56                      	push	si
  4015 00001BAF 57                      	push	di
  4016 00001BB0 8B36[2B3E]              	mov	si, [exec_cmdtail_ptr]
  4017                                  	; DS is already SHELL_SEG, ES is already PSP seg
  4018 00001BB4 BF5C00                  	mov	di, 0x5C
  4019 00001BB7 B80029                  	mov	ax, 0x2900
  4020 00001BBA CD21                    	int	0x21
  4021                                  	; PSP:6C — FCB #2 (parse second arg)
  4022                                  	; SI was advanced past first arg by AH=29
  4023 00001BBC BF6C00                  	mov	di, 0x6C
  4024 00001BBF B80029                  	mov	ax, 0x2900
  4025 00001BC2 CD21                    	int	0x21
  4026 00001BC4 5F                      	pop	di
  4027 00001BC5 5E                      	pop	si
  4028                                  
  4029                                  	; Command tail at PSP:80h
  4030                                  	; Format: [length byte] [space] [arguments...] [0x0D]
  4031 00001BC6 56                      	push	si
  4032 00001BC7 57                      	push	di
  4033 00001BC8 8B36[2B3E]              	mov	si, [exec_cmdtail_ptr]
  4034 00001BCC BF8100                  	mov	di, 0x81		; Start after length byte
  4035 00001BCF 31C9                    	xor	cx, cx			; Count characters
  4036                                  	; Copy command tail
  4037                                  .exec_copy_tail:
  4038 00001BD1 AC                      	lodsb
  4039 00001BD2 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  4040 00001BD4 7409                    	je	.exec_tail_done
  4041 00001BD6 83F97E                  	cmp	cx, 126			; Max 126 chars
  4042 00001BD9 7304                    	jae	.exec_tail_done
  4043 00001BDB AA                      	stosb
  4044 00001BDC 41                      	inc	cx
  4045 00001BDD EBF2                    	jmp	.exec_copy_tail
  4046                                  .exec_tail_done:
  4047 00001BDF 26C6050D                	mov	byte [es:di], 0x0D	; Terminate with CR
  4048 00001BE3 26880E8000              	mov	byte [es:0x80], cl	; Length byte
  4049 00001BE8 5F                      	pop	di
  4050 00001BE9 5E                      	pop	si
  4051                                  
  4052                                  	; Set default DTA to PSP:0080
  4053 00001BEA A1[1C3E]                	mov	ax, [exec_seg]
  4054 00001BED A3[6C3E]                	mov	[dta_seg], ax
  4055 00001BF0 C706[6E3E]8000          	mov	word [dta_off], 0x0080
  4056                                  
  4057                                  	; Load file to allocated_seg:0100
  4058                                  	; Advance ES by cluster size each iteration to avoid 64K crossing
  4059 00001BF6 BB0001                  	mov	bx, 0x0100
  4060 00001BF9 A1[163E]                	mov	ax, [exec_cluster]
  4061                                  
  4062                                  .load_cluster:
  4063 00001BFC 50                      	push	ax
  4064 00001BFD E8D2F1                  	call	cluster_to_chs
  4065 00001C00 06                      	push	es
  4066 00001C01 B402                    	mov	ah, 0x02
  4067 00001C03 B002                    	mov	al, SECS_PER_CLUST
  4068 00001C05 8A16[0D3E]              	mov	dl, [resolved_drive]
  4069 00001C09 CD13                    	int	0x13
  4070 00001C0B 07                      	pop	es
  4071 00001C0C 7303E9D800              	jc	.exec_disk_err_free
  4072                                  
  4073                                  	; Advance ES by cluster size (avoids 64K boundary crossing)
  4074 00001C11 8CC0                    	mov	ax, es
  4075 00001C13 83C040                  	add	ax, SECS_PER_CLUST * 512 / 16
  4076 00001C16 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  4077                                  	; BX stays at same offset within each 1K window
  4078                                  
  4079 00001C18 58                      	pop	ax
  4080 00001C19 E8DF00                  	call	fat12_next_cluster
  4081 00001C1C 3DF80F                  	cmp	ax, 0xFF8
  4082 00001C1F 72DB                    	jb	.load_cluster
  4083                                  
  4084                                  	; Check if .EXE by looking at first two bytes (MZ signature)
  4085 00001C21 A1[1C3E]                	mov	ax, [exec_seg]
  4086 00001C24 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  4087 00001C26 26813E00014D5A          	cmp	word [es:0x100], 0x5A4D	; 'MZ'
  4088 00001C2D 7435                    	je	.exec_is_exe
  4089                                  
  4090                                  	; === .COM execution ===
  4091                                  	; Set up far jump target BEFORE changing DS
  4092 00001C2F C706[263E]0001          	mov	word [exec_jmp_ip], 0x0100	; Reset (EXE may have changed it)
  4093 00001C35 A1[1C3E]                	mov	ax, [exec_seg]
  4094 00001C38 A3[283E]                	mov	[exec_jmp_cs], ax
  4095                                  
  4096                                  	; Update INT 20h to return to shell
  4097 00001C3B 50                      	push	ax
  4098 00001C3C 31C0                    	xor	ax, ax
  4099 00001C3E 06                      	push	es
  4100 00001C3F 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  4101 00001C41 26C7068000[5338]        	mov	word [es:0x80], int20_handler
  4102 00001C48 26C70682000008          	mov	word [es:0x82], SHELL_SEG
  4103 00001C4F 07                      	pop	es
  4104 00001C50 58                      	pop	ax
  4105                                  
  4106                                  	; Now set up program segments
  4107 00001C51 A1[1C3E]                	mov	ax, [exec_seg]
  4108 00001C54 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  4109 00001C56 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  4110 00001C58 FA                      	cli
  4111 00001C59 8ED0                    	mov	ss, ax
  4112 00001C5B BCFEFF                  	mov	sp, 0xFFFE
  4113 00001C5E FB                      	sti
  4114                                  
  4115                                  	; Jump to program
  4116 00001C5F 2EFF2E[263E]            	jmp	far [cs:exec_jmp_ip]
  4117                                  
  4118                                  	; === .EXE execution ===
  4119                                  .exec_is_exe:
  4120                                  	; Read MZ header from exec_seg:0100
  4121 00001C64 A1[1C3E]                	mov	ax, [exec_seg]
  4122 00001C67 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  4123                                  
  4124                                  	; Header size in paragraphs (at file offset 0x08 → memory 0x108)
  4125 00001C69 26A10801                	mov	ax, [es:0x108]
  4126 00001C6D A3[223E]                	mov	[exe_hdr_size], ax
  4127                                  
  4128                                  	; Code segment = exec_seg + 0x10 (PSP) + header_paras
  4129 00001C70 8B1E[1C3E]              	mov	bx, [exec_seg]
  4130 00001C74 83C310                  	add	bx, 0x10		; Past PSP
  4131 00001C77 01C3                    	add	bx, ax			; Past MZ header
  4132 00001C79 891E[243E]              	mov	[exe_load_seg], bx
  4133                                  
  4134                                  	; Get initial CS:IP from header
  4135 00001C7D 26A11601                	mov	ax, [es:0x116]		; Initial CS (relative)
  4136 00001C81 01D8                    	add	ax, bx			; Make absolute
  4137 00001C83 A3[283E]                	mov	[exec_jmp_cs], ax	; CS for far jump
  4138                                  
  4139 00001C86 26A11401                	mov	ax, [es:0x114]		; Initial IP
  4140 00001C8A A3[263E]                	mov	[exec_jmp_ip], ax	; IP for far jump
  4141                                  
  4142                                  	; Get initial SS:SP from header
  4143 00001C8D 26A10E01                	mov	ax, [es:0x10E]		; Initial SS (relative)
  4144 00001C91 01D8                    	add	ax, bx			; Make absolute
  4145 00001C93 268B161001              	mov	dx, [es:0x110]		; Initial SP
  4146                                  
  4147                                  	; Apply relocations
  4148 00001C98 268B0E0601              	mov	cx, [es:0x106]		; Relocation count
  4149 00001C9D E32F                    	jcxz	.exec_exe_no_reloc
  4150 00001C9F 268B3E1801              	mov	di, [es:0x118]		; Relocation table file offset
  4151 00001CA4 81C70001                	add	di, 0x100		; Adjust for load at :0100
  4152                                  
  4153                                  .exec_exe_reloc:
  4154 00001CA8 51                      	push	cx
  4155 00001CA9 268B35                  	mov	si, [es:di]		; Reloc offset
  4156 00001CAC 268B4D02                	mov	cx, [es:di+2]		; Reloc segment (relative)
  4157 00001CB0 030E[243E]              	add	cx, [exe_load_seg]	; Make absolute
  4158 00001CB4 06                      	push	es
  4159 00001CB5 57                      	push	di
  4160 00001CB6 8EC1                    	mov	es, cx
  4161 00001CB8 89F7                    	mov	di, si
  4162 00001CBA 268B0D                  	mov	cx, [es:di]		; Read current value
  4163 00001CBD 2E030E[243E]            	add	cx, [cs:exe_load_seg]	; Add load segment
  4164 00001CC2 26890D                  	mov	[es:di], cx		; Write back
  4165 00001CC5 5F                      	pop	di
  4166 00001CC6 07                      	pop	es
  4167 00001CC7 59                      	pop	cx
  4168 00001CC8 83C704                  	add	di, 4
  4169 00001CCB 49                      	dec	cx
  4170 00001CCC 75DA                    	jnz	.exec_exe_reloc
  4171                                  
  4172                                  .exec_exe_no_reloc:
  4173                                  	; Set up execution
  4174 00001CCE FA                      	cli
  4175 00001CCF 8ED0                    	mov	ss, ax			; SS from header
  4176 00001CD1 89D4                    	mov	sp, dx			; SP from header
  4177 00001CD3 FB                      	sti
  4178                                  
  4179                                  	; DS = ES = PSP segment (standard DOS .EXE convention)
  4180 00001CD4 A1[1C3E]                	mov	ax, [exec_seg]
  4181 00001CD7 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  4182 00001CD9 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  4183                                  
  4184                                  	; Far jump to CS:IP
  4185 00001CDB 2EFF2E[263E]            	jmp	far [cs:exec_jmp_ip]
  4186                                  
  4187                                  .exec_no_mem:
  4188 00001CE0 BE[2F3A]                	mov	si, msg_no_mem
  4189 00001CE3 E8DC1B                  	call	print_string
  4190 00001CE6 E9E2E3                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  4191                                  
  4192                                  .exec_disk_err_free:
  4193 00001CE9 58                      	pop	ax			; Clean stack from push in load_cluster
  4194                                  	; Free allocated memory
  4195 00001CEA 8E06[1C3E]              	mov	es, [exec_seg]
  4196 00001CEE B449                    	mov	ah, 0x49
  4197 00001CF0 CD21                    	int	0x21
  4198                                  
  4199                                  .exec_disk_err:
  4200 00001CF2 BE[853A]                	mov	si, msg_disk_err
  4201 00001CF5 E8CA1B                  	call	print_string
  4202 00001CF8 E9D0E3                  	jmp	cmd_loop
  4203                                  
  4204                                  ; ============================================================================
  4205                                  ; fat12_next_cluster — Get next cluster from FAT12
  4206                                  ; ============================================================================
  4207                                  ; Input:  AX = current cluster
  4208                                  ; Output: AX = next cluster (>= 0xFF8 means end)
  4209                                  fat12_next_cluster:
  4210 00001CFB 53                      	push	bx
  4211 00001CFC 51                      	push	cx
  4212 00001CFD 52                      	push	dx
  4213                                  
  4214 00001CFE 89C2                    	mov	dx, ax			; Save cluster number for odd/even test
  4215 00001D00 89C3                    	mov	bx, ax
  4216                                  	; FAT12 entry offset = cluster * 1.5 = cluster + cluster/2
  4217 00001D02 89C1                    	mov	cx, ax
  4218 00001D04 D1E9                    	shr	cx, 1
  4219 00001D06 01CB                    	add	bx, cx			; BX = byte offset into FAT
  4220                                  
  4221                                  	; Read 16-bit value from FAT buffer
  4222 00001D08 1E                      	push	ds
  4223 00001D09 B90008                  	mov	cx, SHELL_SEG
  4224 00001D0C 8ED9                    	mov	ds, cx
  4225 00001D0E 8B87004E                	mov	ax, [fat_buffer + bx]
  4226 00001D12 1F                      	pop	ds
  4227                                  
  4228                                  	; If original cluster was odd, shift right 4
  4229 00001D13 F7C20100                	test	dx, 1			; Was original cluster odd?
  4230 00001D17 7406                    	jz	.even_cluster
  4231 00001D19 B104                    	mov	cl, 4
  4232 00001D1B D3E8                    	shr	ax, cl
  4233 00001D1D EB03                    	jmp	.fat_done
  4234                                  .even_cluster:
  4235 00001D1F 25FF0F                  	and	ax, 0x0FFF
  4236                                  .fat_done:
  4237 00001D22 5A                      	pop	dx
  4238 00001D23 59                      	pop	cx
  4239 00001D24 5B                      	pop	bx
  4240 00001D25 C3                      	ret
  4241                                  
  4242                                  ; ============================================================================
  4243                                  ; INT 21h — DOS Services Handler
  4244                                  ; ============================================================================
  4245                                  ; Provides basic DOS-compatible services for .COM programs.
  4246                                  ;
  4247                                  int21_handler:
  4248 00001D26 80FC01                  	cmp	ah, 0x01
  4249 00001D29 7503E91D02              	je	.i21_01
  4250 00001D2E 80FC02                  	cmp	ah, 0x02
  4251 00001D31 7503E92002              	je	.i21_02

  4279 00001DA1 7503E91706              	je	.i21_3f

  4407                                  ; --- AH=01: Read character with echo ---
  4408                                  .i21_01:

  4414 00001F54 58                      	pop	ax

  4429                                  ; --- AH=06: Direct console I/O ---
  4430                                  ; DL=FF: input (ZF=1 if no char, AL=char if available)
  4431                                  ; DL<FF: output character DL

  4444 00001F76 CF                      	iret

  4446 00001F77 B401                    	mov	ah, 0x01

  4449 00001F7D B400                    	mov	ah, 0x00
  4450 00001F7F CD16                    	int	0x16		; Get key
  4451 00001F81 08C0                    	or	al, al		; Clear ZF (char available)
  4452 00001F83 CF                      	iret

  4455 00001F86 CF                      	iret

  4457                                  ; --- AH=07: Direct char input without echo ---

  4460 00001F89 CD16                    	int	0x16
  4461 00001F8B CF                      	iret
  4462                                  
  4463                                  ; --- AH=08: Read char without echo (checks Ctrl-C) ---
  4464                                  .i21_08:

  4466 00001F8E CD16                    	int	0x16
  4467 00001F90 CF                      	iret
  4468                                  
  4469                                  ; --- AH=09: Print $-terminated string at DS:DX ---
  4470                                  .i21_09:

  4475                                  .i21_09_loop:

  4485 00001FA5 5B                      	pop	bx
  4486 00001FA6 58                      	pop	ax
  4487 00001FA7 CF                      	iret
  4488                                  
  4489                                  ; --- AH=0A: Buffered input ---
  4490                                  ; DS:DX points to buffer: [max_len] [actual_len] [data...]
  4491                                  .i21_0a:

  4493 00001FA9 53                      	push	bx
  4494 00001FAA 51                      	push	cx
  4495 00001FAB 57                      	push	di

  4497 00001FAE 8A0D                    	mov	cl, [di]	; Max length
  4498 00001FB0 30ED                    	xor	ch, ch
  4499 00001FB2 49                      	dec	cx		; Leave room for CR
  4500 00001FB3 83C702                  	add	di, 2		; Point to data area
  4501 00001FB6 31DB                    	xor	bx, bx		; Character count
  4502                                  .i21_0a_loop:
  4503 00001FB8 B400                    	mov	ah, 0x00
  4504 00001FBA CD16                    	int	0x16		; Read key
  4505 00001FBC 3C0D                    	cmp	al, 0x0D	; Enter?
  4506 00001FBE 742B                    	je	.i21_0a_done
  4507 00001FC0 3C08                    	cmp	al, 0x08	; Backspace?
  4508 00001FC2 740D                    	je	.i21_0a_bs
  4509 00001FC4 39CB                    	cmp	bx, cx		; Buffer full?
  4510 00001FC6 7DF0                    	jge	.i21_0a_loop

  4512 00001FCA 43                      	inc	bx
  4513                                  	; Echo
  4514 00001FCB B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  4515 00001FCD CD10                    	int	0x10
  4516 00001FCF EBE7                    	jmp	.i21_0a_loop

  4518 00001FD1 83FB00                  	cmp	bx, 0
  4519 00001FD4 74E2                    	je	.i21_0a_loop

  4521 00001FD7 B008                    	mov	al, 0x08
  4522 00001FD9 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E

  4524 00001FDD B020                    	mov	al, ' '
  4525 00001FDF B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E

  4527 00001FE3 B008                    	mov	al, 0x08

  4535                                  	; Echo CR/LF
  4536 00001FF3 B00D                    	mov	al, 0x0D

  4544 00002001 5B                      	pop	bx
  4545 00002002 58                      	pop	ax
  4546 00002003 CF                      	iret
  4547                                  
  4548                                  ; --- AH=0B: Check input status ---
  4549                                  ; Returns AL=FF if char available, AL=00 if not
  4550                                  .i21_0b:
  4551 00002004 B401                    	mov	ah, 0x01
  4552 00002006 CD16                    	int	0x16
  4553 00002008 7403                    	jz	.i21_0b_none

  4557 0000200D 30C0                    	xor	al, al
  4558 0000200F CF                      	iret
  4559                                  
  4560                                  ; --- AH=0C: Flush buffer then read ---
  4561                                  ; AL = function to call after flush (01, 06, 07, 08, 0A)
  4562                                  .i21_0c:
  4563                                  	; We don't have a buffer to flush — just dispatch
  4564 00002010 88C4                    	mov	ah, al
  4565 00002012 CD21                    	int	0x21
  4566 00002014 CF                      	iret
  4567                                  
  4568                                  ; --- AH=25: Set interrupt vector ---
  4569                                  ; AL = interrupt number, DS:DX = new handler
  4570                                  .i21_25:
  4571 00002015 50                      	push	ax
  4572 00002016 53                      	push	bx
  4573 00002017 06                      	push	es
  4574 00002018 31DB                    	xor	bx, bx
  4575 0000201A 8EC3                    	mov	es, bx
  4576 0000201C 30FF                    	xor	bh, bh
  4577 0000201E 88C3                    	mov	bl, al
  4578 00002020 D1E3                    	shl	bx, 1
  4579 00002022 D1E3                    	shl	bx, 1		; BX = AL * 4
  4580 00002024 268917                  	mov	[es:bx], dx	; Offset
  4581 00002027 268C5F02                	mov	[es:bx+2], ds	; Segment
  4582 0000202B 07                      	pop	es
  4583 0000202C 5B                      	pop	bx
  4584 0000202D 58                      	pop	ax
  4585 0000202E CF                      	iret
  4586                                  
  4587                                  ; --- AH=30: Get DOS version ---
  4588                                  ; Returns AL=major, AH=minor
  4589                                  .i21_30:
  4590 0000202F B80300                  	mov	ax, 0x0003	; DOS 3.0
  4591 00002032 31DB                    	xor	bx, bx
  4592 00002034 31C9                    	xor	cx, cx
  4593 00002036 CF                      	iret
  4594                                  
  4595                                  ; --- AH=35: Get interrupt vector ---
  4596                                  ; AL = interrupt number → ES:BX = handler address
  4597                                  .i21_35:
  4598 00002037 50                      	push	ax
  4599 00002038 1E                      	push	ds
  4600 00002039 31DB                    	xor	bx, bx
  4601 0000203B 8EDB                    	mov	ds, bx
  4602 0000203D 30FF                    	xor	bh, bh
  4603 0000203F 88C3                    	mov	bl, al

  4605 00002043 D1E3                    	shl	bx, 1		; BX = AL * 4
  4606 00002045 8B4702                  	mov	ax, [bx+2]	; Segment
  4607 00002048 8B1F                    	mov	bx, [bx]	; Offset

  4609 0000204C 1F                      	pop	ds
  4610 0000204D 58                      	pop	ax
  4611 0000204E CF                      	iret
  4612                                  
  4613                                  ; --- AH=3C: Create file ---
  4614                                  ; Input: DS:DX = ASCIIZ filename, CX = attributes
  4615                                  ; Output: AX = handle, CF=0 on success
  4616                                  .i21_3c:
  4617 0000204F 53                      	push	bx
  4618 00002050 51                      	push	cx
  4619 00002051 56                      	push	si
  4620 00002052 57                      	push	di
  4621 00002053 06                      	push	es
  4622                                  
  4623 00002054 2E890E[0022]            	mov	[cs:.i21_3c_attr], cx
  4624                                  
  4625                                  	; Find a free handle (start at 5)
  4626 00002059 BB0500                  	mov	bx, 5
  4627                                  .i21_3c_find_handle:
  4628 0000205C 83FB08                  	cmp	bx, MAX_HANDLES
  4629 0000205F 7203E97901              	jae	.i21_3c_no_handle
  4630 00002064 89D8                    	mov	ax, bx
  4631 00002066 53                      	push	bx
  4632 00002067 51                      	push	cx
  4633 00002068 B104                    	mov	cl, 4
  4634 0000206A D3E3                    	shl	bx, cl
  4635 0000206C 2E80BF[703E]00          	cmp	byte [cs:file_handles + bx], 0
  4636 00002072 59                      	pop	cx
  4637 00002073 5B                      	pop	bx
  4638 00002074 7403                    	je	.i21_3c_got_handle
  4639 00002076 43                      	inc	bx
  4640 00002077 EBE3                    	jmp	.i21_3c_find_handle
  4641                                  .i21_3c_got_handle:
  4642 00002079 2E891E[0222]            	mov	[cs:.i21_3c_handle], bx
  4643                                  
  4644                                  	; Copy filename from caller's DS:DX to cmd_buffer
  4645 0000207E 2E8C1E[0422]            	mov	[cs:.i21_3c_ds], ds
  4646 00002083 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  4647 00002086 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  4648 00002088 BF[9F3C]                	mov	di, cmd_buffer
  4649 0000208B 89D6                    	mov	si, dx
  4650 0000208D B94000                  	mov	cx, 64
  4651                                  .i21_3c_copy:
  4652 00002090 AC                      	lodsb
  4653 00002091 268805                  	mov	[es:di], al
  4654 00002094 47                      	inc	di
  4655 00002095 08C0                    	or	al, al
  4656 00002097 7408                    	jz	.i21_3c_copied
  4657 00002099 49                      	dec	cx
  4658 0000209A 75F4                    	jnz	.i21_3c_copy
  4659 0000209C 26C645FF00              	mov	byte [es:di-1], 0
  4660                                  .i21_3c_copied:
  4661                                  
  4662                                  	; Switch to SHELL_SEG
  4663 000020A1 2E8E1E[0422]            	mov	ds, [cs:.i21_3c_ds]	; Keep caller's DS for now
  4664 000020A6 1E                      	push	ds
  4665 000020A7 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  4666 000020AA 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  4667                                  
  4668                                  	; Resolve path
  4669 000020AC BE[9F3C]                	mov	si, cmd_buffer
  4670 000020AF E892F3                  	call	resolve_path
  4671 000020B2 7303E93701              	jc	.i21_3c_err_pop
  4672                                  
  4673                                  	; Read resolved directory
  4674 000020B7 E8A7F4                  	call	read_resolved_dir
  4675 000020BA 7303E92F01              	jc	.i21_3c_err_pop
  4676                                  
  4677                                  	; Check if file already exists — if so, truncate (overwrite)
  4678 000020BF BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  4679 000020C2 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  4680                                  .i21_3c_check:
  4681 000020C6 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  4682 000020C8 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  4683 000020CA 741B                    	je	.i21_3c_not_exists
  4684 000020CC 3CE5                    	cmp	al, 0xE5
  4685 000020CE 7411                    	je	.i21_3c_check_next
  4686 000020D0 51                      	push	cx
  4687 000020D1 56                      	push	si
  4688 000020D2 BF[F03C]                	mov	di, exec_fname
  4689 000020D5 B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  4690 000020D8 F3A6                    	repe	cmpsb
  4691 000020DA 5E                      	pop	si
  4692 000020DB 59                      	pop	cx
  4693 000020DC 7503E98600              	je	.i21_3c_exists
  4694                                  .i21_3c_check_next:
  4695 000020E1 83C620                  	add	si, 32
  4696 000020E4 49                      	dec	cx
  4697 000020E5 75DF                    	jnz	.i21_3c_check
  4698                                  
  4699                                  .i21_3c_not_exists:
  4700                                  	; Find a free directory entry
  4701 000020E7 BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  4702 000020EA 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  4703                                  .i21_3c_find_free:
  4704 000020EE 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  4705 000020F0 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  4706 000020F2 740D                    	je	.i21_3c_free_found
  4707 000020F4 3CE5                    	cmp	al, 0xE5
  4708 000020F6 7409                    	je	.i21_3c_free_found
  4709 000020F8 83C620                  	add	si, 32
  4710 000020FB 49                      	dec	cx
  4711 000020FC 75F0                    	jnz	.i21_3c_find_free
  4712 000020FE E9EE00                  	jmp	.i21_3c_dir_full
  4713                                  
  4714                                  .i21_3c_free_found:
  4715                                  	; Allocate a cluster for the file
  4716 00002101 E8F9F2                  	call	read_fat
  4717 00002104 7303E9E500              	jc	.i21_3c_err_pop
  4718 00002109 B80200                  	mov	ax, 2
  4719                                  .i21_3c_find_cl:
  4720 0000210C 3DD002                  	cmp	ax, 720
  4721 0000210F 7203E9DB00              	jae	.i21_3c_disk_full
  4722 00002114 50                      	push	ax
  4723 00002115 E8E0EC                  	call	fat12_read_cluster
  4724 00002118 83F800                  	cmp	ax, 0
  4725 0000211B 58                      	pop	ax
  4726 0000211C 7403                    	je	.i21_3c_got_cl
  4727 0000211E 40                      	inc	ax
  4728 0000211F EBEB                    	jmp	.i21_3c_find_cl
  4729                                  .i21_3c_got_cl:
  4730 00002121 2EA3[0622]              	mov	[cs:.i21_3c_cluster], ax
  4731                                  	; Mark cluster as EOF
  4732 00002125 BBFF0F                  	mov	bx, 0xFFF
  4733 00002128 E8F8EC                  	call	fat12_write_cluster
  4734 0000212B E8E8F2                  	call	write_fat
  4735 0000212E 7303E9BB00              	jc	.i21_3c_err_pop
  4736                                  
  4737                                  	; Create directory entry
  4738                                  	; SI still points to the free slot
  4739 00002133 89F7                    	mov	di, si
  4740 00002135 BE[F03C]                	mov	si, exec_fname
  4741 00002138 B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  4742 0000213B F3A4                    	rep	movsb			; Filename
  4743 0000213D 2EA1[0022]              	mov	ax, [cs:.i21_3c_attr]
  4744 00002141 8805                    	mov	byte [di], al		; Attribute
  4745 00002143 47                      	inc	di
  4746 00002144 B90E00                  	mov	cx, 14
  4747 00002147 30C0                    	xor	al, al
  4748 00002149 F3AA                    	rep	stosb			; Zero times/dates
  4749 0000214B 2EA1[0622]              	mov	ax, [cs:.i21_3c_cluster]
  4750 0000214F 8905                    	mov	[di], ax		; Starting cluster
  4751 00002151 83C702                  	add	di, 2
  4752 00002154 31C0                    	xor	ax, ax
  4753 00002156 8905                    	mov	[di], ax		; File size = 0
  4754 00002158 83C702                  	add	di, 2
  4755 0000215B 8905                    	mov	[di], ax
  4756                                  
  4757                                  	; Write directory back
  4758 0000215D E83AF4                  	call	write_resolved_dir
  4759 00002160 7303E98900              	jc	.i21_3c_err_pop
  4760 00002165 EB16                    	jmp	.i21_3c_setup_handle
  4761                                  
  4762                                  .i21_3c_exists:
  4763                                  	; File exists — truncate to 0 (reuse its cluster)
  4764 00002167 8B441A                  	mov	ax, [si+26]		; Existing start cluster
  4765 0000216A 2EA3[0622]              	mov	[cs:.i21_3c_cluster], ax
  4766                                  	; Set file size to 0
  4767 0000216E C7441C0000              	mov	word [si+28], 0
  4768 00002173 C7441E0000              	mov	word [si+30], 0
  4769 00002178 E81FF4                  	call	write_resolved_dir
  4770 0000217B 7271                    	jc	.i21_3c_err_pop
  4771                                  
  4772                                  .i21_3c_setup_handle:
  4773                                  	; Fill handle entry
  4774 0000217D 2E8B1E[0222]            	mov	bx, [cs:.i21_3c_handle]
  4775 00002182 89D8                    	mov	ax, bx
  4776 00002184 B104                    	mov	cl, 4
  4777 00002186 D3E0                    	shl	ax, cl
  4778 00002188 89C7                    	mov	di, ax
  4779                                  
  4780 0000218A 2EC685[703E]02          	mov	byte [cs:file_handles + di], 2	; Open for write
  4781 00002190 2EA0[0D3E]              	mov	al, [cs:resolved_drive]
  4782 00002194 2E8885[713E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + di + 1], al
  4783 00002199 2EA1[0622]              	mov	ax, [cs:.i21_3c_cluster]
  4784 0000219D 2E8985[723E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + di + 2], ax	; Start cluster
  4785 000021A2 2E8985[743E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + di + 4], ax	; Current cluster
  4786 000021A7 2EC785[763E]0000        	mov	word [cs:file_handles + di + 6], 0  ; Cluster position
  4787 000021AE 2EC785[783E]0000        	mov	word [cs:file_handles + di + 8], 0  ; File pointer
  4788 000021B5 2EC785[7A3E]0000        	mov	word [cs:file_handles + di + 10], 0
  4789 000021BC 2EC785[7C3E]0000        	mov	word [cs:file_handles + di + 12], 0 ; File size = 0
  4790 000021C3 2EC785[7E3E]0000        	mov	word [cs:file_handles + di + 14], 0
  4791                                  
  4792 000021CA 1F                      	pop	ds			; Restore caller's DS
  4793 000021CB 2EA1[0222]              	mov	ax, [cs:.i21_3c_handle]
  4794 000021CF 07                      	pop	es
  4795 000021D0 5F                      	pop	di
  4796 000021D1 5E                      	pop	si
  4797 000021D2 59                      	pop	cx
  4798 000021D3 5B                      	pop	bx
  4799 000021D4 55                      	push	bp
  4800 000021D5 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  4801 000021D7 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE
  4802 000021DB 5D                      	pop	bp
  4803 000021DC CF                      	iret
  4804                                  
  4805                                  .i21_3c_no_handle:
  4806 000021DD B80400                  	mov	ax, 4
  4807 000021E0 07                      	pop	es
  4808 000021E1 5F                      	pop	di
  4809 000021E2 5E                      	pop	si
  4810 000021E3 59                      	pop	cx
  4811 000021E4 5B                      	pop	bx
  4812 000021E5 55                      	push	bp
  4813 000021E6 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  4814 000021E8 834E0601                	or	word [bp+6], 0x0001
  4815 000021EC 5D                      	pop	bp
  4816 000021ED CF                      	iret
  4817                                  
  4818                                  .i21_3c_err_pop:
  4819 000021EE 1F                      	pop	ds
  4820                                  .i21_3c_disk_full:
  4821                                  .i21_3c_dir_full:
  4822 000021EF 07                      	pop	es
  4823 000021F0 5F                      	pop	di
  4824 000021F1 5E                      	pop	si
  4825 000021F2 59                      	pop	cx
  4826 000021F3 5B                      	pop	bx
  4827 000021F4 B80500                  	mov	ax, 5
  4828 000021F7 55                      	push	bp
  4829 000021F8 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  4830 000021FA 834E0601                	or	word [bp+6], 0x0001
  4831 000021FE 5D                      	pop	bp
  4832 000021FF CF                      	iret
  4833                                  
  4834 00002200 0000                    .i21_3c_attr	dw	0
  4835 00002202 0000                    .i21_3c_handle	dw	0
  4836 00002204 0000                    .i21_3c_ds	dw	0
  4837 00002206 0000                    .i21_3c_cluster	dw	0
  4838                                  
  4839                                  ; --- AH=3D: Open file ---
  4840                                  ; Input: DS:DX = ASCIIZ filename, AL = access mode (0=read, 1=write, 2=r/w)
  4841                                  ; Output: AX = handle, CF=0 on success
  4842                                  .i21_3d:
  4843 00002208 53                      	push	bx
  4844 00002209 51                      	push	cx
  4845 0000220A 56                      	push	si
  4846 0000220B 57                      	push	di
  4847 0000220C 06                      	push	es
  4848                                  
  4849 0000220D 2EA2[0F23]              	mov	[cs:.i21_3d_mode], al	; Save access mode
  4850                                  
  4851                                  	; Find a free handle (start at 5)
  4852 00002211 BB0500                  	mov	bx, 5
  4853                                  .i21_3d_find_handle:
  4854 00002214 83FB08                  	cmp	bx, MAX_HANDLES
  4855 00002217 7203E9F800              	jae	.i21_3d_no_handle
  4856 0000221C 89D8                    	mov	ax, bx
  4857 0000221E 53                      	push	bx
  4858 0000221F B104                    	mov	cl, 4			; * 16 = FH_SIZE
  4859 00002221 D3E3                    	shl	bx, cl
  4860 00002223 2E80BF[703E]00          	cmp	byte [cs:file_handles + bx], 0	; Closed?
  4861 00002229 5B                      	pop	bx
  4862 0000222A 7403                    	je	.i21_3d_got_handle
  4863 0000222C 43                      	inc	bx
  4864 0000222D EBE5                    	jmp	.i21_3d_find_handle
  4865                                  
  4866                                  .i21_3d_got_handle:
  4867 0000222F 2E891E[1023]            	mov	[cs:.i21_3d_handle], bx
  4868                                  
  4869                                  	; Parse filename from DS:DX using resolve_path
  4870                                  	; Save DS (caller's segment)
  4871 00002234 2E8C1E[1223]            	mov	[cs:.i21_3d_ds], ds
  4872 00002239 53                      	push	bx
  4873                                  
  4874                                  	; Set DS to SHELL_SEG for resolve_path
  4875 0000223A B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  4876 0000223D 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  4877                                  
  4878                                  	; Copy filename from caller's DS:DX to cmd_buffer
  4879 0000223F 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax			; ES = SHELL_SEG
  4880 00002241 BF[9F3C]                	mov	di, cmd_buffer
  4881 00002244 1E                      	push	ds
  4882 00002245 2E8E1E[1223]            	mov	ds, [cs:.i21_3d_ds]
  4883 0000224A 89D6                    	mov	si, dx
  4884 0000224C B94000                  	mov	cx, 64
  4885                                  .i21_3d_copy_name:
  4886 0000224F AC                      	lodsb
  4887 00002250 AA                      	stosb
  4888 00002251 08C0                    	or	al, al
  4889 00002253 7408                    	jz	.i21_3d_name_done
  4890 00002255 49                      	dec	cx
  4891 00002256 75F7                    	jnz	.i21_3d_copy_name
  4892 00002258 26C645FF00              	mov	byte [es:di-1], 0
  4893                                  .i21_3d_name_done:
  4894 0000225D 1F                      	pop	ds			; DS = SHELL_SEG again
  4895                                  
  4896 0000225E BE[9F3C]                	mov	si, cmd_buffer
  4897 00002261 E8E0F1                  	call	resolve_path
  4898 00002264 722A                    	jc	.i21_3d_not_found
  4899                                  
  4900                                  	; Read directory
  4901 00002266 E8F8F2                  	call	read_resolved_dir
  4902 00002269 7225                    	jc	.i21_3d_not_found
  4903                                  
  4904                                  	; Search for file
  4905 0000226B BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  4906 0000226E 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  4907                                  .i21_3d_search:
  4908 00002272 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  4909 00002274 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  4910 00002276 7418                    	je	.i21_3d_not_found
  4911 00002278 3CE5                    	cmp	al, 0xE5
  4912 0000227A 740E                    	je	.i21_3d_search_next
  4913 0000227C 51                      	push	cx
  4914 0000227D 56                      	push	si
  4915 0000227E BF[F03C]                	mov	di, exec_fname
  4916 00002281 B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  4917 00002284 F3A6                    	repe	cmpsb
  4918 00002286 5E                      	pop	si
  4919 00002287 59                      	pop	cx
  4920 00002288 741D                    	je	.i21_3d_found
  4921                                  .i21_3d_search_next:
  4922 0000228A 83C620                  	add	si, 32
  4923 0000228D 49                      	dec	cx
  4924 0000228E 75E2                    	jnz	.i21_3d_search
  4925                                  
  4926                                  .i21_3d_not_found:
  4927 00002290 5B                      	pop	bx
  4928 00002291 2E8E1E[1223]            	mov	ds, [cs:.i21_3d_ds]
  4929 00002296 07                      	pop	es
  4930 00002297 5F                      	pop	di
  4931 00002298 5E                      	pop	si
  4932 00002299 59                      	pop	cx
  4933 0000229A 5B                      	pop	bx
  4934 0000229B B80200                  	mov	ax, 2			; File not found
  4935 0000229E 55                      	push	bp
  4936 0000229F 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  4937 000022A1 834E0601                	or	word [bp+6], 0x0001
  4938 000022A5 5D                      	pop	bp
  4939 000022A6 CF                      	iret
  4940                                  
  4941                                  .i21_3d_found:
  4942                                  	; Fill handle entry
  4943 000022A7 5B                      	pop	bx			; Handle number
  4944 000022A8 53                      	push	bx
  4945 000022A9 89D8                    	mov	ax, bx
  4946 000022AB B104                    	mov	cl, 4
  4947 000022AD D3E0                    	shl	ax, cl
  4948 000022AF 89C7                    	mov	di, ax			; DI = handle table offset
  4949                                  
  4950                                  	; Flags
  4951 000022B1 2EA0[0F23]              	mov	al, [cs:.i21_3d_mode]
  4952 000022B5 FEC0                    	inc	al			; 0→1(read), 1→2(write), 2→3(r/w)
  4953 000022B7 2E8885[703E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + di], al
  4954                                  	; Drive
  4955 000022BC A0[0D3E]                	mov	al, [resolved_drive]
  4956 000022BF 2E8885[713E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + di + 1], al
  4957                                  	; Start cluster
  4958 000022C4 8B441A                  	mov	ax, [si+26]
  4959 000022C7 2E8985[723E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + di + 2], ax
  4960                                  	; Current cluster = start cluster
  4961 000022CC 2E8985[743E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + di + 4], ax
  4962                                  	; Position in cluster = 0
  4963 000022D1 2EC785[763E]0000        	mov	word [cs:file_handles + di + 6], 0
  4964                                  	; File pointer = 0
  4965 000022D8 2EC785[783E]0000        	mov	word [cs:file_handles + di + 8], 0
  4966 000022DF 2EC785[7A3E]0000        	mov	word [cs:file_handles + di + 10], 0
  4967                                  	; File size
  4968 000022E6 8B441C                  	mov	ax, [si+28]
  4969 000022E9 2E8985[7C3E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + di + 12], ax
  4970 000022EE 8B441E                  	mov	ax, [si+30]
  4971 000022F1 2E8985[7E3E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + di + 14], ax
  4972                                  
  4973                                  	; Load FAT (needed for cluster chain traversal)
  4974 000022F6 E804F1                  	call	read_fat
  4975                                  
  4976 000022F9 5B                      	pop	bx			; Handle number
  4977 000022FA 89D8                    	mov	ax, bx			; Return handle in AX
  4978                                  
  4979 000022FC 2E8E1E[1223]            	mov	ds, [cs:.i21_3d_ds]
  4980 00002301 07                      	pop	es
  4981 00002302 5F                      	pop	di
  4982 00002303 5E                      	pop	si
  4983 00002304 59                      	pop	cx
  4984 00002305 5B                      	pop	bx
  4985 00002306 55                      	push	bp
  4986 00002307 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  4987 00002309 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE	; Clear CF
  4988 0000230D 5D                      	pop	bp
  4989 0000230E CF                      	iret
  4990                                  
  4991 0000230F 00                      .i21_3d_mode	db	0
  4992 00002310 0000                    .i21_3d_handle	dw	0
  4993 00002312 0000                    .i21_3d_ds	dw	0
  4994                                  .i21_3d_no_handle:
  4995 00002314 5B                      	pop	bx
  4996 00002315 07                      	pop	es
  4997 00002316 5F                      	pop	di
  4998 00002317 5E                      	pop	si
  4999 00002318 59                      	pop	cx
  5000 00002319 5B                      	pop	bx
  5001 0000231A B80400                  	mov	ax, 4			; Too many open files
  5002 0000231D 55                      	push	bp
  5003 0000231E 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5004 00002320 834E0601                	or	word [bp+6], 0x0001
  5005 00002324 5D                      	pop	bp
  5006 00002325 CF                      	iret
  5007                                  
  5008                                  ; --- AH=3E: Close file ---
  5009                                  ; Input: BX = handle
  5010                                  .i21_3e:
  5011 00002326 83FB08                  	cmp	bx, MAX_HANDLES
  5012 00002329 7203E98300              	jae	.i21_3e_bad
  5013 0000232E 83FB05                  	cmp	bx, 5
  5014 00002331 7275                    	jb	.i21_3e_ok
  5015 00002333 50                      	push	ax
  5016 00002334 51                      	push	cx
  5017 00002335 56                      	push	si
  5018 00002336 57                      	push	di
  5019 00002337 1E                      	push	ds
  5020 00002338 06                      	push	es
  5021                                  
  5022 00002339 89D8                    	mov	ax, bx
  5023 0000233B B104                    	mov	cl, 4
  5024 0000233D D3E0                    	shl	ax, cl
  5025 0000233F 89C6                    	mov	si, ax			; SI = handle offset
  5026                                  
  5027                                  	; Check if file was opened for write — update directory with file size
  5028 00002341 2E80BC[703E]02          	cmp	byte [cs:file_handles + si], 2
  5029 00002347 7253                    	jb	.i21_3e_just_close	; Read-only, no update needed
  5030                                  
  5031                                  	; Read the directory to find and update the file entry
  5032 00002349 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  5033 0000234C 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  5034 0000234E 2E8A84[713E]            	mov	al, [cs:file_handles + si + 1]
  5035 00002353 A2[0D3E]                	mov	[resolved_drive], al
  5036                                  	; For simplicity, re-read root directory and search for the file by cluster
  5037 00002356 C706[093E]0000          	mov	word [resolved_dir_cluster], 0
  5038 0000235C C706[0B3E]7000          	mov	word [resolved_dir_entries], MAX_DIR_ENTRIES
  5039 00002362 E8FCF1                  	call	read_resolved_dir
  5040 00002365 7235                    	jc	.i21_3e_just_close
  5041                                  
  5042                                  	; Search for entry with matching start cluster
  5043 00002367 BF0040                  	mov	di, dir_buffer
  5044 0000236A B97000                  	mov	cx, MAX_DIR_ENTRIES
  5045 0000236D 2E8B84[723E]            	mov	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 2]	; Start cluster
  5046                                  .i21_3e_search:
  5047 00002372 803D00                  	cmp	byte [di], 0
  5048 00002375 7425                    	je	.i21_3e_just_close
  5049 00002377 803DE5                  	cmp	byte [di], 0xE5
  5050 0000237A 7405                    	je	.i21_3e_next
  5051 0000237C 39451A                  	cmp	[di+26], ax
  5052 0000237F 7408                    	je	.i21_3e_found
  5053                                  .i21_3e_next:
  5054 00002381 83C720                  	add	di, 32
  5055 00002384 49                      	dec	cx
  5056 00002385 75EB                    	jnz	.i21_3e_search
  5057 00002387 EB13                    	jmp	.i21_3e_just_close
  5058                                  
  5059                                  .i21_3e_found:
  5060                                  	; Update file size in directory entry from file pointer
  5061 00002389 2E8B84[783E]            	mov	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 8]	; File pointer = actual bytes written
  5062 0000238E 89451C                  	mov	[di+28], ax
  5063 00002391 2E8B84[7A3E]            	mov	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 10]
  5064 00002396 89451E                  	mov	[di+30], ax
  5065 00002399 E8FEF1                  	call	write_resolved_dir
  5066                                  
  5067                                  .i21_3e_just_close:
  5068 0000239C 2EC684[703E]00          	mov	byte [cs:file_handles + si], 0	; Mark closed
  5069                                  
  5070 000023A2 07                      	pop	es
  5071 000023A3 1F                      	pop	ds
  5072 000023A4 5F                      	pop	di
  5073 000023A5 5E                      	pop	si
  5074 000023A6 59                      	pop	cx
  5075 000023A7 58                      	pop	ax
  5076                                  .i21_3e_ok:
  5077 000023A8 55                      	push	bp
  5078 000023A9 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5079 000023AB 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE
  5080 000023AF 5D                      	pop	bp
  5081 000023B0 CF                      	iret
  5082                                  .i21_3e_bad:
  5083 000023B1 B80600                  	mov	ax, 6			; Invalid handle
  5084 000023B4 55                      	push	bp
  5085 000023B5 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5086 000023B7 834E0601                	or	word [bp+6], 0x0001
  5087 000023BB 5D                      	pop	bp
  5088 000023BC CF                      	iret
  5089                                  
  5090                                  ; --- AH=3F: Read from file ---
  5091                                  ; Input: BX = handle, CX = bytes to read, DS:DX = buffer
  5092                                  ; Output: AX = bytes actually read, CF=0
  5093                                  .i21_3f:
  5094                                  	; Check for device handles (stdin)
  5095 000023BD 83FB00                  	cmp	bx, 0
  5096 000023C0 7503E91D01              	je	.i21_3f_stdin
  5097 000023C5 83FB08                  	cmp	bx, MAX_HANDLES
  5098 000023C8 7203E93501              	jae	.i21_3f_bad
  5099                                  
  5100 000023CD 56                      	push	si
  5101 000023CE 57                      	push	di
  5102 000023CF 06                      	push	es
  5103                                  
  5104                                  	; Get handle entry
  5105 000023D0 89D8                    	mov	ax, bx
  5106 000023D2 51                      	push	cx
  5107 000023D3 B104                    	mov	cl, 4
  5108 000023D5 D3E0                    	shl	ax, cl
  5109 000023D7 59                      	pop	cx
  5110 000023D8 89C6                    	mov	si, ax			; SI = handle table offset
  5111                                  
  5112                                  	; Check handle is open
  5113 000023DA 2E80BC[703E]00          	cmp	byte [cs:file_handles + si], 0
  5114 000023E0 7503E91A01              	je	.i21_3f_bad_pop
  5115                                  
  5116                                  	; Save caller's DS:DX
  5117 000023E5 2E8C1E[0E25]            	mov	[cs:.i21_3f_ds], ds
  5118 000023EA 2E8916[1025]            	mov	[cs:.i21_3f_dx], dx
  5119 000023EF 2E890E[1225]            	mov	[cs:.i21_3f_cx], cx
  5120                                  
  5121                                  	; Switch to SHELL_SEG for FAT/disk access
  5122 000023F4 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  5123 000023F7 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  5124                                  
  5125                                  	; How many bytes left in file?
  5126 000023F9 2E8B84[7C3E]            	mov	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 12]	; File size low
  5127 000023FE 2E8B94[7E3E]            	mov	dx, [cs:file_handles + si + 14]	; File size high
  5128 00002403 2E2B84[783E]            	sub	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 8]	; Subtract file pointer low
  5129 00002408 2E1B94[7A3E]            	sbb	dx, [cs:file_handles + si + 10]	; Subtract file pointer high
  5130                                  	; DX:AX = bytes remaining
  5131                                  	; Cap CX to bytes remaining
  5132 0000240D 09D2                    	or	dx, dx
  5133 0000240F 750B                    	jnz	.i21_3f_cx_ok		; More than 64K remaining
  5134 00002411 2E3B06[1225]            	cmp	ax, [cs:.i21_3f_cx]
  5135 00002416 7304                    	jae	.i21_3f_cx_ok
  5136 00002418 2EA3[1225]              	mov	[cs:.i21_3f_cx], ax	; Reduce to remaining
  5137                                  .i21_3f_cx_ok:
  5138                                  
  5139                                  	; Read loop: read from current cluster, advance
  5140 0000241C 2EC706[1425]0000        	mov	word [cs:.i21_3f_read], 0	; Bytes read so far
  5141                                  
  5142                                  	; Load FAT for cluster chain traversal
  5143 00002423 56                      	push	si
  5144 00002424 E8D6EF                  	call	read_fat
  5145 00002427 5E                      	pop	si
  5146                                  
  5147                                  	; Load byte count AFTER read_fat (which clobbers CX)
  5148 00002428 2E8B0E[1225]            	mov	cx, [cs:.i21_3f_cx]
  5149                                  
  5150                                  .i21_3f_read_loop:
  5151 0000242D 83F900                  	cmp	cx, 0
  5152 00002430 7503E99800              	je	.i21_3f_done
  5153                                  
  5154                                  	; Read current cluster into dir_buffer
  5155 00002435 2E8B84[743E]            	mov	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 4]	; Current cluster
  5156 0000243A 83F800                  	cmp	ax, 0
  5157 0000243D 7503E98B00              	je	.i21_3f_done
  5158 00002442 3DF80F                  	cmp	ax, 0xFF8
  5159 00002445 7203E98300              	jae	.i21_3f_done
  5160

  5162 0000244F A2[0D3E]                	mov	[resolved_drive], al
  5163 00002452 2E8B84[743E]            	mov	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 4]
  5164 00002457 E878E9                  	call	cluster_to_chs
  5165 0000245A B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  5166 0000245D 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  5167 0000245F BB0040                  	mov	bx, dir_buffer
  5168 00002462 B402                    	mov	ah, 0x02
  5169 00002464 B002                    	mov	al, SECS_PER_CLUST
  5170 00002466 8A16[0D3E]              	mov	dl, [resolved_drive]

  5173 0000246D 5E                      	pop	si

  5175                                  
  5176                                  	; Copy bytes from dir_buffer + cluster_offset to caller's buffer
  5177 00002470 2E8B9C[763E]            	mov	bx, [cs:file_handles + si + 6]	; Position in cluster
  5178 00002475 2E8B3E[1025]            	mov	di, [cs:.i21_3f_dx]	; Dest offset in caller's buffer
  5179                                  
  5180                                  .i21_3f_copy:
  5181 0000247A 83F900                  	cmp	cx, 0
  5182 0000247D 7444                    	je	.i21_3f_advance_done

  5184 00002483 7324                    	jae	.i21_3f_next_cluster

  5190 0000248F 268805                  	mov	[es:di], al

  5209                                  
  5210                                  .i21_3f_advance_done:

  5212 000024C8 2E893E[1025]            	mov	[cs:.i21_3f_dx], di		; Update buffer position
  5213                                  
  5214                                  .i21_3f_done:
  5215 000024CD 2E8E1E[0E25]            	mov	ds, [cs:.i21_3f_ds]
  5216 000024D2 2EA1[1425]              	mov	ax, [cs:.i21_3f_read]
  5217 000024D6 07                      	pop	es

  5219 000024D8 5E                      	pop	si

  5224 000024E1 CF                      	iret

  5238 000024F1 59                      	pop	cx

  5267                                  ; --- AH=40: Write to file/device ---
  5268                                  ; Input: BX = handle, CX = bytes, DS:DX = buffer
  5269                                  ; Output: AX = bytes written

  5271                                  	; Handle stdout/stderr — print to screen

  5321 0000258B A2[0D3E]                	mov	[resolved_drive], al
  5322 0000258E 2E8B84[743E]            	mov	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 4]
  5323 00002593 51                      	push	cx			; Save byte count BEFORE cluster_to_chs trashes CX
  5324 00002594 E83BE8                  	call	cluster_to_chs

  5334                                  
  5335                                  	; Copy bytes from caller's buffer into dir_buffer
  5336 000025AF 2E8B9C[763E]            	mov	bx, [cs:file_handles + si + 6]	; Position in cluster
  5337 000025B4 2E8B3E[CA26]            	mov	di, [cs:.i21_40_dx]
  5338                                  
  5339                                  .i21_40_copy:
  5340 000025B9 83F900                  	cmp	cx, 0
  5341 000025BC 7503E99100              	je	.i21_40_flush

  5344                                  
  5345                                  	; Copy one byte from caller to cluster buffer
  5346 000025C7 06                      	push	es

  5348 000025CD 268A05                  	mov	al, [es:di]
  5349 000025D0 07                      	pop	es

  5352 000025D6 47                      	inc	di
