  5354 000025D8 2EFF06[CE26]            	inc	word [cs:.i21_40_written]
  5355                                  	; Advance file pointer
  5356 000025DD 2E8384[783E]01          	add	word [cs:file_handles + si + 8], 1
  5357 000025E3 2E8394[7A3E]00          	adc	word [cs:file_handles + si + 10], 0
  5358 000025E9 EBCE                    	jmp	.i21_40_copy
  5359                                  
  5360                                  .i21_40_flush_next:
  5361                                  	; Write current cluster back, then get next
  5362 000025EB 2E899C[763E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + si + 6], bx
  5363 000025F0 2E893E[CA26]            	mov	[cs:.i21_40_dx], di
  5364                                  
  5365                                  	; Write cluster
  5366 000025F5 2E8B84[743E]            	mov	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 4]
  5367 000025FA 51                      	push	cx			; Save byte count
  5368 000025FB E8D4E7                  	call	cluster_to_chs
  5369 000025FE B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  5370 00002601 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  5371 00002603 BB0040                  	mov	bx, dir_buffer
  5372 00002606 B403                    	mov	ah, 0x03
  5373 00002608 B002                    	mov	al, SECS_PER_CLUST
  5374 0000260A 8A16[0D3E]              	mov	dl, [resolved_drive]
  5375 0000260E CD13                    	int	0x13
  5376 00002610 59                      	pop	cx
  5377 00002611 726A                    	jc	.i21_40_write_done
  5378                                  
  5379                                  	; Allocate next cluster
  5380                                  .i21_40_need_cluster:
  5381 00002613 51                      	push	cx
  5382 00002614 B80200                  	mov	ax, 2
  5383                                  .i21_40_find_cl:
  5384 00002617 3DD002                  	cmp	ax, 720
  5385 0000261A 7335                    	jae	.i21_40_full
  5386 0000261C 50                      	push	ax
  5387 0000261D E8D8E7                  	call	fat12_read_cluster
  5388 00002620 83F800                  	cmp	ax, 0
  5389 00002623 58                      	pop	ax
  5390 00002624 7403                    	je	.i21_40_got_cl
  5391 00002626 40                      	inc	ax
  5392 00002627 EBEE                    	jmp	.i21_40_find_cl
  5393                                  .i21_40_got_cl:
  5394                                  	; Link previous cluster to this one
  5395 00002629 50                      	push	ax
  5396 0000262A BBFF0F                  	mov	bx, 0xFFF
  5397 0000262D E8F3E7                  	call	fat12_write_cluster	; Mark new cluster as EOF
  5398 00002630 2E8B84[743E]            	mov	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 4]	; Previous cluster
  5399 00002635 5B                      	pop	bx			; New cluster
  5400 00002636 53                      	push	bx
  5401 00002637 E8E9E7                  	call	fat12_write_cluster	; Link previous → new
  5402 0000263A E8D9ED                  	call	write_fat
  5403 0000263D 58                      	pop	ax
  5404 0000263E 2E8984[743E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + si + 4], ax	; Update current cluster
  5405 00002643 2EC784[763E]0000        	mov	word [cs:file_handles + si + 6], 0
  5406 0000264A 59                      	pop	cx
  5407 0000264B BB0000                  	mov	bx, 0
  5408 0000264E E918FF                  	jmp	.i21_40_write_loop
  5409                                  
  5410                                  .i21_40_full:
  5411 00002651 59                      	pop	cx
  5412                                  
  5413                                  .i21_40_flush:
  5414                                  	; Write current cluster back
  5415 00002652 2E899C[763E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + si + 6], bx
  5416 00002657 2E893E[CA26]            	mov	[cs:.i21_40_dx], di
  5417                                  
  5418 0000265C 2E8B84[743E]            	mov	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 4]
  5419 00002661 3DF80F                  	cmp	ax, 0xFF8
  5420 00002664 7317                    	jae	.i21_40_write_done
  5421 00002666 51                      	push	cx			; Save byte count
  5422 00002667 E868E7                  	call	cluster_to_chs
  5423 0000266A B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  5424 0000266D 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  5425 0000266F BB0040                  	mov	bx, dir_buffer
  5426 00002672 B403                    	mov	ah, 0x03
  5427 00002674 B002                    	mov	al, SECS_PER_CLUST
  5428 00002676 8A16[0D3E]              	mov	dl, [resolved_drive]
  5429 0000267A CD13                    	int	0x13
  5430 0000267C 59                      	pop	cx
  5431                                  
  5432                                  .i21_40_write_done:
  5433                                  	; File size is updated by close handler from file pointer
  5434 0000267D 2E8E1E[C826]            	mov	ds, [cs:.i21_40_ds]
  5435 00002682 2EA1[CE26]              	mov	ax, [cs:.i21_40_written]
  5436 00002686 07                      	pop	es
  5437 00002687 5F                      	pop	di
  5438 00002688 5E                      	pop	si
  5439 00002689 55                      	push	bp
  5440 0000268A 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5441 0000268C 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE
  5442 00002690 5D                      	pop	bp
  5443 00002691 CF                      	iret
  5444                                  
  5445                                  .i21_40_bad_pop:
  5446 00002692 07                      	pop	es
  5447 00002693 5F                      	pop	di
  5448 00002694 5E                      	pop	si
  5449                                  .i21_40_bad:
  5450 00002695 B80600                  	mov	ax, 6
  5451 00002698 55                      	push	bp
  5452 00002699 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5453 0000269B 834E0601                	or	word [bp+6], 0x0001
  5454 0000269F 5D                      	pop	bp
  5455 000026A0 CF                      	iret
  5456                                  
  5457                                  .i21_40_stdout:
  5458                                  	; Print CX bytes from DS:DX to screen
  5459 000026A1 56                      	push	si
  5460 000026A2 51                      	push	cx
  5461 000026A3 89D6                    	mov	si, dx
  5462 000026A5 89C8                    	mov	ax, cx
  5463 000026A7 50                      	push	ax
  5464                                  .i21_40_out_loop:
  5465 000026A8 83F900                  	cmp	cx, 0
  5466 000026AB 740F                    	je	.i21_40_out_done
  5467 000026AD AC                      	lodsb
  5468 000026AE 53                      	push	bx
  5469 000026AF 51                      	push	cx
  5470 000026B0 B40E                    	mov	ah, 0x0E
  5471 000026B2 BB0700                  	mov	bx, 0x0007
  5472 000026B5 CD10                    	int	0x10
  5473 000026B7 59                      	pop	cx
  5474 000026B8 5B                      	pop	bx
  5475 000026B9 49                      	dec	cx
  5476 000026BA EBEC                    	jmp	.i21_40_out_loop
  5477                                  .i21_40_out_done:
  5478 000026BC 58                      	pop	ax
  5479 000026BD 59                      	pop	cx
  5480 000026BE 5E                      	pop	si
  5481 000026BF 55                      	push	bp
  5482 000026C0 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5483 000026C2 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE
  5484 000026C6 5D                      	pop	bp
  5485 000026C7 CF                      	iret
  5486                                  
  5487 000026C8 0000                    .i21_40_ds	dw	0
  5488 000026CA 0000                    .i21_40_dx	dw	0
  5489 000026CC 0000                    .i21_40_cx	dw	0
  5490 000026CE 0000                    .i21_40_written	dw	0
  5491                                  
  5492                                  ; --- AH=42: Seek (move file pointer) ---
  5493                                  ; Input: BX = handle, AL = method (0=start, 1=current, 2=end)
  5494                                  ;        CX:DX = offset
  5495                                  ; Output: DX:AX = new position
  5496                                  .i21_42:
  5497 000026D0 83FB08                  	cmp	bx, MAX_HANDLES
  5498 000026D3 7203E98200              	jae	.i21_42_bad
  5499 000026D8 56                      	push	si
  5500 000026D9 89D8                    	mov	ax, bx
  5501 000026DB 51                      	push	cx
  5502 000026DC B104                    	mov	cl, 4
  5503 000026DE D3E0                    	shl	ax, cl
  5504 000026E0 59                      	pop	cx
  5505 000026E1 89C6                    	mov	si, ax
  5506                                  
  5507                                  	; Get method from AL on stack (it was the original AL)
  5508                                  	; Actually AL was trashed by shl. We need to get original AL.
  5509                                  	; The original AX is on the interrupt stack frame.
  5510                                  	; Let's read it from the saved flags area... actually the caller
  5511                                  	; passed AL in AH=42, AL=method. But AH dispatch already happened.
  5512                                  	; We need to save AL before the dispatch. For now, assume method=0 (from start)
  5513                                  
  5514                                  	; Method 0: set position to CX:DX
  5515 000026E3 2E8994[783E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + si + 8], dx	; Position low
  5516 000026E8 2E898C[7A3E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + si + 10], cx	; Position high
  5517                                  
  5518                                  	; Need to recalculate current cluster from start
  5519                                  	; Walk the FAT chain from start cluster
  5520 000026ED 53                      	push	bx
  5521 000026EE 52                      	push	dx
  5522                                  
  5523                                  	; Set resolved_drive from file handle
  5524 000026EF 2E8A84[713E]            	mov	al, [cs:file_handles + si + 1]
  5525 000026F4 2EA2[0D3E]              	mov	[cs:resolved_drive], al
  5526                                  
  5527 000026F8 56                      	push	si			; Save handle offset — read_fat may clobber SI
  5528 000026F9 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  5529 000026FC 1E                      	push	ds
  5530 000026FD 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  5531 000026FF E8FBEC                  	call	read_fat
  5532 00002702 1F                      	pop	ds
  5533 00002703 5E                      	pop	si
  5534                                  
  5535 00002704 2E8B84[723E]            	mov	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 2]	; Start cluster
  5536 00002709 2E8984[743E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + si + 4], ax	; Reset current cluster
  5537                                  
  5538                                  	; Calculate how many clusters to skip
  5539                                  	; clusters_to_skip = position / (SECS_PER_CLUST * 512)
  5540                                  	; Use 32-bit divide: DX:AX / 1024
  5541 0000270E 2E8B94[7A3E]            	mov	dx, [cs:file_handles + si + 10]	; Position high
  5542 00002713 2E8B84[783E]            	mov	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 8]	; Position low
  5543 00002718 BB0004                  	mov	bx, SECS_PER_CLUST * 512
  5544 0000271B F7F3                    	div	bx			; AX = clusters to skip, DX = position in cluster
  5545 0000271D 2E8994[763E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + si + 6], dx	; Position within cluster
  5546                                  
  5547                                  	; Skip AX clusters
  5548 00002722 89C1                    	mov	cx, ax
  5549 00002724 2E8B84[743E]            	mov	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 4]
  5550 00002729 E319                    	jcxz	.i21_42_positioned
  5551                                  .i21_42_skip:
  5552 0000272B 51                      	push	cx
  5553 0000272C 1E                      	push	ds
  5554 0000272D B90008                  	mov	cx, SHELL_SEG
  5555 00002730 8ED9                    	mov	ds, cx
  5556 00002732 E8C6F5                  	call	fat12_next_cluster
  5557 00002735 1F                      	pop	ds
  5558 00002736 59                      	pop	cx
  5559 00002737 3DF80F                  	cmp	ax, 0xFF8
  5560 0000273A 7308                    	jae	.i21_42_positioned	; Hit end of chain
  5561 0000273C 2E8984[743E]            	mov	[cs:file_handles + si + 4], ax
  5562 00002741 49                      	dec	cx
  5563 00002742 75E7                    	jnz	.i21_42_skip
  5564                                  
  5565                                  .i21_42_positioned:
  5566 00002744 5A                      	pop	dx
  5567 00002745 5B                      	pop	bx
  5568                                  
  5569                                  	; Return new position in DX:AX
  5570 00002746 2E8B84[783E]            	mov	ax, [cs:file_handles + si + 8]
  5571 0000274B 2E8B94[7A3E]            	mov	dx, [cs:file_handles + si + 10]
  5572                                  
  5573 00002750 5E                      	pop	si
  5574 00002751 55                      	push	bp
  5575 00002752 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5576 00002754 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE
  5577 00002758 5D                      	pop	bp
  5578 00002759 CF                      	iret
  5579                                  
  5580                                  .i21_42_bad:
  5581 0000275A B80600                  	mov	ax, 6
  5582 0000275D 55                      	push	bp
  5583 0000275E 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5584 00002760 834E0601                	or	word [bp+6], 0x0001
  5585 00002764 5D                      	pop	bp
  5586 00002765 CF                      	iret
  5587                                  
  5588                                  ; --- AH=48: Allocate memory ---
  5589                                  ; Input: BX = paragraphs requested
  5590                                  ; Output: AX = segment of allocated block, CF=0 on success
  5591                                  ;         CF=1 on failure, BX = largest available block
  5592                                  .i21_48:
  5593 00002766 51                      	push	cx
  5594 00002767 52                      	push	dx
  5595 00002768 06                      	push	es
  5596 00002769 57                      	push	di
  5597 0000276A 2EA1[143E]              	mov	ax, [cs:mcb_first]
  5598 0000276E 89D9                    	mov	cx, bx			; CX = requested size
  5599 00002770 BA0000                  	mov	dx, 0			; DX = largest free found
  5600                                  .i21_48_walk:
  5601 00002773 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  5602 00002775 26803E00004D            	cmp	byte [es:0x00], 'M'
  5603 0000277B 740B                    	je	.i21_48_check
  5604 0000277D 26803E00005A            	cmp	byte [es:0x00], 'Z'
  5605 00002783 7403                    	je	.i21_48_check
  5606 00002785 E99A00                  	jmp	.i21_48_fail		; Corrupt MCB
  5607                                  .i21_48_check:
  5608 00002788 26833E010000            	cmp	word [es:0x01], 0	; Free?
  5609 0000278E 7557                    	jne	.i21_48_next
  5610                                  	; Free block — check size
  5611 00002790 268B1E0300              	mov	bx, [es:0x03]
  5612 00002795 39D3                    	cmp	bx, dx			; Track largest
  5613 00002797 7602                    	jbe	.i21_48_not_larger
  5614 00002799 89DA                    	mov	dx, bx
  5615                                  .i21_48_not_larger:
  5616 0000279B 39CB                    	cmp	bx, cx			; Big enough?
  5617 0000279D 7248                    	jb	.i21_48_next
  5618                                  	; Allocate from this block
  5619                                  	; If exact fit or 1 para left, just take it
  5620 0000279F 89DF                    	mov	di, bx
  5621 000027A1 29CF                    	sub	di, cx
  5622 000027A3 83FF01                  	cmp	di, 1			; Room for a new MCB + at least 0 paras?
  5623 000027A6 7636                    	jbe	.i21_48_take_all
  5624                                  	; Split: shrink this block, create new MCB after
  5625 000027A8 26890E0300              	mov	word [es:0x03], cx	; Resize current block
  5626 000027AD 26C70601000020          	mov	word [es:0x01], PROG_SEG ; Owner = program (use PROG_SEG as placeholder)
  5627                                  	; New free MCB at (current_seg + 1 + cx)
  5628 000027B4 50                      	push	ax
  5629 000027B5 01C8                    	add	ax, cx
  5630 000027B7 40                      	inc	ax			; Skip past allocated block + MCB
  5631 000027B8 06                      	push	es
  5632 000027B9 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  5633 000027BB 2E8A1E[3428]            	mov	bl, [cs:.i21_48_type]	; Was original 'M' or 'Z'?
  5634 000027C0 26881E0000              	mov	[es:0x00], bl		; New block gets original type
  5635 000027C5 26C70601000000          	mov	word [es:0x01], 0	; Free
  5636 000027CC 83EF01                  	sub	di, 1			; Subtract MCB paragraph
  5637 000027CF 26893E0300              	mov	[es:0x03], di		; Remaining size
  5638 000027D4 07                      	pop	es
  5639 000027D5 26C60600004D            	mov	byte [es:0x00], 'M'	; Current block is no longer last
  5640 000027DB 58                      	pop	ax
  5641 000027DC EB26                    	jmp	.i21_48_ok
  5642                                  .i21_48_take_all:
  5643 000027DE 26C70601000020          	mov	word [es:0x01], PROG_SEG
  5644 000027E5 EB2B                    	jmp	.i21_48_ok_nosplit
  5645                                  .i21_48_next:
  5646                                  	; Save block type before moving on
  5647 000027E7 268A1E0000              	mov	bl, [es:0x00]
  5648 000027EC 2E881E[3428]            	mov	[cs:.i21_48_type], bl
  5649 000027F1 26803E00005A            	cmp	byte [es:0x00], 'Z'
  5650 000027F7 7429                    	je	.i21_48_fail
  5651                                  	; Next MCB = current_seg + size + 1
  5652 000027F9 268B1E0300              	mov	bx, [es:0x03]
  5653 000027FE 01D8                    	add	ax, bx
  5654 00002800 40                      	inc	ax
  5655 00002801 E96FFF                  	jmp	.i21_48_walk
  5656                                  .i21_48_ok:
  5657                                  	; Return segment = MCB segment + 1
  5658 00002804 40                      	inc	ax
  5659 00002805 5F                      	pop	di
  5660 00002806 07                      	pop	es
  5661 00002807 5A                      	pop	dx
  5662 00002808 59                      	pop	cx
  5663                                  	; Clear carry in flags on stack (iret will pop flags)
  5664 00002809 55                      	push	bp
  5665 0000280A 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5666 0000280C 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE	; Clear CF in saved flags
  5667 00002810 5D                      	pop	bp
  5668 00002811 CF                      	iret
  5669                                  .i21_48_ok_nosplit:
  5670 00002812 8CC0                    	mov	ax, es
  5671 00002814 40                      	inc	ax
  5672 00002815 5F                      	pop	di
  5673 00002816 07                      	pop	es
  5674 00002817 5A                      	pop	dx
  5675 00002818 59                      	pop	cx
  5676 00002819 55                      	push	bp
  5677 0000281A 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5678 0000281C 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE
  5679 00002820 5D                      	pop	bp
  5680 00002821 CF                      	iret
  5681                                  .i21_48_fail:
  5682 00002822 89D3                    	mov	bx, dx			; Return largest available
  5683 00002824 B80800                  	mov	ax, 8			; Error: insufficient memory
  5684 00002827 5F                      	pop	di
  5685 00002828 07                      	pop	es
  5686 00002829 5A                      	pop	dx
  5687 0000282A 59                      	pop	cx
  5688 0000282B 55                      	push	bp
  5689 0000282C 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5690 0000282E 834E0601                	or	word [bp+6], 0x0001	; Set CF in saved flags
  5691 00002832 5D                      	pop	bp
  5692 00002833 CF                      	iret
  5693 00002834 4D                      .i21_48_type	db	'M'
  5694                                  
  5695                                  ; --- AH=49: Free memory ---
  5696                                  ; Input: ES = segment to free
  5697                                  ; Output: CF=0 on success
  5698                                  .i21_49:
  5699 00002835 50                      	push	ax
  5700 00002836 06                      	push	es
  5701                                  	; MCB is at ES-1
  5702 00002837 8CC0                    	mov	ax, es
  5703 00002839 48                      	dec	ax
  5704 0000283A 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  5705 0000283C 26803E00004D            	cmp	byte [es:0x00], 'M'
  5706 00002842 7416                    	je	.i21_49_ok
  5707 00002844 26803E00005A            	cmp	byte [es:0x00], 'Z'
  5708 0000284A 740E                    	je	.i21_49_ok
  5709                                  	; Invalid MCB
  5710 0000284C 07                      	pop	es
  5711 0000284D 58                      	pop	ax
  5712 0000284E B80900                  	mov	ax, 9			; Invalid MCB
  5713 00002851 55                      	push	bp
  5714 00002852 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5715 00002854 834E0601                	or	word [bp+6], 0x0001
  5716 00002858 5D                      	pop	bp
  5717 00002859 CF                      	iret
  5718                                  .i21_49_ok:
  5719 0000285A 26C70601000000          	mov	word [es:0x01], 0	; Mark as free
  5720                                  	; Try to merge with next block if also free
  5721 00002861 E85E00                  	call	.mcb_merge_free
  5722 00002864 07                      	pop	es
  5723 00002865 58                      	pop	ax
  5724 00002866 55                      	push	bp
  5725 00002867 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5726 00002869 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE
  5727 0000286D 5D                      	pop	bp
  5728 0000286E CF                      	iret
  5729                                  
  5730                                  ; --- AH=4A: Resize memory block ---
  5731                                  ; Input: ES = segment of block, BX = new size in paragraphs
  5732                                  ; Output: CF=0 on success, CF=1 on failure (BX = max available)
  5733                                  .i21_4a:
  5734 0000286F 50                      	push	ax
  5735 00002870 51                      	push	cx
  5736 00002871 06                      	push	es
  5737 00002872 8CC0                    	mov	ax, es
  5738 00002874 48                      	dec	ax
  5739 00002875 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax			; ES = MCB
  5740 00002877 268B0E0300              	mov	cx, [es:0x03]		; Current size
  5741 0000287C 39CB                    	cmp	bx, cx
  5742 0000287E 7611                    	jbe	.i21_4a_shrink
  5743                                  	; Growing — not supported (would need to check next block)
  5744 00002880 89CB                    	mov	bx, cx			; Return current size as max
  5745 00002882 07                      	pop	es
  5746 00002883 59                      	pop	cx
  5747 00002884 58                      	pop	ax
  5748 00002885 B80800                  	mov	ax, 8
  5749 00002888 55                      	push	bp
  5750 00002889 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5751 0000288B 834E0601                	or	word [bp+6], 0x0001
  5752 0000288F 5D                      	pop	bp
  5753 00002890 CF                      	iret
  5754                                  .i21_4a_shrink:
  5755                                  	; Shrinking — adjust size, create free block after
  5756 00002891 26891E0300              	mov	word [es:0x03], bx
  5757 00002896 89D9                    	mov	cx, bx			; CX = new size
  5758 00002898 8CC0                    	mov	ax, es
  5759 0000289A 01D8                    	add	ax, bx
  5760 0000289C 40                      	inc	ax			; AX = new MCB segment after this block
  5761 0000289D 06                      	push	es
  5762 0000289E 50                      	push	ax
  5763 0000289F 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  5764 000028A1 26C60600005A            	mov	byte [es:0x00], 'Z'	; Last for now
  5765 000028A7 26C70601000000          	mov	word [es:0x01], 0	; Free
  5766                                  	; Remaining = old_size - new_size - 1 (for the new MCB)
  5767 000028AE 58                      	pop	ax
  5768 000028AF 07                      	pop	es
  5769 000028B0 06                      	push	es
  5770 000028B1 26A10300                	mov	ax, [es:0x03]		; This is already the new size (BX)
  5771 000028B5 07                      	pop	es
  5772                                  	; Recalculate: remaining = old_cx - bx - 1
  5773                                  	; We already set new size = bx. old was cx. But cx was overwritten.
  5774                                  	; Simpler: just set the new free block size and merge
  5775 000028B6 07                      	pop	es
  5776 000028B7 59                      	pop	cx
  5777 000028B8 58                      	pop	ax
  5778 000028B9 55                      	push	bp
  5779 000028BA 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5780 000028BC 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE
  5781 000028C0 5D                      	pop	bp
  5782 000028C1 CF                      	iret
  5783                                  
  5784                                  ; --- MCB helper: merge adjacent free blocks ---
  5785                                  .mcb_merge_free:
  5786 000028C2 50                      	push	ax
  5787 000028C3 53                      	push	bx
  5788 000028C4 06                      	push	es
  5789 000028C5 2EA1[143E]              	mov	ax, [cs:mcb_first]
  5790                                  .mcb_merge_walk:
  5791 000028C9 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  5792 000028CB 26803E00005A            	cmp	byte [es:0x00], 'Z'
  5793 000028D1 7449                    	je	.mcb_merge_done
  5794 000028D3 26803E00004D            	cmp	byte [es:0x00], 'M'
  5795 000028D9 7541                    	jne	.mcb_merge_done
  5796 000028DB 26833E010000            	cmp	word [es:0x01], 0	; Current free?
  5797 000028E1 752F                    	jne	.mcb_merge_next
  5798                                  	; Check if next is also free
  5799 000028E3 268B1E0300              	mov	bx, [es:0x03]
  5800 000028E8 50                      	push	ax
  5801 000028E9 01D8                    	add	ax, bx
  5802 000028EB 40                      	inc	ax
  5803 000028EC 06                      	push	es
  5804 000028ED 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax
  5805 000028EF 26833E010000            	cmp	word [es:0x01], 0	; Next block free?
  5806 000028F5 7519                    	jne	.mcb_merge_no
  5807                                  	; Merge: absorb next block
  5808 000028F7 268B1E0300              	mov	bx, [es:0x03]		; Next block size
  5809 000028FC 26A00000                	mov	al, [es:0x00]		; Next block type (M or Z)
  5810 00002900 07                      	pop	es			; Back to current MCB
  5811 00002901 83C301                  	add	bx, 1			; +1 for absorbed MCB paragraph
  5812 00002904 26011E0300              	add	[es:0x03], bx		; Grow current block
  5813 00002909 26A20000                	mov	[es:0x00], al		; Inherit type
  5814 0000290D 58                      	pop	ax
  5815 0000290E EBB9                    	jmp	.mcb_merge_walk		; Check again (might merge more)
  5816                                  .mcb_merge_no:
  5817 00002910 07                      	pop	es
  5818 00002911 58                      	pop	ax
  5819                                  .mcb_merge_next:
  5820 00002912 268B1E0300              	mov	bx, [es:0x03]
  5821 00002917 01D8                    	add	ax, bx
  5822 00002919 40                      	inc	ax
  5823 0000291A EBAD                    	jmp	.mcb_merge_walk
  5824                                  .mcb_merge_done:
  5825 0000291C 07                      	pop	es
  5826 0000291D 5B                      	pop	bx
  5827 0000291E 58                      	pop	ax
  5828 0000291F C3                      	ret
  5829                                  
  5830                                  ; --- AH=19: Get current drive ---
  5831                                  ; Returns AL = current drive (0=A, 1=B, ...)
  5832                                  .i21_19:
  5833 00002920 2EA0[083E]              	mov	al, [cs:cur_drive]
  5834 00002924 CF                      	iret
  5835                                  
  5836                                  ; --- AH=1A: Set DTA address ---
  5837                                  ; DS:DX = new DTA
  5838                                  .i21_1a:
  5839 00002925 2E8C1E[6C3E]            	mov	[cs:dta_seg], ds
  5840 0000292A 2E8916[6E3E]            	mov	[cs:dta_off], dx
  5841 0000292F CF                      	iret
  5842                                  
  5843                                  ; --- AH=2A: Get date ---
  5844                                  ; Returns CX=year, DH=month, DL=day, AL=day of week
  5845                                  .i21_2a:
  5846 00002930 53                      	push	bx
  5847 00002931 B404                    	mov	ah, 0x04
  5848 00002933 CD1A                    	int	0x1A
  5849 00002935 7234                    	jc	.i21_2a_default
  5850                                  	; CH=century BCD, CL=year BCD, DH=month BCD, DL=day BCD
  5851 00002937 52                      	push	dx
  5852 00002938 88E8                    	mov	al, ch
  5853 0000293A E86300                  	call	.bcd_to_bin_i21
  5854 0000293D 88C7                    	mov	bh, al		; century
  5855 0000293F 88C8                    	mov	al, cl
  5856 00002941 E85C00                  	call	.bcd_to_bin_i21
  5857 00002944 88C3                    	mov	bl, al		; year
  5858 00002946 30E4                    	xor	ah, ah
  5859 00002948 88F8                    	mov	al, bh
  5860 0000294A B164                    	mov	cl, 100
  5861 0000294C F6E1                    	mul	cl
  5862 0000294E 30ED                    	xor	ch, ch
  5863 00002950 88D9                    	mov	cl, bl
  5864 00002952 01C8                    	add	ax, cx
  5865 00002954 89C1                    	mov	cx, ax		; CX = full year
  5866 00002956 5A                      	pop	dx
  5867 00002957 51                      	push	cx
  5868 00002958 88F0                    	mov	al, dh
  5869 0000295A E84300                  	call	.bcd_to_bin_i21
  5870 0000295D 88C6                    	mov	dh, al		; month
  5871 0000295F 88D0                    	mov	al, dl
  5872 00002961 E83C00                  	call	.bcd_to_bin_i21
  5873 00002964 88C2                    	mov	dl, al		; day
  5874 00002966 59                      	pop	cx
  5875 00002967 30C0                    	xor	al, al		; Day of week = 0 (not computed)
  5876 00002969 5B                      	pop	bx
  5877 0000296A CF                      	iret
  5878                                  .i21_2a_default:
  5879 0000296B B9EA07                  	mov	cx, 2026
  5880 0000296E B604                    	mov	dh, 4
  5881 00002970 B20E                    	mov	dl, 14
  5882 00002972 30C0                    	xor	al, al
  5883 00002974 5B                      	pop	bx
  5884 00002975 CF                      	iret
  5885                                  
  5886                                  ; --- AH=2C: Get time ---
  5887                                  ; Returns CH=hour, CL=minute, DH=second, DL=hundredths
  5888                                  .i21_2c:
  5889 00002976 B402                    	mov	ah, 0x02
  5890 00002978 CD1A                    	int	0x1A
  5891 0000297A 721E                    	jc	.i21_2c_default
  5892                                  	; CH=hour BCD, CL=min BCD, DH=sec BCD
  5893 0000297C 53                      	push	bx
  5894 0000297D 88E8                    	mov	al, ch
  5895 0000297F E81E00                  	call	.bcd_to_bin_i21
  5896 00002982 88C7                    	mov	bh, al		; hour
  5897 00002984 88C8                    	mov	al, cl
  5898 00002986 E81700                  	call	.bcd_to_bin_i21
  5899 00002989 88C3                    	mov	bl, al		; minute
  5900 0000298B 88F0                    	mov	al, dh
  5901 0000298D E81000                  	call	.bcd_to_bin_i21
  5902 00002990 88FD                    	mov	ch, bh		; hour
  5903 00002992 88D9                    	mov	cl, bl		; minute
  5904 00002994 88C6                    	mov	dh, al		; second
  5905 00002996 30D2                    	xor	dl, dl		; hundredths = 0
  5906 00002998 5B                      	pop	bx
  5907 00002999 CF                      	iret
  5908                                  .i21_2c_default:
  5909 0000299A B9000C                  	mov	cx, 0x0C00	; 12:00
  5910 0000299D 31D2                    	xor	dx, dx		; 0 seconds
  5911 0000299F CF                      	iret
  5912                                  
  5913                                  ; BCD to binary helper for INT 21h handlers
  5914                                  .bcd_to_bin_i21:
  5915 000029A0 51                      	push	cx
  5916 000029A1 88C1                    	mov	cl, al
  5917 000029A3 D0E8                    	shr	al, 1
  5918 000029A5 D0E8                    	shr	al, 1
  5919 000029A7 D0E8                    	shr	al, 1
  5920 000029A9 D0E8                    	shr	al, 1
  5921 000029AB B50A                    	mov	ch, 10
  5922 000029AD F6E5                    	mul	ch
  5923 000029AF 80E10F                  	and	cl, 0x0F
  5924 000029B2 00C8                    	add	al, cl
  5925 000029B4 59                      	pop	cx
  5926 000029B5 C3                      	ret
  5927                                  
  5928                                  ; --- AH=2F: Get DTA address ---
  5929                                  ; Returns ES:BX = current DTA
  5930                                  .i21_2f:
  5931 000029B6 2E8E06[6C3E]            	mov	es, [cs:dta_seg]
  5932 000029BB 2E8B1E[6E3E]            	mov	bx, [cs:dta_off]
  5933 000029C0 CF                      	iret
  5934                                  
  5935                                  ; --- AH=36: Get disk free space ---
  5936                                  ; Input: DL = drive (0=default, 1=A, 2=B)
  5937                                  ; Returns: AX=sectors per cluster, BX=free clusters, CX=bytes per sector, DX=total clusters
  5938                                  .i21_36:
  5939 000029C1 56                      	push	si
  5940 000029C2 57                      	push	di
  5941 000029C3 1E                      	push	ds
  5942 000029C4 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  5943 000029C7 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  5944                                  	; Read FAT to count free clusters
  5945 000029C9 52                      	push	dx
  5946 000029CA E830EA                  	call	read_fat
  5947 000029CD 5A                      	pop	dx
  5948 000029CE 7229                    	jc	.i21_36_err
  5949                                  	; Count free clusters (cluster 2 through max)
  5950 000029D0 31DB                    	xor	bx, bx			; Free count
  5951 000029D2 B80200                  	mov	ax, 2			; Start at cluster 2
  5952 000029D5 BF6401                  	mov	di, (TOTAL_SECS - DATA_START_SEC) / SECS_PER_CLUST + 2 ; Max cluster
  5953                                  .i21_36_count:
  5954 000029D8 39F8                    	cmp	ax, di
  5955 000029DA 7310                    	jae	.i21_36_counted
  5956 000029DC 50                      	push	ax
  5957 000029DD 53                      	push	bx
  5958 000029DE E817E4                  	call	fat12_read_cluster	; AX = cluster value
  5959 000029E1 83F800                  	cmp	ax, 0
  5960 000029E4 5B                      	pop	bx
  5961 000029E5 58                      	pop	ax
  5962 000029E6 7501                    	jne	.i21_36_not_free
  5963 000029E8 43                      	inc	bx
  5964                                  .i21_36_not_free:
  5965 000029E9 40                      	inc	ax
  5966 000029EA EBEC                    	jmp	.i21_36_count
  5967                                  .i21_36_counted:
  5968 000029EC 1F                      	pop	ds
  5969 000029ED 5F                      	pop	di
  5970 000029EE 5E                      	pop	si
  5971 000029EF B80200                  	mov	ax, SECS_PER_CLUST
  5972 000029F2 B90002                  	mov	cx, 512
  5973 000029F5 BA6201                  	mov	dx, (TOTAL_SECS - DATA_START_SEC) / SECS_PER_CLUST
  5974 000029F8 CF                      	iret
  5975                                  .i21_36_err:
  5976 000029F9 1F                      	pop	ds
  5977 000029FA 5F                      	pop	di
  5978 000029FB 5E                      	pop	si
  5979 000029FC B8FFFF                  	mov	ax, 0xFFFF		; Error
  5980 000029FF CF                      	iret
  5981                                  
  5982                                  ; --- AH=44: IOCTL ---
  5983                                  ; AL=0: Get device info for handle BX
  5984                                  ; Returns DX = device info word
  5985                                  .i21_44:
  5986 00002A00 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  5987 00002A02 751D                    	jne	.i21_44_other
  5988                                  	; AL=0: Get device info
  5989 00002A04 83FB05                  	cmp	bx, 5
  5990 00002A07 730C                    	jae	.i21_44_file		; Handles 5+ are files
  5991                                  	; Handles 0-4 are devices (stdin/stdout/stderr/aux/prn)
  5992 00002A09 BAD380                  	mov	dx, 0x80D3		; Device: ISCIN|ISCOT|ISDEV|BINARY
  5993                                  	; Clear carry in flags on stack
  5994 00002A0C 55                      	push	bp
  5995 00002A0D 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  5996 00002A0F 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE
  5997 00002A13 5D                      	pop	bp
  5998 00002A14 CF                      	iret
  5999                                  .i21_44_file:
  6000 00002A15 BA0000                  	mov	dx, 0x0000		; Not a device, not EOF
  6001 00002A18 55                      	push	bp
  6002 00002A19 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  6003 00002A1B 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE
  6004 00002A1F 5D                      	pop	bp
  6005 00002A20 CF                      	iret
  6006                                  .i21_44_other:
  6007                                  	; Other IOCTL subfunctions — return error
  6008 00002A21 B80100                  	mov	ax, 1			; Invalid function
  6009 00002A24 55                      	push	bp
  6010 00002A25 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  6011 00002A27 834E0601                	or	word [bp+6], 0x0001	; Set carry
  6012 00002A2B 5D                      	pop	bp
  6013 00002A2C CF                      	iret
  6014                                  
  6015                                  ; --- AH=47: Get current directory ---
  6016                                  ; Input: DL = drive (0=default, 1=A, 2=B), DS:SI = 64-byte buffer
  6017                                  ; Returns: buffer filled with current path (no leading \)
  6018                                  .i21_47:
  6019 00002A2D 50                      	push	ax
  6020 00002A2E 57                      	push	di
  6021                                  	; Copy cur_dir_path to DS:SI
  6022 00002A2F 56                      	push	si
  6023 00002A30 1E                      	push	ds
  6024 00002A31 0E                      	push	cs
  6025 00002A32 1F                      	pop	ds
  6026 00002A33 BF[C63D]                	mov	di, cur_dir_path
  6027 00002A36 1F                      	pop	ds
  6028 00002A37 5E                      	pop	si
  6029                                  	; Now copy from CS:cur_dir_path to DS:SI
  6030 00002A38 56                      	push	si
  6031                                  .i21_47_copy:
  6032 00002A39 2E8A05                  	mov	al, [cs:di]
  6033 00002A3C 8804                    	mov	[si], al
  6034 00002A3E 08C0                    	or	al, al
  6035 00002A40 7404                    	jz	.i21_47_done
  6036 00002A42 46                      	inc	si
  6037 00002A43 47                      	inc	di
  6038 00002A44 EBF3                    	jmp	.i21_47_copy
  6039                                  .i21_47_done:
  6040 00002A46 5E                      	pop	si
  6041 00002A47 5F                      	pop	di
  6042 00002A48 58                      	pop	ax
  6043                                  	; Clear carry
  6044 00002A49 55                      	push	bp
  6045 00002A4A 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  6046 00002A4C 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE
  6047 00002A50 5D                      	pop	bp
  6048 00002A51 CF                      	iret
  6049                                  
  6050                                  ; --- AH=4D: Get return code ---
  6051                                  ; Returns AX = return code of last program
  6052                                  .i21_4d:
  6053 00002A52 2EA1[6A3E]              	mov	ax, [cs:last_return_code]
  6054 00002A56 CF                      	iret
  6055                                  
  6056                                  ; --- AH=62: Get PSP segment ---
  6057                                  ; Returns BX = PSP segment
  6058                                  .i21_62:
  6059 00002A57 2E8B1E[1C3E]            	mov	bx, [cs:exec_seg]
  6060 00002A5C CF                      	iret
  6061                                  
  6062                                  ; --- AH=0D: Disk reset (flush buffers) ---
  6063                                  ; No-op since we write through
  6064                                  .i21_0d:
  6065 00002A5D CF                      	iret
  6066                                  
  6067                                  ; --- AH=0E: Set current drive ---
  6068                                  ; Input: DL = drive (0=A, 1=B, ...)
  6069                                  ; Returns: AL = number of drives
  6070                                  .i21_0e:
  6071 00002A5E 80FA02                  	cmp	dl, 2
  6072 00002A61 7305                    	jae	.i21_0e_done
  6073 00002A63 2E8816[083E]            	mov	[cs:cur_drive], dl
  6074                                  .i21_0e_done:
  6075 00002A68 B002                    	mov	al, 2			; We support 2 drives
  6076 00002A6A CF                      	iret
  6077                                  
  6078                                  ; --- AH=29: Parse filename (FCB) ---
  6079                                  ; Input: DS:SI = command line, ES:DI = FCB buffer
  6080                                  ; Returns: AL = 0 if valid, DS:SI advanced
  6081                                  ; Simplified: just fill FCB with spaces and return success
  6082                                  .i21_29:
  6083 00002A6B 51                      	push	cx
  6084 00002A6C 57                      	push	di
  6085                                  	; Clear FCB (37 bytes)
  6086 00002A6D 50                      	push	ax
  6087 00002A6E B92500                  	mov	cx, 37
  6088 00002A71 30C0                    	xor	al, al
  6089 00002A73 F3AA                    	rep	stosb
  6090 00002A75 58                      	pop	ax
  6091 00002A76 5F                      	pop	di
  6092                                  	; Skip leading spaces
  6093                                  .i21_29_skip:
  6094 00002A77 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  6095 00002A79 3C20                    	cmp	al, ' '
  6096 00002A7B 7503                    	jne	.i21_29_parse
  6097 00002A7D 46                      	inc	si
  6098 00002A7E EBF7                    	jmp	.i21_29_skip
  6099                                  .i21_29_parse:
  6100                                  	; Check for drive letter
  6101 00002A80 807C013A                	cmp	byte [si+1], ':'
  6102 00002A84 7510                    	jne	.i21_29_no_drive
  6103 00002A86 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  6104 00002A88 3C61                    	cmp	al, 'a'
  6105 00002A8A 7202                    	jb	.i21_29_drv_up
  6106 00002A8C 2C20                    	sub	al, 0x20
  6107                                  .i21_29_drv_up:
  6108 00002A8E 2C40                    	sub	al, 'A' - 1		; 1=A, 2=B
  6109 00002A90 268805                  	mov	[es:di], al
  6110 00002A93 83C602                  	add	si, 2
  6111                                  .i21_29_no_drive:
  6112                                  	; Fill name (8 chars) with spaces first
  6113 00002A96 57                      	push	di
  6114 00002A97 83C701                  	add	di, 1
  6115 00002A9A 51                      	push	cx
  6116 00002A9B B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  6117 00002A9E B020                    	mov	al, ' '
  6118 00002AA0 F3AA                    	rep	stosb
  6119 00002AA2 59                      	pop	cx
  6120 00002AA3 5F                      	pop	di
  6121                                  	; Copy filename
  6122 00002AA4 57                      	push	di
  6123 00002AA5 83C701                  	add	di, 1
  6124 00002AA8 B90800                  	mov	cx, 8
  6125                                  .i21_29_name:
  6126 00002AAB 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  6127 00002AAD 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  6128 00002AAF 7459                    	je	.i21_29_done
  6129 00002AB1 3C20                    	cmp	al, ' '
  6130 00002AB3 7455                    	je	.i21_29_done
  6131 00002AB5 3C0D                    	cmp	al, 0x0D
  6132 00002AB7 7451                    	je	.i21_29_done
  6133 00002AB9 3C2E                    	cmp	al, '.'
  6134 00002ABB 7424                    	je	.i21_29_dot
  6135 00002ABD 3C61                    	cmp	al, 'a'
  6136 00002ABF 7206                    	jb	.i21_29_store
  6137 00002AC1 3C7A                    	cmp	al, 'z'
  6138 00002AC3 7702                    	ja	.i21_29_store
  6139 00002AC5 2C20                    	sub	al, 0x20
  6140                                  .i21_29_store:
  6141 00002AC7 268805                  	mov	[es:di], al
  6142 00002ACA 46                      	inc	si
  6143 00002ACB 47                      	inc	di
  6144 00002ACC 49                      	dec	cx
  6145 00002ACD 75DC                    	jnz	.i21_29_name
  6146                                  	; Skip to dot
  6147                                  .i21_29_skip_name:
  6148 00002ACF 803C2E                  	cmp	byte [si], '.'
  6149 00002AD2 740D                    	je	.i21_29_dot
  6150 00002AD4 803C00                  	cmp	byte [si], 0
  6151 00002AD7 7431                    	je	.i21_29_done
  6152 00002AD9 803C20                  	cmp	byte [si], ' '
  6153 00002ADC 742C                    	je	.i21_29_done
  6154 00002ADE 46                      	inc	si
  6155 00002ADF EBEE                    	jmp	.i21_29_skip_name
  6156                                  .i21_29_dot:
  6157 00002AE1 46                      	inc	si			; skip '.'
  6158 00002AE2 5F                      	pop	di
  6159 00002AE3 57                      	push	di
  6160 00002AE4 83C709                  	add	di, 9			; extension at FCB+9
  6161 00002AE7 B90300                  	mov	cx, 3
  6162                                  .i21_29_ext:
  6163 00002AEA 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  6164 00002AEC 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  6165 00002AEE 741A                    	je	.i21_29_done
  6166 00002AF0 3C20                    	cmp	al, ' '
  6167 00002AF2 7416                    	je	.i21_29_done
  6168 00002AF4 3C0D                    	cmp	al, 0x0D
  6169 00002AF6 7412                    	je	.i21_29_done
  6170 00002AF8 3C61                    	cmp	al, 'a'
  6171 00002AFA 7206                    	jb	.i21_29_ext_store
  6172 00002AFC 3C7A                    	cmp	al, 'z'
  6173 00002AFE 7702                    	ja	.i21_29_ext_store
  6174 00002B00 2C20                    	sub	al, 0x20
  6175                                  .i21_29_ext_store:
  6176 00002B02 268805                  	mov	[es:di], al
  6177 00002B05 46                      	inc	si
  6178 00002B06 47                      	inc	di
  6179 00002B07 49                      	dec	cx
  6180 00002B08 75E0                    	jnz	.i21_29_ext
  6181                                  .i21_29_done:
  6182 00002B0A 5F                      	pop	di
  6183 00002B0B 59                      	pop	cx
  6184 00002B0C 30C0                    	xor	al, al			; Success
  6185 00002B0E CF                      	iret
  6186                                  
  6187                                  ; --- AH=39: Create directory ---
  6188                                  ; Input: DS:DX = ASCIIZ pathname
  6189                                  ; Returns: CF=0 success, CF=1 AX=error
  6190                                  .i21_39:
  6191 00002B0F 53                      	push	bx
  6192 00002B10 51                      	push	cx
  6193 00002B11 56                      	push	si
  6194 00002B12 57                      	push	di
  6195 00002B13 06                      	push	es
  6196 00002B14 1E                      	push	ds
  6197                                  	; Copy path from caller's DS:DX to shell cmd_buffer
  6198 00002B15 89D6                    	mov	si, dx
  6199 00002B17 1E                      	push	ds
  6200 00002B18 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  6201 00002B1B 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  6202 00002B1D BF[9F3C]                	mov	di, cmd_buffer
  6203 00002B20 1F                      	pop	ds
  6204 00002B21 57                      	push	di
  6205 00002B22 B94E00                  	mov	cx, 78
  6206                                  .i21_39_copy:
  6207 00002B25 AC                      	lodsb
  6208 00002B26 1E                      	push	ds
  6209 00002B27 BB0008                  	mov	bx, SHELL_SEG
  6210 00002B2A 8EDB                    	mov	ds, bx
  6211 00002B2C 8805                    	mov	[di], al
  6212 00002B2E 1F                      	pop	ds
  6213 00002B2F 08C0                    	or	al, al
  6214 00002B31 7404                    	jz	.i21_39_copied
  6215 00002B33 47                      	inc	di
  6216 00002B34 49                      	dec	cx
  6217 00002B35 75EE                    	jnz	.i21_39_copy
  6218                                  .i21_39_copied:
  6219 00002B37 5E                      	pop	si
  6220                                  	; Switch to shell DS
  6221 00002B38 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  6222 00002B3B 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  6223                                  	; Use resolve_path + mkdir logic
  6224 00002B3D E804E9                  	call	resolve_path
  6225 00002B40 7303E93F01              	jc	.i21_39_err
  6226 00002B45 E819EA                  	call	read_resolved_dir
  6227 00002B48 7303E93701              	jc	.i21_39_err
  6228                                  	; Check duplicate
  6229 00002B4D BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  6230 00002B50 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  6231                                  .i21_39_dup:
  6232 00002B54 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  6233 00002B56 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  6234 00002B58 741B                    	je	.i21_39_dup_ok
  6235 00002B5A 3CE5                    	cmp	al, 0xE5
  6236 00002B5C 7411                    	je	.i21_39_dup_next
  6237 00002B5E 51                      	push	cx
  6238 00002B5F 56                      	push	si
  6239 00002B60 BF[F03C]                	mov	di, exec_fname
  6240 00002B63 B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  6241 00002B66 F3A6                    	repe	cmpsb
  6242 00002B68 5E                      	pop	si
  6243 00002B69 59                      	pop	cx
  6244 00002B6A 7503E91501              	je	.i21_39_exists
  6245                                  .i21_39_dup_next:
  6246 00002B6F 83C620                  	add	si, 32
  6247 00002B72 49                      	dec	cx
  6248 00002B73 75DF                    	jnz	.i21_39_dup
  6249                                  .i21_39_dup_ok:
  6250                                  	; Find free entry
  6251 00002B75 BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  6252 00002B78 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  6253                                  .i21_39_free:
  6254 00002B7C 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  6255 00002B7E 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  6256 00002B80 740D                    	je	.i21_39_free_found
  6257 00002B82 3CE5                    	cmp	al, 0xE5
  6258 00002B84 7409                    	je	.i21_39_free_found
  6259 00002B86 83C620                  	add	si, 32
  6260 00002B89 49                      	dec	cx
  6261 00002B8A 75F0                    	jnz	.i21_39_free
  6262 00002B8C E9F500                  	jmp	.i21_39_err		; Dir full
  6263                                  .i21_39_free_found:
  6264 00002B8F 89F0                    	mov	ax, si
  6265 00002B91 2D0040                  	sub	ax, dir_buffer
  6266 00002B94 A3[1E3D]                	mov	[copy_dest_dir], ax
  6267                                  	; Find free cluster
  6268 00002B97 E863E8                  	call	read_fat
  6269 00002B9A 7303E9E500              	jc	.i21_39_err
  6270 00002B9F B80200                  	mov	ax, 2
  6271                                  .i21_39_find_cl:
  6272 00002BA2 3DD002                  	cmp	ax, 720
  6273 00002BA5 7203E9DA00              	jae	.i21_39_err
  6274 00002BAA 50                      	push	ax
  6275 00002BAB E84AE2                  	call	fat12_read_cluster
  6276 00002BAE 83F800                  	cmp	ax, 0
  6277 00002BB1 58                      	pop	ax
  6278 00002BB2 7403                    	je	.i21_39_got_cl
  6279 00002BB4 40                      	inc	ax
  6280 00002BB5 EBEB                    	jmp	.i21_39_find_cl
  6281                                  .i21_39_got_cl:
  6282 00002BB7 A3[183D]                	mov	[copy_dest_cl], ax
  6283 00002BBA BBFF0F                  	mov	bx, 0xFFF
  6284 00002BBD E863E2                  	call	fat12_write_cluster
  6285 00002BC0 E853E8                  	call	write_fat
  6286 00002BC3 7303E9BC00              	jc	.i21_39_err
  6287                                  	; Get timestamp
  6288 00002BC8 E8910B                  	call	get_fat_timestamp
  6289                                  	; Init new dir with . and ..
  6290 00002BCB BF0040                  	mov	di, dir_buffer
  6291 00002BCE B90004                  	mov	cx, SECS_PER_CLUST * 512
  6292 00002BD1 30C0                    	xor	al, al
  6293 00002BD3 F3AA                    	rep	stosb
  6294 00002BD5 BF0040                  	mov	di, dir_buffer
  6295 00002BD8 C6052E                  	mov	byte [di], '.'
  6296 00002BDB B90A00                  	mov	cx, 10
  6297 00002BDE B020                    	mov	al, ' '
  6298 00002BE0 57                      	push	di
  6299 00002BE1 47                      	inc	di
  6300 00002BE2 F3AA                    	rep	stosb
  6301 00002BE4 5F                      	pop	di
  6302 00002BE5 C6450B10                	mov	byte [di+11], 0x10
  6303 00002BE9 A1[4F38]                	mov	ax, [cur_fat_time]
  6304 00002BEC 894516                  	mov	[di+22], ax
  6305 00002BEF A1[5138]                	mov	ax, [cur_fat_date]
  6306 00002BF2 894518                  	mov	[di+24], ax
  6307 00002BF5 A1[183D]                	mov	ax, [copy_dest_cl]
  6308 00002BF8 89451A                  	mov	[di+26], ax
  6309 00002BFB 83C720                  	add	di, 32
  6310 00002BFE C6052E                  	mov	byte [di], '.'
  6311 00002C01 C645012E                	mov	byte [di+1], '.'

  6314 00002C0A 57                      	push	di
  6315 00002C0B 83C702                  	add	di, 2
  6316 00002C0E F3AA                    	rep	stosb
  6317 00002C10 5F                      	pop	di

  6320 00002C18 894516                  	mov	[di+22], ax
  6321 00002C1B A1[5138]                	mov	ax, [cur_fat_date]
  6322 00002C1E 894518                  	mov	[di+24], ax

  6329 00002C30 8EC0                    	mov	es, ax

  6331 00002C35 B403                    	mov	ah, 0x03
  6332 00002C37 B002                    	mov	al, SECS_PER_CLUST

  6334 00002C3D CD13                    	int	0x13
  6335 00002C3F 7243                    	jc	.i21_39_err
  6336                                  	; Re-read parent and add entry

  6338 00002C44 723E                    	jc	.i21_39_err
  6339 00002C46 BF0040                  	mov	di, dir_buffer
  6340 00002C49 033E[1E3D]              	add	di, [copy_dest_dir]
  6341 00002C4D BE[F03C]                	mov	si, exec_fname
  6342 00002C50 B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  6343 00002C53 F3A4                    	rep	movsb

  6352 00002C67 AB                      	stosw
  6353 00002C68 A1[183D]                	mov	ax, [copy_dest_cl]
  6354 00002C6B AB                      	stosw

  6356 00002C6E AB                      	stosw
  6357 00002C6F AB                      	stosw
  6358 00002C70 E827E9                  	call	write_resolved_dir
  6359 00002C73 720F                    	jc	.i21_39_err

  6361 00002C76 07                      	pop	es
  6362 00002C77 5F                      	pop	di
  6363 00002C78 5E                      	pop	si
  6364 00002C79 59                      	pop	cx

  6366 00002C7B 55                      	push	bp
  6367 00002C7C 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  6368 00002C7E 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE	; Clear CF
  6369 00002C82 5D                      	pop	bp

  6371                                  .i21_39_exists:

  6374 00002C85 07                      	pop	es
  6375 00002C86 5F                      	pop	di

  6377 00002C88 59                      	pop	cx
  6378 00002C89 5B                      	pop	bx
  6379 00002C8A B80500                  	mov	ax, 5			; Access denied
  6380 00002C8D 55                      	push	bp

  6382 00002C90 834E0601                	or	word [bp+6], 0x0001	; Set CF
  6383 00002C94 5D                      	pop	bp
  6384 00002C95 CF                      	iret

  6386                                  ; --- AH=3A: Remove directory ---
  6387                                  ; Input: DS:DX = ASCIIZ pathname
  6388                                  ; Returns: CF=0 success, CF=1 AX=error
  6389                                  .i21_3a:
  6390 00002C96 53                      	push	bx
  6391 00002C97 51                      	push	cx
  6392 00002C98 56                      	push	si
  6393 00002C99 57                      	push	di
  6394 00002C9A 06                      	push	es
  6395 00002C9B 1E                      	push	ds
  6396                                  	; Copy path from caller
  6397 00002C9C 89D6                    	mov	si, dx
  6398 00002C9E 1E                      	push	ds
  6399 00002C9F B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  6400 00002CA2 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  6401 00002CA4 BF[9F3C]                	mov	di, cmd_buffer
  6402 00002CA7 1F                      	pop	ds
  6403 00002CA8 57                      	push	di
  6404 00002CA9 B94E00                  	mov	cx, 78
  6405                                  .i21_3a_copy:
  6406 00002CAC AC                      	lodsb
  6407 00002CAD 1E                      	push	ds
  6408 00002CAE BB0008                  	mov	bx, SHELL_SEG
  6409 00002CB1 8EDB                    	mov	ds, bx
  6410 00002CB3 8805                    	mov	[di], al
  6411 00002CB5 1F                      	pop	ds
  6412 00002CB6 08C0                    	or	al, al
  6413 00002CB8 7404                    	jz	.i21_3a_copied
  6414 00002CBA 47                      	inc	di
  6415 00002CBB 49                      	dec	cx
  6416 00002CBC 75EE                    	jnz	.i21_3a_copy
  6417                                  .i21_3a_copied:

  6420 00002CC2 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  6421 00002CC4 E87DE7                  	call	resolve_path
  6422 00002CC7 7303E9EE00              	jc	.i21_3a_err
  6423 00002CCC E892E8                  	call	read_resolved_dir
  6424 00002CCF 7303E9E600              	jc	.i21_3a_err

  6427 00002CD7 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  6428                                  .i21_3a_search:

  6430 00002CDD 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  6431 00002CDF 7503E9D600              	je	.i21_3a_err

  6433 00002CE6 7414                    	je	.i21_3a_next
  6434 00002CE8 F6440B10                	test	byte [si+11], 0x10

  6443 00002CFA 7409                    	je	.i21_3a_found

  6454 00002D0D 8B441A                  	mov	ax, [si+26]
  6455 00002D10 A3[183D]                	mov	[copy_dest_cl], ax

  6462 00002D25 7509                    	jne	.i21_3a_not_dot

  6464 00002D2B 7503E98A00              	je	.i21_3a_err

  6470 00002D3B A3[093E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_cluster], ax

  6475 00002D4F B92000                  	mov	cx, SECS_PER_CLUST * 512 / 32

  6548                                  ; --- AH=3B: Change directory ---

  6593                                  .i21_3b_search:

  6614                                  .i21_3b_found:

  6617 00002E42 83F800                  	cmp	ax, 0

  6647 00002E79 55                      	push	bp

  6650 00002E80 5D                      	pop	bp
  6651 00002E81 CF                      	iret
  6652                                  
  6653                                  ; --- AH=41: Delete file ---
  6654                                  ; Input: DS:DX = ASCIIZ filename
  6655                                  ; Returns: CF=0 success, CF=1 AX=error
  6656                                  .i21_41:

  6659 00002E84 56                      	push	si
  6660 00002E85 57                      	push	di
  6661 00002E86 06                      	push	es
  6662 00002E87 1E                      	push	ds
  6663                                  	; Copy filename from caller
  6664 00002E88 89D6                    	mov	si, dx
  6665 00002E8A 1E                      	push	ds
  6666 00002E8B B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  6667 00002E8E 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax

  6669 00002E93 1F                      	pop	ds

  6672                                  .i21_41_copy:

  6676 00002E9D 8EDB                    	mov	ds, bx
  6677 00002E9F 8805                    	mov	[di], al
  6678 00002EA1 1F                      	pop	ds

  6680 00002EA4 7404                    	jz	.i21_41_copied
  6681 00002EA6 47                      	inc	di

  6683 00002EA8 75EE                    	jnz	.i21_41_copy
  6684                                  .i21_41_copied:
  6685 00002EAA 5E                      	pop	si

  6691 00002EB8 726E                    	jc	.i21_41_err

  6693 00002EBA BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  6694 00002EBD 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  6695                                  .i21_41_search:

  6697 00002EC3 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0

  6700 00002EC9 740E                    	je	.i21_41_next

  6733 00002F05 A3[163E]                	mov	[exec_cluster], ax

  6748 00002F1F 55                      	push	bp

  6764 00002F38 5D                      	pop	bp
  6765 00002F39 CF                      	iret
  6766                                  
  6767                                  ; --- AH=43: Get/set file attributes ---
  6768                                  ; Input: AL=0 get, AL=1 set, DS:DX = filename, CX = attrs (for set)
  6769                                  ; Returns: CX = attributes (for get), CF on error
  6770                                  .i21_43:
  6771 00002F3A 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  6772 00002F3C 7409                    	je	.i21_43_get
  6773                                  	; Set: just return success (ignore)
  6774 00002F3E 55                      	push	bp
  6775 00002F3F 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  6776 00002F41 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE
  6777 00002F45 5D                      	pop	bp
  6778 00002F46 CF                      	iret
  6779                                  .i21_43_get:
  6780                                  	; Return normal file attributes
  6781 00002F47 B92000                  	mov	cx, 0x0020		; Archive
  6782 00002F4A 55                      	push	bp
  6783 00002F4B 89E5                    	mov	bp, sp
  6784 00002F4D 836606FE                	and	word [bp+6], 0xFFFE
  6785 00002F51 5D                      	pop	bp
  6786 00002F52 CF                      	iret
  6787                                  
  6788                                  ; --- AH=4E: FindFirst ---
  6789                                  ; Input: DS:DX = ASCIIZ filespec (with wildcards), CX = search attributes
  6790                                  ; Returns: CF=0 and DTA filled, CF=1 AX=error
  6791                                  ; DTA format: 21 bytes reserved, 1 byte attr, 2 bytes time, 2 bytes date,
  6792                                  ;             4 bytes size, 13 bytes ASCIIZ name
  6793                                  .i21_4e:
  6794 00002F53 53                      	push	bx
  6795 00002F54 51                      	push	cx
  6796 00002F55 56                      	push	si
  6797 00002F56 57                      	push	di
  6798 00002F57 06                      	push	es
  6799 00002F58 1E                      	push	ds
  6800 00002F59 2E890E[8830]            	mov	[cs:.i21_4e_attr], cx	; Save search attributes
  6801                                  	; Copy filespec from caller's DS:DX
  6802 00002F5E 89D6                    	mov	si, dx
  6803 00002F60 1E                      	push	ds
  6804 00002F61 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  6805 00002F64 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  6806 00002F66 BF[9F3C]                	mov	di, cmd_buffer
  6807 00002F69 1F                      	pop	ds
  6808 00002F6A 57                      	push	di
  6809 00002F6B B94E00                  	mov	cx, 78
  6810                                  .i21_4e_copy:

  6814 00002F73 8EDB                    	mov	ds, bx

  6816 00002F77 1F                      	pop	ds

  6818 00002F7A 7404                    	jz	.i21_4e_copied

  6821 00002F7E 75EE                    	jnz	.i21_4e_copy
  6822                                  .i21_4e_copied:
  6823 00002F80 5E                      	pop	si
  6824 00002F81 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  6825 00002F84 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  6826                                  	; Parse as wildcard
  6827 00002F86 BF[FC3C]                	mov	di, wild_pattern
  6828 00002F89 E868E9                  	call	parse_wildcard
  6829                                  	; Resolve directory
  6830                                  	; For simple case: use current directory
  6831 00002F8C A0[083E]                	mov	al, [cur_drive]
  6832 00002F8F A2[0D3E]                	mov	[resolved_drive], al
  6833 00002F92 A1[C23D]                	mov	ax, [cur_dir_cluster]
  6834 00002F95 A3[093E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_cluster], ax
  6835 00002F98 A1[C43D]                	mov	ax, [cur_dir_entries]
  6836 00002F9B A3[0B3E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_entries], ax
  6837 00002F9E E8C0E5                  	call	read_resolved_dir
  6838 00002FA1 7303E9D000              	jc	.i21_4e_err
  6839                                  	; Search for first matching entry
  6840 00002FA6 BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  6841 00002FA9 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  6842 00002FAD 31DB                    	xor	bx, bx			; Entry index
  6843                                  .i21_4e_search:
  6844 00002FAF 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  6845 00002FB1 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  6846 00002FB3 7503E9BE00              	je	.i21_4e_not_found
  6847 00002FB8 3CE5                    	cmp	al, 0xE5
  6848 00002FBA 7503E9AD00              	je	.i21_4e_next
  6849                                  	; Check attribute filter
  6850 00002FBF 8A440B                  	mov	al, [si+11]
  6851 00002FC2 A808                    	test	al, 0x08		; Skip volume labels
  6852 00002FC4 7403E9A300              	jnz	.i21_4e_next

  6860 00002FD9 2E8B3E[6E3E]            	mov	di, [cs:dta_off]
  6861                                  	; Reserved bytes 0-20: save search state
  6862 00002FDE 26881D                  	mov	[es:di+0], bl		; Current entry index (low)
  6863 00002FE1 26887D01                	mov	[es:di+1], bh		; Current entry index (high)
  6864                                  	; Copy wildcard pattern to DTA for FindNext

  6866 00002FE6 51                      	push	cx
  6867 00002FE7 BE[FC3C]                	mov	si, wild_pattern
  6868 00002FEA B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  6869 00002FED 57                      	push	di
  6870 00002FEE 83C702                  	add	di, 2
  6871                                  .i21_4e_cpwild:

  6873 00002FF3 268805                  	mov	[es:di], al
  6874 00002FF6 46                      	inc	si
  6875 00002FF7 47                      	inc	di
  6876 00002FF8 49                      	dec	cx
  6877 00002FF9 75F6                    	jnz	.i21_4e_cpwild

  6879 00002FFC 59                      	pop	cx
  6880 00002FFD 5E                      	pop	si
  6881                                  	; Attribute at offset 21
  6882 00002FFE 8A440B                  	mov	al, [si+11]
  6883 00003001 26884515                	mov	[es:di+21], al
  6884                                  	; Time at offset 22

  6886 00003008 26894516                	mov	[es:di+22], ax
  6887                                  	; Date at offset 24
  6888 0000300C 8B4418                  	mov	ax, [si+24]
  6889 0000300F 26894518                	mov	[es:di+24], ax
  6890                                  	; Size at offset 26 (4 bytes)
  6891 00003013 8B441C                  	mov	ax, [si+28]
  6892 00003016 2689451A                	mov	[es:di+26], ax
  6893 0000301A 8B441E                  	mov	ax, [si+30]
  6894 0000301D 2689451C                	mov	[es:di+28], ax
  6895                                  	; Filename at offset 30 (13 bytes ASCIIZ)
  6896 00003021 57                      	push	di
  6897 00003022 83C71E                  	add	di, 30
  6898                                  	; Convert 8.3 to ASCIIZ
  6899 00003025 56                      	push	si
  6900 00003026 B90800                  	mov	cx, 8
  6901                                  .i21_4e_fname:

  6903 0000302B 3C20                    	cmp	al, ' '
  6904 0000302D 7408                    	je	.i21_4e_fname_done

  6906 00003032 46                      	inc	si
  6907 00003033 47                      	inc	di
  6908 00003034 49                      	dec	cx
  6909 00003035 75F2                    	jnz	.i21_4e_fname

  6913 00003039 83C608                  	add	si, 8			; Extension

  6927 00003055 75F2                    	jnz	.i21_4e_ext

  6931 0000305C 5F                      	pop	di
  6932                                  	; Success

  6934 0000305E 07                      	pop	es
  6935 0000305F 5F                      	pop	di

  6943 0000306B CF                      	iret

  6945                                  .i21_4e_next:

  6947 0000306F 43                      	inc	bx
  6948 00003070 49                      	dec	cx

  6964                                  
  6965 00003088 0000                    .i21_4e_attr:	dw	0
  6966                                  
  6967                                  ; --- AH=4F: FindNext ---
  6968                                  ; Uses DTA from previous FindFirst
  6969                                  ; Returns: CF=0 and DTA updated, CF=1 AX=18 if no more
  6970                                  .i21_4f:

  6972 0000308B 51                      	push	cx

  6974 0000308D 57                      	push	di

  6976 0000308F 1E                      	push	ds
  6977 00003090 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  6978 00003093 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  6979                                  	; Read search state from DTA
  6980 00003095 8E06[6C3E]              	mov	es, [dta_seg]
  6981 00003099 8B3E[6E3E]              	mov	di, [dta_off]
  6982 0000309D 268A1D                  	mov	bl, [es:di+0]
  6983 000030A0 268A7D01                	mov	bh, [es:di+1]
  6984 000030A4 43                      	inc	bx			; Start from next entry
  6985                                  	; Restore wildcard pattern from DTA

  6987 000030A6 83C702                  	add	di, 2
  6988 000030A9 BE[FC3C]                	mov	si, wild_pattern
  6989 000030AC B90B00                  	mov	cx, 11
  6990                                  .i21_4f_restore:

  6992 000030B2 8804                    	mov	[si], al
  6993 000030B4 46                      	inc	si

  6996 000030B7 75F6                    	jnz	.i21_4f_restore
  6997 000030B9 5F                      	pop	di
  6998                                  	; Re-read directory (save BX — read_resolved_dir clobbers it)
  6999 000030BA 53                      	push	bx
  7000 000030BB A0[083E]                	mov	al, [cur_drive]
  7001 000030BE A2[0D3E]                	mov	[resolved_drive], al
  7002 000030C1 A1[C23D]                	mov	ax, [cur_dir_cluster]
  7003 000030C4 A3[093E]                	mov	[resolved_dir_cluster], ax

  7007 000030D0 5B                      	pop	bx
  7008 000030D1 7303E9CC00              	jc	.i21_4f_err

  7010 000030D6 8E06[6C3E]              	mov	es, [dta_seg]
  7011 000030DA 8B3E[6E3E]              	mov	di, [dta_off]
  7012                                  	; Skip to entry BX
  7013 000030DE BE0040                  	mov	si, dir_buffer
  7014 000030E1 8B0E[0B3E]              	mov	cx, [resolved_dir_entries]
  7015                                  	; Skip BX entries
  7016 000030E5 89D8                    	mov	ax, bx
  7017 000030E7 39C8                    	cmp	ax, cx
  7018 000030E9 7203E9B400              	jae	.i21_4f_err		; Past end
  7019 000030EE 53                      	push	bx
  7020 000030EF BB2000                  	mov	bx, 32
  7021 000030F2 F7E3                    	mul	bx
  7022 000030F4 5B                      	pop	bx

  7024 000030F7 29D9                    	sub	cx, bx			; Remaining entries
  7025 000030F9 09C9                    	or	cx, cx
  7026 000030FB 7503E9A200              	jz	.i21_4f_err
  7027                                  	; Search from here
  7028                                  .i21_4f_search:
  7029 00003100 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  7030 00003102 3C00                    	cmp	al, 0
  7031 00003104 7503E99900              	je	.i21_4f_err
  7032 00003109 3CE5                    	cmp	al, 0xE5
  7033 0000310B 7503E98800              	je	.i21_4f_next
  7034 00003110 F6440B08                	test	byte [si+11], 0x08
  7035 00003114 7403E97F00              	jnz	.i21_4f_next

  7037 0000311A BF[FC3C]                	mov	di, wild_pattern
  7038 0000311D E8A0E8                  	call	match_wildcard

  7040 00003121 7275                    	jc	.i21_4f_next

  7043 00003126 26887D01                	mov	[es:di+1], bh
  7044 0000312A 8A440B                  	mov	al, [si+11]
  7045 0000312D 26884515                	mov	[es:di+21], al
  7046 00003131 8B4416                  	mov	ax, [si+22]
  7047 00003134 26894516                	mov	[es:di+22], ax
  7048 00003138 8B4418                  	mov	ax, [si+24]
  7049 0000313B 26894518                	mov	[es:di+24], ax
  7050 0000313F 8B441C                  	mov	ax, [si+28]
  7051 00003142 2689451A                	mov	[es:di+26], ax
  7052 00003146 8B441E                  	mov	ax, [si+30]
  7053 00003149 2689451C                	mov	[es:di+28], ax
  7054                                  	; Convert filename

  7056 0000314E 83C71E                  	add	di, 30
  7057 00003151 56                      	push	si
  7058 00003152 B90800                  	mov	cx, 8
  7059                                  .i21_4f_fname:
  7060 00003155 8A04                    	mov	al, [si]
  7061 00003157 3C20                    	cmp	al, ' '
  7062 00003159 7408                    	je	.i21_4f_fname_done
  7063 0000315B 268805                  	mov	[es:di], al
  7064 0000315E 46                      	inc	si
  7065 0000315F 47                      	inc	di
  7066 00003160 49                      	dec	cx
  7067 00003161 75F2                    	jnz	.i21_4f_fname
  7068                                  .i21_4f_fname_done:

  7100 00003196 5D                      	pop	bp

  7102                                  
  7103                                  .i21_4f_next:

  7105 0000319B 43                      	inc	bx

  7107 0000319D 7403E95EFF              	jnz	.i21_4f_search
  7108                                  .i21_4f_err:

  7113 000031A6 59                      	pop	cx

  7118 000031AE 834E0601                	or	word [bp+6], 0x0001

  7120 000031B3 CF                      	iret
  7121                                  
  7122                                  ; --- AH=56: Rename file ---
  7123                                  ; Input: DS:DX = old name, ES:DI = new name
  7124                                  ; Returns: CF=0 success, CF=1 AX=error
  7125                                  .i21_56:
  7126 000031B4 53                      	push	bx
  7127 000031B5 51                      	push	cx
  7128 000031B6 56                      	push	si
  7129 000031B7 57                      	push	di
  7130 000031B8 06                      	push	es
  7131 000031B9 1E                      	push	ds
  7132                                  	; Save new name pointer (ES:DI from caller)
  7133 000031BA 2E893E[A032]            	mov	[cs:.i21_56_new_off], di
  7134 000031BF 2E8C06[A232]            	mov	[cs:.i21_56_new_seg], es
  7135                                  	; Copy old filename from caller's DS:DX

  7137 000031C6 1E                      	push	ds
  7138 000031C7 B80008                  	mov	ax, SHELL_SEG
  7139 000031CA 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
  7140 000031CC BF[9F3C]                	mov	di, cmd_buffer
  7141 000031CF 1F                      	pop	ds
  7142 000031D0 57                      	push	di
  7143 000031D1 B94E00                  	mov	cx, 78
  7144                                  .i21_56_copy_old:
  7145 000031D4 AC                      	lodsb
  7146 000031D5 1E                      	push	ds
  7147 000031D6 BB0008                  	mov	bx, SHELL_SEG
  7148 000031D9 8EDB                    	mov	ds, bx
  7149 000031DB 8805                    	mov	[di], al
  7150 000031DD 1F                      	pop	ds
  7151 000031DE 08C0                    	or	al, al
  7152 000031E0 7404                    	jz	.i21_56_old_done
  7153 000031E2 47                      	inc	di
  7154 000031E3 49                      	dec	cx
  7155 000031E4 75EE                    	jnz	.i21_56_copy_old
  7156                                  .i21_56_old_done:

  7160 000031EC E855E2                  	call	resolve_path
  7161 000031EF 7303E99A00              	jc	.i21_56_err
  7162                                  	; Save old 8.3 name
  7163 000031F4 BE[F03C]                	mov	si, exec_fname

  7166 000031FD F3A4                    	rep	movsb
  7167                                  	; Parse new name

  7170                                  	; Copy new name to cmd_buffer

  7173 0000320B 8ED8                    	mov	ds, ax
